Safe learning-based control via function-based uncertainty quantification
Authors: Abdullah Tokmak, Toni Karvonen, Thomas B. Schön, Dominik Baumann
First: 2026-04-01T17:23:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T17:23:30+00:00
Comments: Under review for CDC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Uncertainty quantification is essential when deploying learning-based control methods in safety-critical systems. This is commonly realized by constructing uncertainty tubes that enclose the unknown function of interest, e.g., the reward and constraint functions or the underlying dynamics model, with high probability. However, existing approaches for uncertainty quantification typically rely on restrictive assumptions on the unknown function, such as known bounds on functional norms or Lipschitz constants, and struggle with discontinuities. In this paper, we model the unknown function as a random function from which independent and identically distributed realizations can be generated, and construct uncertainty tubes via the scenario approach that hold with high probability and rely solely on the sampled realizations. We integrate these uncertainty tubes into a safe Bayesian optimization algorithm, which we then use to safely tune control parameters on a real Furuta pendulum.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于函数不确定性量化的安全学习控制
在安全关键系统中部署基于学习的控制方法时，不确定性量化至关重要。通常通过构建高概率覆盖目标未知函数（如奖励函数、约束函数或底层动力学模型）的不确定性管来实现。然而，现有不确定性量化方法通常依赖于对未知函数的严格假设，例如函数范数或Lipschitz常数的已知界限，且难以处理不连续性。本文中，我们将未知函数建模为可生成独立同分布实现样本的随机函数，并基于场景方法构建仅依赖采样实现的高概率不确定性管。我们将这些不确定性管集成至安全贝叶斯优化算法中，并应用于真实Furuta摆的控制参数安全调优。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for reliable uncertainty quantification in safety-critical learning-based control systems, this paper proposes a method that models unknown functions as random processes from which independent realizations can be sampled, constructing high-probability uncertainty tubes via the scenario approach without relying on restrictive assumptions like Lipschitz continuity. The approach is integrated into a safe Bayesian optimization framework, and experimental results demonstrate its successful application in safely tuning control parameters on a real Furuta pendulum.
本文针对安全关键学习控制系统中不确定性量化的需求，提出了一种方法，将未知函数建模为可从中采样独立实现的随机过程，通过场景方法构建高概率不确定性区间，无需依赖利普希茨连续性等限制性假设。该方法被集成到安全贝叶斯优化框架中，实验结果表明，其在真实Furuta摆上安全调整控制参数的应用取得了成功。
Deep Reinforcement Learning for Robotic Manipulation under Distribution Shift with Bounded Extremum Seeking
Authors: Shaifalee Saxena, Rafael Fierro, Alexander Scheinker
First: 2026-04-01T16:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T16:59:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has shown strong performance in robotic manipulation, but learned policies often degrade in performance when test conditions differ from the training distribution. This limitation is especially important in contact-rich tasks such as pushing and pick-and-place, where changes in goals, contact conditions, or robot dynamics can drive the system out-of-distribution at inference time. In this paper, we investigate a hybrid controller that combines reinforcement learning with bounded extremum seeking to improve robustness under such conditions. In the proposed approach, deep deterministic policy gradient (DDPG) policies are trained under standard conditions on the robotic pushing and pick-and-place tasks, and are then combined with bounded ES during deployment. The RL policy provides fast manipulation behavior, while bounded ES ensures robustness of the overall controller to time variations when operating conditions depart from those seen during training. The resulting controller is evaluated under several out-of-distribution settings, including time-varying goals and spatially varying friction patches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于有界极值搜索的分布偏移下机器人操作深度强化学习
强化学习在机器人操作任务中表现出色，但训练策略在测试条件与训练分布不同时性能常会下降。这一局限在接触密集型任务（如推物和抓放）中尤为突出，目标、接触条件或机器人动力学的变化均可能在推理时使系统偏离分布。本文研究一种混合控制器，将强化学习与有界极值搜索结合，以提升此类条件下的鲁棒性。所提方法中，深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）策略在标准条件下针对机器人推物和抓放任务进行训练，并在部署时与有界极值搜索结合。强化学习策略提供快速操作行为，而有界极值搜索确保整体控制器在运行条件偏离训练条件时对时变干扰的鲁棒性。该控制器在多种分布偏移场景下进行评估，包括时变目标和空间变化的摩擦区域。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the performance degradation of reinforcement learning policies in robotic manipulation when test conditions differ from the training distribution, particularly in contact-rich tasks like pushing and pick-and-place. To improve robustness under such distribution shifts, the authors propose a hybrid controller that combines a deep deterministic policy gradient (DDPG) policy, trained under standard conditions, with bounded extremum seeking during deployment. Experimental results show that this approach maintains robust performance in out-of-distribution settings, including scenarios with time-varying goals and spatially varying friction patches, by leveraging the RL policy for fast manipulation and bounded ES for adaptation to time-varying conditions.
本文针对强化学习策略在机器人操作中，当测试条件与训练分布不同时性能下降的问题，特别是在推和抓放等接触丰富的任务中。为提高在此类分布偏移下的鲁棒性，作者提出了一种混合控制器，将在标准条件下训练的深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）策略与有界极值搜索在部署时结合。实验结果表明，该方法在包括时变目标和空间变化摩擦块在内的分布外设置中保持了鲁棒性能，通过利用RL策略实现快速操作，并借助有界极值搜索适应时变条件。
Approximating Pareto Frontiers in Stochastic Multi-Objective Optimization via Hashing and Randomization
Authors: Jinzhao Li, Nan Jiang, Yexiang Xue
First: 2026-04-01T16:24:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T16:24:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Stochastic Multi-Objective Optimization (SMOO) is critical for decision-making trading off multiple potentially conflicting objectives in uncertain environments. SMOO aims at identifying the Pareto frontier, which contains all mutually non-dominating decisions. The problem is highly intractable due to the embedded probabilistic inference, such as computing the marginal, posterior probabilities, or expectations. Existing methods, such as scalarization, sample average approximation, and evolutionary algorithms, either offer arbitrarily loose approximations or may incur prohibitive computational costs. We propose XOR-SMOO, a novel algorithm that with probability $1-δ$, obtains $γ$-approximate Pareto frontiers ($γ>1$) for SMOO by querying an SAT oracle poly-log times in $γ$ and $δ$. A $γ$-approximate Pareto frontier is only below the true frontier by a fixed, multiplicative factor $γ$. Thus, XOR-SMOO solves highly intractable SMOO problems (\#P-hard) with only queries to SAT oracles while obtaining tight, constant factor approximation guarantees. Experiments on real-world road network strengthening and supply chain design problems demonstrate that XOR-SMOO outperforms several baselines in identifying Pareto frontiers that have higher objective values, better coverage of the optimal solutions, and the solutions found are more evenly distributed. Overall, XOR-SMOO significantly enhanced the practicality and reliability of SMOO solvers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于哈希与随机化的随机多目标优化帕累托前沿逼近方法
随机多目标优化（SMOO）在不确定环境下权衡多个潜在冲突目标时至关重要，其核心在于识别包含所有互不支配决策的帕累托前沿。由于涉及概率推断（如计算边缘概率、后验概率或期望），该问题具有高度难解性。现有方法（如标量化、样本平均逼近和进化算法）要么提供任意宽松的近似解，要么计算成本过高。本文提出XOR-SMOO算法，以概率$1-δ$通过查询SAT预言机$γ$和$δ$的多对数次数，获得$γ$近似帕累托前沿（$γ>1$）。$γ$近似前沿仅以固定乘积因子$γ$低于真实前沿，因此XOR-SMOO仅需查询SAT预言机即可解决高度难解的SMOO问题（#P难），并获得紧致的常数因子近似保证。在现实道路网络强化和供应链设计问题上的实验表明，XOR-SMOO在帕累托前沿识别方面优于多种基线方法：所得前沿具有更高目标值、更优解覆盖度，且解分布更均匀。总体而言，XOR-SMOO显著提升了SMOO求解器的实用性与可靠性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the intractability of Stochastic Multi-Objective Optimization (SMOO), which involves finding Pareto frontiers under uncertainty, a problem often #P-hard due to complex probabilistic inference. To overcome the limitations of existing methods like scalarization or evolutionary algorithms that may yield loose approximations or high computational costs, the authors propose XOR-SMOO, an algorithm that uses hashing and randomization to query an SAT oracle poly-logarithmically in parameters γ and δ, guaranteeing with high probability a γ-approximate Pareto frontier where solutions are within a multiplicative factor γ of the true frontier. Experimental results on real-world applications, such as road network strengthening and supply chain design, show that XOR-SMOO outperforms baselines by producing Pareto frontiers with higher objective values, better coverage of optimal solutions, and more evenly distributed solutions, thereby enhancing the practicality and reliability of SMOO solvers.
本文针对随机多目标优化（SMOO）中因概率推理（如计算边缘或后验概率）导致问题高度难解（#P难）的挑战，旨在近似帕累托前沿以支持不确定性下的决策权衡。现有方法如标量化或进化算法可能产生松散近似或计算成本过高，为此作者提出XOR-SMOO算法，通过哈希和随机化技术，以多项式对数次查询SAT预言机，以高概率获得γ近似帕累托前沿，确保解在真前沿的固定乘数γ范围内。在真实世界道路网络强化和供应链设计问题上的实验表明，XOR-SMOO优于多种基线方法，其帕累托前沿具有更高的目标值、更优的覆盖范围以及更均匀的解分布，从而显著提升了SMOO求解器的实用性和可靠性。
Adversarial Attacks in AI-Driven RAN Slicing: SLA Violations and Recovery
Authors: Deemah H. Tashman, Soumaya Cherkaoui
First: 2026-04-01T15:54:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T15:54:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Next-generation (NextG) cellular networks are designed to support emerging applications with diverse data rate and latency requirements, such as immersive multimedia services and large-scale Internet of Things deployments. A key enabling mechanism is radio access network (RAN) slicing, which dynamically partitions radio resources into virtual resource blocks to efficiently serve heterogeneous traffic classes, including enhanced mobile broadband (eMBB), massive machine-type communications (mMTC), and ultra-reliable low-latency communications (URLLC). In this paper, we study the impact of adversarial attacks on AI-driven RAN slicing decisions, where a budget-constrained adversary selectively jams slice transmissions to bias deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-based resource allocation, and quantify the resulting service level agreement (SLA) violations and post-attack recovery behavior. Our results indicate that budget-constrained adversarial jamming can induce severe and slice-dependent steady-state SLA violations. Moreover, the DRL agent's reward converges toward the clean baseline only after a non-negligible recovery period.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AI驱动的RAN切片中的对抗性攻击：SLA违规与恢复
下一代蜂窝网络旨在支持具有多样化数据速率和延迟需求的新兴应用，如沉浸式多媒体服务和大规模物联网部署。其关键使能机制是无线接入网络切片，该技术动态划分无线资源为虚拟资源块，以高效服务异构流量类别，包括增强移动宽带、大规模机器类通信和超可靠低延迟通信。本文研究了对抗性攻击对AI驱动的RAN切片决策的影响：预算受限的对手通过选择性干扰切片传输，使基于深度强化学习的资源分配产生偏差，并量化了由此导致的服务水平协议违规及攻击后恢复行为。结果表明，预算受限的对抗性干扰可引发严重且依赖切片类型的稳态SLA违规。此外，深度强化学习智能体的奖励仅在经历不可忽略的恢复期后，才能收敛至无攻击基线水平。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the vulnerability of AI-driven radio access network (RAN) slicing to adversarial attacks, motivated by the need to secure next-generation networks that support diverse services through dynamic resource allocation. The method involves a budget-constrained adversary that selectively jams slice transmissions to bias a deep reinforcement learning (DRL) agent responsible for resource allocation, with the impact quantified in terms of service level agreement (SLA) violations and recovery. Experimental results show that such jamming can cause severe, slice-dependent SLA violations in steady state, and the DRL agent requires a non-negligible recovery period before its reward converges back to the clean baseline performance.
本文研究了人工智能驱动的无线接入网络切片在对抗性攻击下的脆弱性，其动机在于保护通过动态资源分配支持多样化服务的下一代网络安全。方法上，一个预算受限的对手选择性地干扰切片传输，以影响负责资源分配的深度强化学习智能体，并量化由此导致的服务水平协议违规和恢复情况。实验结果表明，此类干扰可在稳态下造成严重的、依赖于切片类型的服务水平协议违规，且深度强化学习智能体需要经过不可忽略的恢复期，其奖励才能收敛回干净的基线性能。
Ego-Foresight: Self-supervised Learning of Agent-Aware Representations for Improved RL
Authors: Manuel Serra Nunes, Atabak Dehban, Yiannis Demiris, José Santos-Victor
First: 2024-05-27T13:32:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T15:51:54+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 8 figures, conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the significant advances in Deep Reinforcement Learning (RL) observed in the last decade, the amount of training experience necessary to learn effective policies remains one of the primary concerns in both simulated and real environments. Looking to solve this issue, previous work has shown that improved efficiency can be achieved by separately modeling the agent and environment, but usually requires a supervisory signal. In contrast to RL, humans can perfect a new skill from a small number of trials and often do so without a supervisory signal, making neuroscientific studies of human development a valuable source of inspiration for RL. In particular, we explore the idea of motor prediction, which states that humans develop an internal model of themselves and of the consequences that their motor commands have on the immediate sensory inputs. Our insight is that the movementofthe agent provides a cue that allows the duality between the agent and environment to be learned. To instantiate this idea, we present Ego-Foresight (EF), a self-supervised method for disentangling agent information based on motion and prediction. Our main finding is that, when used as an auxiliary task in feature learning, self-supervised agent awareness improves the sample-efficiency and performance of the underlying RL algorithm. To test our approach, we study the ability of EF to predict agent movement and disentangle agent information. Then, we integrate EF with model-free and model based RL algorithms to solve simulated control tasks, showing improved sample-efficiency and performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Ego-Foresight：基于自监督学习的智能体感知表征提升强化学习性能
尽管深度强化学习在过去十年取得显著进展，但在模拟和真实环境中，学习有效策略所需的训练经验量仍是核心挑战。为解决此问题，先前研究表明通过分别建模智能体与环境可提升效率，但通常需要监督信号。与强化学习不同，人类仅需少量尝试即可掌握新技能，且常无需监督信号，这使得人类发展的神经科学研究成为强化学习的重要灵感来源。我们特别探索运动预测理论——该理论认为人类会建立自身内部模型，并理解其运动指令对即时感官输入的影响。我们的核心观点是：智能体的运动轨迹提供了学习智能体与环境二元对偶性的线索。基于此，我们提出Ego-Foresight（EF）——一种基于运动预测的自监督解耦智能体信息方法。主要发现表明：将自监督的智能体感知作为特征学习的辅助任务，可提升基础强化学习算法的样本效率与性能。我们通过EF预测智能体运动及解耦智能体信息的能力验证方法有效性，并将EF与无模型及基于模型的强化学习算法结合解决模拟控制任务，实验证明其能显著提升样本效率与性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to improve the sample efficiency of deep reinforcement learning (RL) and inspired by neuroscientific studies of human motor prediction, this paper introduces Ego-Foresight (EF), a self-supervised method that learns agent-aware representations by predicting the agent's own motion. The method disentangles agent information from environmental observations without requiring a supervisory signal, using this learned representation as an auxiliary task during feature learning. Experimental results demonstrate that EF successfully predicts agent movement and disentangles agent information, and when integrated with model-free and model-based RL algorithms, it leads to improved sample efficiency and performance on simulated control tasks.
本文旨在提升深度强化学习的样本效率，其动机源于对人类运动预测神经科学研究的借鉴，提出了名为Ego-Foresight（EF）的自监督方法，该方法通过预测智能体自身运动来学习智能体感知表征。该方法无需监督信号，即可从环境观测中分离出智能体信息，并将此学习到的表征作为特征学习的辅助任务。实验结果表明，EF能有效预测智能体运动并分离智能体信息，当与无模型和基于模型的强化学习算法结合时，在模拟控制任务中提高了样本效率和性能。
Query-Conditioned Evidential Keyframe Sampling for MLLM-Based Long-Form Video Understanding
Authors: Yiheng Wang, Lichen Zhu, Yueqian Lin, Yudong Liu, Jingyang Zhang, Hai "Helen" Li, Yiran Chen
First: 2026-04-01T15:02:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T15:02:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown strong performance on video question answering, but their application to long-form videos is constrained by limited context length and computational cost, making keyframe sampling essential. Existing approaches typically rely on semantic relevance or reinforcement learning, which either fail to capture evidential clues or suffer from inefficient combinatorial optimization. In this work, we propose an evidence-driven keyframe sampling framework grounded in information bottleneck theory. We formulate keyframe selection as maximizing the conditional mutual information between selected frames and the query, providing a principled objective that reflects each frame's contribution to answering the question. To make this objective tractable, we exploit its structure to derive a decomposed optimization that reduces subset selection to independent frame-level scoring. We further introduce a query-conditioned evidence scoring network trained with a contrastive objective to estimate evidential importance efficiently. Experiments on long-form video understanding benchmarks show that our method consistently outperforms prior sampling strategies under strict token budgets, while significantly improving training efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多模态大语言模型长视频理解的查询条件化证据关键帧采样
多模态大语言模型在视频问答任务中表现出色，但其在长视频应用时受限于上下文长度与计算成本，使得关键帧采样至关重要。现有方法通常依赖语义相关性或强化学习，这些方法要么无法捕捉证据线索，要么受困于低效的组合优化。本研究提出一种基于信息瓶颈理论的证据驱动关键帧采样框架，将关键帧选择建模为最大化选定帧与查询间的条件互信息，从而构建一个能反映各帧对问题回答贡献度的理论目标。为使该目标可求解，我们利用其结构推导出分解优化方法，将子集选择简化为独立的帧级评分。进一步引入基于对比目标训练的查询条件化证据评分网络，以高效估计证据重要性。在长视频理解基准测试上的实验表明，该方法在严格令牌预算下持续优于先前的采样策略，同时显著提升了训练效率。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) in processing long-form videos, where constraints on context length and computational cost necessitate efficient keyframe sampling, as existing methods often miss evidential clues or are inefficient. The method proposes an evidence-driven keyframe sampling framework based on information bottleneck theory, formulating selection as maximizing conditional mutual information between frames and the query, which is decomposed into a tractable optimization using a query-conditioned evidence scoring network trained contrastively. Main experimental results on long-form video understanding benchmarks demonstrate that this approach consistently outperforms prior sampling strategies under strict token budgets while significantly improving training efficiency.
本研究的动机是解决多模态大语言模型在处理长视频时面临的上下文长度和计算成本限制，这需要高效的关键帧采样，而现有方法常忽略证据线索或效率低下。方法上，提出了一种基于信息瓶颈理论的证据驱动关键帧采样框架，将选择问题形式化为最大化选定帧与查询之间的条件互信息，并通过分解优化和对比训练的查询条件证据评分网络实现高效处理。主要实验结果表明，在严格令牌预算下，该方法在长视频理解基准上持续优于先前的采样策略，同时显著提升了训练效率。
Focal plane wavefront control with model-based reinforcement learning
Authors: Jalo Nousiainen, Iremsu Taskin, Markus Kasper, Gilles Orban De Xivry, Olivier Absil
First: 2026-04-01T14:55:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T14:55:15+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 11 figures accepted by A&A
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The direct imaging of potentially habitable exoplanets is one prime science case for high-contrast imaging instruments on extremely large telescopes. Most such exoplanets orbit close to their host stars, where their observation is limited by fast-moving atmospheric speckles and quasi-static non-common-path aberrations (NCPA). Conventional NCPA correction methods often use mechanical mirror probes, which compromise performance during operation. This work presents machine-learning-based NCPA control methods that automatically detect and correct both dynamic and static NCPA errors by leveraging sequential phase diversity. We extend previous work in reinforcement learning for AO to focal plane control. A new model-based RL algorithm, Policy Optimization for NCPAs (PO4NCPA), interprets the focal-plane image as input data and, through sequential phase diversity, determines phase corrections that optimize both non-coronagraphic and post-coronagraphic PSFs without prior system knowledge. Further, we demonstrate the effectiveness of this approach by numerically simulating static NCPA errors on a ground-based telescope and an infrared imager affected by water-vapor-induced seeing (dynamic NCPAs). Simulations show that PO4NCPA robustly compensates static and dynamic NCPAs. In static cases, it achieves near-optimal focal-plane light suppression with a coronagraph and near-optimal Strehl without one. With dynamics NCPA, it matches the performance of the modal least-squares reconstruction combined with a 1-step delay integrator in these metrics. The method remains effective for the ELT pupil, vector vortex coronagraph, and under photon and background noise. PO4NCPA is model-free and can be directly applied to standard imaging as well as to any coronagraph. Its sub-millisecond inference times and performance also make it suitable for real-time low-order correction of atmospheric turbulence beyond HCI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于模型强化学习的焦平面波前控制
对潜在宜居系外行星的直接成像，是超大型望远镜上高对比度成像仪器的一项核心科学任务。多数此类系外行星围绕其宿主恒星近距离运行，观测受限于快速移动的大气散斑和准静态非共路像差（NCPA）。传统NCPA校正方法常使用机械镜面探针，会在运行期间影响性能。本研究提出了基于机器学习的NCPA控制方法，通过利用序列相位多样性，自动检测并校正动态和静态NCPA误差。我们将先前自适应光学中的强化学习研究扩展至焦平面控制。一种新的基于模型的强化学习算法——NCPA策略优化（PO4NCPA），将焦平面图像作为输入数据，通过序列相位多样性确定相位校正，以优化非日冕仪和日冕仪后点扩散函数，且无需先验系统知识。此外，我们通过数值模拟地面望远镜受水汽视宁度影响（动态NCPA）的红外成像仪上的静态NCPA误差，验证了该方法的有效性。模拟显示，PO4NCPA能稳健补偿静态和动态NCPA。在静态情况下，使用日冕仪时能实现接近最优的焦平面光抑制，无日冕仪时则达到接近最优的斯特列尔比。对于动态NCPA，其在上述指标上匹配了模态最小二乘重建结合单步延迟积分器的性能。该方法对ELT孔径、矢量涡旋日冕仪以及在光子和背景噪声下仍保持有效。PO4NCPA无需模型，可直接应用于标准成像及任何日冕仪。其亚毫秒级推理时间和性能也使其适用于高对比度成像之外的大气湍流实时低阶校正。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the challenge of directly imaging habitable exoplanets, which is hindered by fast-moving atmospheric speckles and quasi-static non-common-path aberrations (NCPA) that degrade image contrast near stars. The method introduces a model-based reinforcement learning algorithm called PO4NCPA, which uses sequential phase diversity to interpret focal-plane images and determine phase corrections without prior system knowledge, enabling automatic detection and correction of both static and dynamic NCPAs. Experimental simulations on ground-based telescopes show that PO4NCPA robustly compensates for these errors, achieving near-optimal focal-plane light suppression with a coronagraph and near-optimal Strehl without one in static cases, while matching the performance of conventional modal least-squares reconstruction with a delay integrator for dynamic NCPAs, and it remains effective under various conditions including noise and different telescope setups.
本文旨在解决直接成像宜居系外行星的挑战，该过程受到快速移动的大气散斑和准静态非共路像差（NCPA）的阻碍，这些像差会降低恒星附近的图像对比度。方法提出了一种基于模型的强化学习算法PO4NCPA，它利用序列相位多样性分析焦平面图像并确定相位校正，无需先验系统知识，从而自动检测和校正静态与动态NCPA。在基于地面望远镜的数值模拟实验中，PO4NCPA能稳健地补偿这些像差：在静态情况下，使用日冕仪时实现接近最优的焦平面光抑制，不使用日冕仪时达到接近最优的斯特列尔比；对于动态NCPA，其性能与模态最小二乘重建结合延迟积分器的传统方法相当，并且在噪声、不同望远镜配置等条件下仍保持有效。
Flow-based Policy With Distributional Reinforcement Learning in Trajectory Optimization
Authors: Ruijie Hao, Longfei Zhang, Yang Dai, Yang Ma, Xingxing Liang, Guangquan Cheng
First: 2026-04-01T14:47:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T14:47:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has proven highly effective in addressing complex control and decision-making tasks. However, in most traditional RL algorithms, the policy is typically parameterized as a diagonal Gaussian distribution, which constrains the policy from capturing multimodal distributions, making it difficult to cover the full range of optimal solutions in multi-solution problems, and the return is reduced to a mean value, losing its multimodal nature and thus providing insufficient guidance for policy updates. In response to these problems, we propose a RL algorithm termed flow-based policy with distributional RL (FP-DRL). This algorithm models the policy using flow matching, which offers both computational efficiency and the capacity to fit complex distributions. Additionally, it employs a distributional RL approach to model and optimize the entire return distribution, thereby more effectively guiding multimodal policy updates and improving agent performance. Experimental trails on MuJoCo benchmarks demonstrate that the FP-DRL algorithm achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance in most MuJoCo control tasks while exhibiting superior representation capability of the flow policy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于流策略与分布强化学习的轨迹优化方法
强化学习（RL）在解决复杂控制与决策任务方面已展现出显著成效。然而，传统RL算法通常将策略参数化为对角高斯分布，这限制了策略捕捉多模态分布的能力，难以覆盖多解问题中的全部最优解，且回报被简化为均值，丧失了多模态特性，从而对策略更新的指导不足。针对这些问题，我们提出了一种称为基于流策略的分布强化学习（FP-DRL）算法。该算法通过流匹配对策略进行建模，兼具计算效率与拟合复杂分布的能力。同时，采用分布强化学习方法对完整回报分布进行建模与优化，从而更有效地指导多模态策略更新并提升智能体性能。在MuJoCo基准测试中的实验表明，FP-DRL算法在多数MuJoCo控制任务中实现了最先进的性能，并展现出流策略卓越的表征能力。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work arises from the limitations of traditional reinforcement learning algorithms, which typically use a diagonal Gaussian distribution to parameterize the policy, thereby failing to capture multimodal distributions and reducing returns to a mean value, which inadequately guides policy updates in multi-solution problems. To address this, the authors propose FP-DRL, a method that combines flow matching for policy modeling to efficiently fit complex distributions and distributional reinforcement learning to model the full return distribution, enabling more effective multimodal policy optimization. Experimental results on MuJoCo benchmarks show that FP-DRL achieves state-of-the-art performance in most control tasks and demonstrates superior representation capability of the flow-based policy.
本研究的动机源于传统强化学习算法的局限性，这些算法通常使用对角高斯分布参数化策略，无法捕捉多模态分布，并将回报简化为均值，从而在多解问题中对策略更新的指导不足。为解决这些问题，作者提出了FP-DRL方法，该方法结合流匹配进行策略建模以高效拟合复杂分布，并采用分布式强化学习对完整回报分布进行建模，从而更有效地指导多模态策略优化。在MuJoCo基准测试中的实验结果表明，FP-DRL在大多数控制任务中实现了最先进的性能，并展现出流策略的优越表示能力。
CHEEM: Continual Learning by Reuse, New, Adapt and Skip -- A Hierarchical Exploration-Exploitation Approach
Authors: Chinmay Savadikar, Michelle Dai, Tianfu Wu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2023-03-14T21:52:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T14:18:35+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
To effectively manage the complexities of real-world dynamic environments, continual learning must incrementally acquire, update, and accumulate knowledge from a stream of tasks of different nature without suffering from catastrophic forgetting of prior knowledge. While this capability is innate to human cognition, it remains a significant challenge for modern deep learning systems. At the heart of this challenge lies the stability-plasticity dilemma: the need to balance leveraging prior knowledge, integrating novel information, and allocating model capacity adaptively based on task complexity and synergy. In this paper, we propose a novel exemplar-free class-incremental continual learning (ExfCCL) framework that addresses these issues through a Hierarchical Exploration-Exploitation (HEE) approach. The core of our method is a HEE-guided efficient neural architecture search (HEE-NAS) that enables a learning-to-adapt backbone via four primitive operations - reuse, new, adapt, and skip - thereby serving as an internal memory that dynamically updates selected components across streaming tasks. To address the task ID inference problem in ExfCCL, we exploit an external memory of task centroids proposed in the prior art. We term our method CHEEM (Continual Hierarchical-Exploration-Exploitation Memory). CHEEM is evaluated on the challenging MTIL and VDD benchmarks using both Tiny and Base Vision Transformers and a proposed holistic Figure-of-Merit (FoM) metric. It significantly outperforms state-of-the-art prompting-based continual learning methods, closely approaching full fine-tuning upper bounds. Furthermore, it learns adaptive model structures tailored to individual tasks in a semantically meaningful way. Our code is available at https://github.com/savadikarc/cheem .
中文标题/摘要
标题：CHEEM：通过复用、新建、适应与跳过实现持续学习——一种分层探索-利用方法
为有效应对现实动态环境的复杂性，持续学习需从不同性质的任务流中逐步获取、更新并积累知识，同时避免对先前知识的灾难性遗忘。尽管人类认知天生具备此能力，但对现代深度学习系统仍是重大挑战。其核心在于稳定性-可塑性困境：需平衡利用先验知识、整合新信息，以及根据任务复杂度与协同性自适应分配模型容量。本文提出一种新型无示例类增量持续学习框架，通过分层探索-利用方法解决上述问题。方法核心为HEE引导的高效神经架构搜索，通过复用、新建、适应与跳过四种基本操作实现自适应主干网络，作为内部记忆动态更新跨任务流组件。针对任务ID推断问题，我们采用现有技术中的任务质心外部记忆。该方法命名为CHEEM。在MTIL与VDD基准测试中，使用Tiny/Base Vision Transformer及提出的综合性能指标进行评估，CHEEM显著优于当前基于提示的持续学习方法，接近全微调理论上限，且能以语义有意义的方式学习适应各任务的模型结构。代码已开源：https://github.com/savadikarc/cheem。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of continual learning in dynamic environments, where models must incrementally acquire knowledge from a stream of tasks without catastrophic forgetting, balancing the stability-plasticity dilemma. The authors propose CHEEM, an exemplar-free class-incremental continual learning framework that employs a Hierarchical Exploration-Exploitation approach to guide neural architecture search, enabling a learning-to-adapt backbone through four primitive operations: reuse, new, adapt, and skip, which dynamically update model components across tasks. Experimental results on MTIL and VDD benchmarks using Vision Transformers show that CHEEM significantly outperforms state-of-the-art prompting-based methods, closely approaching full fine-tuning upper bounds, while learning adaptive, semantically meaningful model structures tailored to individual tasks.
本文针对动态环境中的持续学习挑战，旨在使模型能够从任务流中增量获取知识而不发生灾难性遗忘，平衡稳定性与可塑性之间的困境。作者提出CHEEM框架，一种无需示例的类增量持续学习方法，采用分层探索-利用策略来指导神经架构搜索，通过重用、新建、适应和跳过四种基本操作，实现学习自适应主干网络，动态更新跨任务的模型组件。在MTIL和VDD基准测试中使用视觉变换器的实验结果表明，CHEEM显著优于基于提示的先进持续学习方法，接近全微调的上限，同时学习到适应个体任务、具有语义意义的自适应模型结构。
Policy Improvement Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Huaiyang Wang, Xiaojie Li, Deqing Wang, Haoyi Zhou, Zixuan Huang, Yaodong Yang, Jianxin Li, Yikun Ban
First: 2026-04-01T13:10:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T13:10:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become a central post-training paradigm for improving the reasoning capabilities of large language models. Yet existing methods share a common blind spot: they optimize policies based on instantaneous group-level or batch-level statistics without ever verifying whether the resulting update actually improved the model. This open-loop design -- updating in isolation at each step, guided only by within-group (batch) reward signals -- means optimization can drift or collapse with no mechanism to detect and correct these failures. We argue that the missing ingredient is policy improvement feedback: the ability to measure and optimize inter-iteration progress directly. To this end, we introduce Policy Improvement Reinforcement Learning (PIRL), a framework that replaces surrogate reward maximization with the explicit objective of maximizing cumulative policy improvement across iterations, and prove this temporal objective is perfectly aligned with maximizing final task performance. Building on PIRL, we propose Policy Improvement Policy Optimization (PIPO), which implements closed-loop optimization through retrospective verification. At each iteration, PIPO evaluates whether the previous update yielded genuine improvement against a sliding-window historical baseline, then actively reinforces beneficial updates and suppresses the harmful ones -- transforming an open-loop process into a self-correcting one. We provide theoretical analysis showing that PIPO performs ascent on the PIRL objective in expectation, and experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate improved stability and performance over GRPO and its variants.
中文标题/摘要
标题：策略改进强化学习
可验证奖励的强化学习已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的核心后训练范式。然而现有方法存在一个共同的盲点：它们基于瞬时组级或批次级统计优化策略，却从未验证更新是否真正改进了模型。这种开环设计——仅依赖组内奖励信号在每一步独立更新——意味着优化可能漂移或崩溃，且无法检测和修正这些故障。我们认为缺失的关键是策略改进反馈：直接测量和优化迭代间进度的能力。为此，我们提出策略改进强化学习框架，用最大化跨迭代累积策略改进的显式目标替代代理奖励最大化，并证明该时序目标与最大化最终任务性能完全一致。基于此框架，我们进一步提出策略改进策略优化方法，通过回顾性验证实现闭环优化：每次迭代时，该方法基于滑动窗口历史基线评估前次更新是否带来真实改进，进而主动强化有益更新并抑制有害更新，从而将开环过程转化为自校正过程。理论分析表明该方法在期望上沿策略改进强化学习目标实现上升，数学推理基准实验也验证了其相比GRPO及其变体具有更好的稳定性与性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing reinforcement learning methods for language models, which optimize policies based on batch-level statistics without verifying actual improvement, this paper introduces Policy Improvement Reinforcement Learning (PIRL) to explicitly maximize cumulative policy improvement across iterations. The method, implemented as Policy Improvement Policy Optimization (PIPO), employs closed-loop optimization through retrospective verification, where each update is assessed against a historical baseline to reinforce beneficial changes and suppress harmful ones. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PIPO achieves improved stability and performance over baseline methods like GRPO, with theoretical analysis confirming its alignment with maximizing final task performance.
针对现有强化学习方法在优化语言模型策略时仅依赖批量统计而未验证实际改进的局限，本文提出了策略改进强化学习（PIRL），旨在显式最大化跨迭代的累积策略改进。该方法通过策略改进策略优化（PIPO）实现，采用基于回顾验证的闭环优化，即根据历史基线评估每次更新，以增强有益更改并抑制有害更改。在数学推理基准测试中的实验结果表明，PIPO相比GRPO等基线方法实现了更高的稳定性和性能，理论分析也证实了其与最终任务性能最大化目标的一致性。
DreamerAD: Efficient Reinforcement Learning via Latent World Model for Autonomous Driving
Authors: Pengxuan Yang, Yupeng Zheng, Deheng Qian, Zebin Xing, Qichao Zhang, Linbo Wang, Yichen Zhang, Shaoyu Guo, Zhongpu Xia, Qiang Chen, Junyu Han, Lingyun Xu, Yifeng Pan, Dongbin Zhao
First: 2026-03-25T17:57:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T13:02:07+00:00
Comments: authors update
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce DreamerAD, the first latent world model framework that enables efficient reinforcement learning for autonomous driving by compressing diffusion sampling from 100 steps to 1 - achieving 80x speedup while maintaining visual interpretability. Training RL policies on real-world driving data incurs prohibitive costs and safety risks. While existing pixel-level diffusion world models enable safe imagination-based training, they suffer from multi-step diffusion inference latency (2s/frame) that prevents high-frequency RL interaction. Our approach leverages denoised latent features from video generation models through three key mechanisms: (1) shortcut forcing that reduces sampling complexity via recursive multi-resolution step compression, (2) an autoregressive dense reward model operating directly on latent representations for fine-grained credit assignment, and (3) Gaussian vocabulary sampling for GRPO that constrains exploration to physically plausible trajectories. DreamerAD achieves 87.7 EPDMS on NavSim v2, establishing state-of-the-art performance and demonstrating that latent-space RL is effective for autonomous driving.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DreamerAD：基于潜在世界模型的高效自动驾驶强化学习框架
我们提出了首个潜在世界模型框架DreamerAD，通过将扩散采样从100步压缩至1步，在保持视觉可解释性的同时实现80倍加速，从而为自动驾驶实现高效强化学习。基于真实驾驶数据训练RL策略存在高昂成本与安全风险。现有像素级扩散世界模型虽支持基于想象的安全训练，但其多步扩散推理延迟（2秒/帧）阻碍了高频RL交互。我们的方法通过三项关键机制利用视频生成模型的去噪潜在特征：（1）通过递归多分辨率步长压缩降低采样复杂度的捷径强制机制；（2）直接在潜在表征上运行的自回归密集奖励模型，实现细粒度信用分配；（3）为GRPO设计的高斯词汇采样，将探索约束在物理可行的轨迹空间。DreamerAD在NavSim v2上取得87.7 EPDMS，达到最先进性能，证明潜在空间强化学习对自动驾驶具有实效性。

The method employs a latent world model that compresses diffusion sampling from 100 steps to just 1, achieving an 80x speedup, through techniques like shortcut forcing for step compression, an autoregressive dense reward model in latent space, and Gaussian vocabulary sampling to constrain exploration to plausible trajectories. Experimental results show that DreamerAD attains state-of-the-art performance with 87.7 EPDMS on the NavSim v2 benchmark, demonstrating the effectiveness of efficient latent-space RL for autonomous driving.
本文提出了DreamerAD框架，其动机在于解决在真实世界自动驾驶数据上直接训练强化学习策略所面临的高成本和安全风险问题。该方法采用潜在世界模型，通过快捷强制压缩、潜在空间自回归密集奖励模型以及高斯词汇采样等技术，将扩散采样步骤从100步压缩至1步，实现了80倍的速度提升。实验结果表明，DreamerAD在NavSim v2基准测试中取得了87.7 EPDMS的最先进性能，证明了潜在空间强化学习在自动驾驶中的高效性和有效性。
Incoherence in Goal-Conditioned Autoregressive Models
Authors: Jacek Karwowski, Raymond Douglas
First: 2025-10-08T00:52:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T11:58:51+00:00
Comments: To appear in the Proceedings of the 29th International Conference on Artificial Intelligence and Statistics (AISTATS) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We investigate mathematically the notion of incoherence: a structural issue with reinforcement learning policies derived by naive goal-conditioning of autoregressive models. We focus on the process of re-training models on their own actions, that is, fine-tuning offline-learned policies with online RL. We prove that it decreases incoherence and leads to an improvement in return, and we aim to characterize the resulting trajectory of policies. By re-framing standard notions of control-as-inference and soft Q learning, we establish a three-way correspondence with two other ways of understanding the iterative re-training process: as folding the posterior into the reward and, in the deterministic case, as decreasing the temperature parameter; the correspondence has computational content via the training-inference trade-off. Through soft-conditioning generative models, we discuss the link between incoherence and the effective horizon.
中文标题/摘要
标题：目标条件自回归模型中的非一致性研究
本文从数学角度探讨了非一致性的概念：这是一种源于对自回归模型进行朴素目标条件化所导出的强化学习策略的结构性问题。我们重点关注模型基于自身动作进行再训练的过程，即通过在线强化学习对离线学习策略进行微调。我们证明了该过程能够降低非一致性并提升回报，旨在刻画由此产生的策略轨迹。通过重构控制即推断与软Q学习的标准概念，我们建立了与理解迭代再训练过程的另外两种方式的三重对应关系：一种是将后验融入奖励函数，另一种在确定性场景下等同于降低温度参数；这种对应关系通过训练-推断权衡体现了计算内涵。借助软条件生成模型，我们进一步讨论了非一致性与有效视野之间的联系。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the structural issue of incoherence in reinforcement learning policies derived from naively goal-conditioned autoregressive models, particularly when fine-tuning offline-learned policies with online RL. The authors mathematically prove that iterative re-training of such models on their own actions reduces incoherence and improves policy return, and they characterize the resulting policy trajectory by reframing control-as-inference and soft Q learning. This establishes a three-way correspondence with alternative interpretations—folding the posterior into the reward and, in deterministic cases, decreasing the temperature—linked computationally via a training-inference trade-off, while also connecting incoherence to the effective horizon through soft-conditioned generative models.
本文研究了在朴素目标条件自回归模型衍生的强化学习策略中存在的结构性问题——不连贯性，特别是在使用在线强化学习对离线学习策略进行微调时。作者通过数学证明，在自身动作上迭代重训练此类模型可以减少不连贯性并提升策略回报，同时通过重构控制即推断和软Q学习来刻画由此产生的策略轨迹。这建立了一个三方面的对应关系，包括将后验折叠到奖励中以及在确定性情况下降低温度参数，并通过训练-推断权衡在计算上联系起来，同时借助软条件生成模型探讨了不连贯性与有效视野之间的联系。
RefineRL: Advancing Competitive Programming with Self-Refinement Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shaopeng Fu, Xingxing Zhang, Li Dong, Di Wang, Furu Wei
First: 2026-04-01T11:54:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T11:54:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance on complex reasoning tasks such as competitive programming (CP), existing methods predominantly focus on single-attempt settings, overlooking their capacity for iterative refinement. In this paper, we present RefineRL, a novel approach designed to unleash the self-refinement capabilities of LLMs for CP problem solving. RefineRL introduces two key innovations: (1) Skeptical-Agent, an iterative self-refinement agent equipped with local execution tools to validate generated solutions against public test cases of CP problems. This agent always maintains a skeptical attitude towards its own outputs and thereby enforces rigorous self-refinement even when validation suggests correctness. (2) A reinforcement learning (RL) solution to incentivize LLMs to self-refine with only standard RLVR data (i.e., problems paired with their verifiable answers). Extensive experiments on Qwen3-4B and Qwen3-4B-2507 demonstrate that our method yields substantial gains: after our RL training, these compact 4B models integrated with the Skeptical-Agent not only outperform much larger 32B models but also approach the single-attempt performance of 235B models. These findings suggest that self-refinement holds considerable promise for scaling LLM reasoning, with significant potential for further advancement.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RefineRL：通过自优化强化学习推进竞技编程
尽管大语言模型（LLMs）在竞技编程（CP）等复杂推理任务中展现出强大性能，现有方法主要聚焦于单次尝试场景，忽视了其迭代优化的潜力。本文提出RefineRL，一种旨在释放LLMs在CP问题求解中自优化能力的新方法。RefineRL包含两项核心创新：（1）Skeptical-Agent：配备本地执行工具的迭代自优化智能体，可通过CP问题的公开测试用例验证生成方案。该智能体始终对自身输出保持审慎态度，即使在验证通过时仍强制执行严格的自优化。（2）采用强化学习（RL）方案激励LLMs进行自优化，仅需标准RLVR数据（即问题与可验证答案配对）。在Qwen3-4B和Qwen3-4B-2507上的大量实验表明，经过RL训练后，集成Skeptical-Agent的紧凑4B模型不仅超越规模更大的32B模型，且逼近235B模型的单次尝试性能。这些发现证明自优化对扩展LLM推理能力具有显著潜力，存在广阔的提升空间。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind RefineRL is to enhance large language models' performance in competitive programming by moving beyond single-attempt solutions and leveraging their self-refinement capabilities, which are often underutilized. The method introduces a Skeptical-Agent that iteratively validates generated code against public test cases while maintaining a skeptical stance to enforce rigorous self-improvement, combined with a reinforcement learning approach trained on standard RLVR data to incentivize this refinement process. Experimental results on compact 4B models like Qwen3-4B show that after RL training, these models integrated with the Skeptical-Agent outperform larger 32B models and approach the single-attempt performance of much larger 235B models, indicating significant potential for scaling reasoning through self-refinement.
RefineRL的动机是通过超越单次尝试的解决方案并利用大型语言模型常被忽视的自我优化能力，来提升其在竞争性编程中的表现。该方法引入了Skeptical-Agent，该代理通过本地执行工具迭代验证生成的代码是否符合公开测试用例，并保持怀疑态度以强制进行严格自我改进，同时结合基于标准RLVR数据训练的强化学习方法激励这一优化过程。在Qwen3-4B等紧凑型4B模型上的实验结果表明，经过强化学习训练后，这些结合Skeptical-Agent的模型性能超越了更大的32B模型，并接近了庞大235B模型的单次尝试表现，这揭示了通过自我优化扩展推理能力的巨大潜力。
Finding Low Star Discrepancy 3D Kronecker Point Sets Using Algorithm Configuration Techniques
Authors: Imène Ait Abderrahim, Carola Doerr, Martin Durand
First: 2026-04-01T11:51:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T11:51:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The L infinity star discrepancy is a measure for how uniformly a point set is distributed in a given space. Point sets of low star discrepancy are used as designs of experiments, as initial designs for Bayesian optimization algorithms, for quasi-Monte Carlo integration methods, and many other applications. Recent work has shown that classical constructions such as Sobol', Halton, or Hammersley sequences can be outperformed by large margins when considering point sets of fixed sizes rather than their convergence behavior. These results, highly relevant to the aforementioned applications, raise the question of how much existing constructions can be improved through size-specific optimization. In this work, we study this question for the so-called Kronecker construction. Focusing on the 3-dimensional setting, we show that optimizing the two configurable parameters of its construction yields point sets outperforming the state-of-the-art value for sets of at least 500 points. Using the algorithm configuration technique irace, we then derive parameters that yield new state-of-the-art discrepancy values for whole ranges of set sizes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：运用算法配置技术寻找低星差异三维克罗内克点集
L无穷星差异是衡量点集在给定空间中分布均匀性的指标。低星差异点集被广泛应用于实验设计、贝叶斯优化算法的初始设计、拟蒙特卡洛积分方法及其他诸多领域。近期研究表明，在固定点集规模而非收敛行为的考量下，经典构造方法（如Sobol'、Halton或Hammersley序列）的性能可被大幅超越。这些与前述应用高度相关的结果引出一个问题：通过针对特定规模的优化，现有构造方法能获得多大程度的改进？本研究针对所谓的克罗内克构造方法探讨该问题。聚焦三维场景，我们证明通过优化其两个可配置参数，所得点集在至少500点规模上能超越现有最优值。运用算法配置技术irace，我们进一步推导出可为连续点集规模范围带来全新最优差异值的参数配置。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for highly uniform point sets in applications like experimental design and quasi-Monte Carlo integration, this paper investigates whether optimizing size-specific parameters can improve upon classical low-discrepancy sequences. The method focuses on the Kronecker construction in 3D, using the algorithm configuration tool irace to tune its two configurable parameters for fixed set sizes. Experimental results demonstrate that the optimized parameters produce point sets with lower star discrepancy than state-of-the-art constructions for sets of at least 500 points, achieving new best values across various size ranges.
本研究旨在为实验设计和拟蒙特卡洛积分等应用寻找高度均匀的点集，探讨通过优化特定尺寸参数能否改进经典的低差异序列构造方法。方法上聚焦于三维Kronecker构造，利用算法配置工具irace对其两个可调参数进行针对固定点集尺寸的优化。实验结果表明，优化后的参数生成的500点以上点集，其星差异值优于现有最优构造，并在多个尺寸范围内取得了新的最佳记录。
HiMA-Ecom: Enabling Joint Training of Hierarchical Multi-Agent E-commerce Assistants
Authors: Junxing Hu, Ai Han, Haolan Zhan, Pu Wei, Zhiqian Zhang, Yuhang Guo, Jiawei Lu, Zhen Chen, Haoran Li, Zicheng Zhang
First: 2025-06-24T17:59:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T10:25:03+00:00
Comments: 39 pages, 10 figures, under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hierarchical multi-agent systems based on large language models (LLMs) have become a common paradigm for building AI assistants in vertical domains such as e-commerce, where a master agent coordinates multiple specialized sub-agents. Despite their practical importance, realistic benchmarks for training and evaluating such systems remain scarce, and joint optimization across functionally distinct agents is still challenging. To address this gap, we introduce HiMA-Ecom, the first hierarchical multi-agent benchmark tailored for e-commerce scenarios. HiMA-Ecom contains 22.8K instances, including agent-specific supervised fine-tuning samples with memory and system-level input-output pairs for joint multi-agent reinforcement learning. Building upon it, a joint training method named HiMA-R1 is proposed. It presents Variance-Reduction Group Relative Policy Optimization (VR-GRPO), which employs initial trajectory-based Monte Carlo sampling to mitigate the exponential joint action space and selects informative agent groups for efficient updates based on reward variance. Furthermore, an adaptive memory evolution mechanism that repurposes GRPO rewards as cost-free supervisory signals is designed to eliminate repetitive reasoning and accelerate convergence. Experiments on HiMA-Ecom demonstrate that our method, built upon smaller 3B/7B open-source models, achieves performance comparable to that of larger LLMs, such as DeepSeek-R1, and surpasses DeepSeek-V3 by an average of 6\%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HiMA-Ecom：实现分层多智能体电商助手的联合训练
基于大语言模型的分层多智能体系统已成为构建电商等垂直领域AI助手的常见范式，其中主智能体协调多个专业子智能体。尽管其具有重要实践意义，用于训练和评估此类系统的真实基准仍十分稀缺，且跨功能各异智能体的联合优化仍具挑战。为填补这一空白，我们推出首个专为电商场景定制的分层多智能体基准HiMA-Ecom。该基准包含22.8K个实例，涵盖用于智能体特定监督微调的带记忆样本，以及用于联合多智能体强化学习的系统级输入-输出对。在此基础上，我们提出名为HiMA-R1的联合训练方法，其核心是方差缩减组相对策略优化算法。该算法采用基于初始轨迹的蒙特卡洛采样以缓解指数级联合动作空间，并根据奖励方差选择信息量大的智能体组进行高效更新。此外，设计了一种自适应记忆演化机制，将GRPO奖励重新用作无成本监督信号，以消除重复推理并加速收敛。在HiMA-Ecom上的实验表明，基于较小3B/7B开源模型构建的方法，其性能可媲美DeepSeek-R1等更大规模模型，并平均超越DeepSeek-V3达6%。

The paper addresses the lack of realistic benchmarks and joint training methods for hierarchical multi-agent AI assistants in e-commerce, where a master agent coordinates specialized sub-agents. Experimental results show that this approach, using smaller 3B/7B models, achieves performance comparable to larger models like DeepSeek-R1 and surpasses DeepSeek-V3 by an average of 6%.
本文针对电子商务中由主智能体协调多个专业子智能体的分层多智能体AI助手，缺乏现实基准和联合训练方法的问题，提出了HiMA-Ecom基准，包含22.8K个实例，用于监督微调和多智能体强化学习，并设计了HiMA-R1联合训练方法，其核心是方差缩减组相对策略优化（VR-GRPO），通过蒙特卡洛采样处理指数级动作空间并进行基于组的更新，以及自适应记忆演化机制以减少重复推理。实验结果表明，该方法基于较小的3B/7B模型，实现了与DeepSeek-R1等更大模型相当的性能，并平均超越DeepSeek-V3达6%。
G-ICSO-NAS: Shifting Gears between Gradient and Swarm for Robust Neural Architecture Search
Authors: Xingbang Du, Enzhi Zhang, Rui Zhong, Yang Cao, Masaharu Munetomo
First: 2026-04-01T10:06:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T10:06:59+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the International Joint Conference on Neural Networks (IJCNN), WCCI 2026. This is a preprint version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural Architecture Search (NAS) has become a pivotal technique in automated machine learning. Evolutionary Algorithm (EA)-based methods demonstrate superior search quality but suffer from prohibitive computational costs, while gradient-based approaches like DARTS offer high efficiency but are prone to premature convergence and performance collapse. To bridge this gap, we propose G-ICSO-NAS, a hybrid framework implementing a three-stage optimization strategy. The Warm-up Phase pre-trains supernet weights ($w$) via differentiable methods while architecture parameters ($α$) remain frozen. The Exploration Phase adopts a hybrid co-optimization mechanism: an Improved Competitive Swarm Optimizer (ICSO) with diversity-aware fitness navigates the architecture space to update $α$, while gradient descent concurrently updates $w$. The Stability Phase employs fine-grained gradient-based search with early stopping to converge to the optimal architecture. By synergizing ICSO's global navigation capability with differentiable methods' efficiency, G-ICSO-NAS achieves remarkable performance with minimal cost. In the context of the DARTS search space, an accuracy of 97.46\% is achieved on CIFAR-10 with a computational budget of just 0.15 GPU-Days. The method also exhibits strong transfer potential, recording accuracies of 83.1\% (CIFAR-100) and 75.02\% (ImageNet). Furthermore, regarding the NAS-Bench-201 benchmark, G-ICSO-NAS is shown to deliver state-of-the-art results across all evaluated datasets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：G-ICSO-NAS：在梯度与群体智能间切换以实现鲁棒的神经架构搜索
神经架构搜索已成为自动化机器学习的关键技术。基于进化算法的方法展现出卓越的搜索质量，但计算成本过高；而如DARTS的梯度方法虽效率高，却易陷入早熟收敛与性能崩溃。为弥合此差距，我们提出G-ICSO-NAS——一种实施三阶段优化策略的混合框架：预热阶段通过可微分方法预训练超网络权重（$w$），同时冻结架构参数（$α$）；探索阶段采用混合协同优化机制：具备多样性感知适应度的改进竞争群体优化器在架构空间中导航以更新$α$，同时梯度下降并行更新$w$；稳定阶段采用细粒度梯度搜索与早停策略收敛至最优架构。通过融合ICSO的全局导航能力与可微分方法的高效性，G-ICSO-NAS以极低成本取得显著性能：在DARTS搜索空间下，仅用0.15 GPU天计算预算即在CIFAR-10达到97.46%准确率；同时展现强大迁移潜力，在CIFAR-100与ImageNet分别获得83.1%与75.02%准确率；在NAS-Bench-201基准测试中，G-ICSO-NAS在所有评估数据集上均取得前沿成果。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the trade-off between the high search quality but prohibitive cost of evolutionary NAS methods and the efficiency but instability of gradient-based approaches like DARTS, this paper proposes G-ICSO-NAS, a hybrid three-stage framework. The method combines gradient and swarm optimization: it begins with a warm-up phase for supernet weights, then enters an exploration phase where an Improved Competitive Swarm Optimizer (ICSO) updates architecture parameters for global navigation while gradients update weights, and finally a stability phase uses fine-grained gradient search for convergence. Key experimental results show the method achieves 97.46% accuracy on CIFAR-10 with only 0.15 GPU-days, along with strong transfer performance of 83.1% on CIFAR-100 and 75.02% on ImageNet, and delivers state-of-the-art results on the NAS-Bench-201 benchmark.
本文的动机是解决神经架构搜索中进化算法搜索质量高但计算成本巨大，与梯度方法（如DARTS）效率高但易早熟收敛之间的权衡。为此，提出了G-ICSO-NAS这一混合三阶段框架，其方法融合了梯度和群智能优化：首先通过预热阶段预训练超网络权重，然后在探索阶段采用改进的竞争群优化器（ICSO）更新架构参数以实现全局探索，同时用梯度下降更新权重，最后在稳定阶段进行细粒度梯度搜索以收敛到最优架构。主要实验结果表明，该方法在CIFAR-10上仅用0.15 GPU天就达到了97.46%的准确率，在CIFAR-100和ImageNet上分别取得了83.1%和75.02%的迁移性能，并在NAS-Bench-201基准测试中实现了最先进的结果。
Learning to Hint for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yu Xia, Canwen Xu, Zhewei Yao, Julian McAuley, Yuxiong He
First: 2026-04-01T09:58:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:58:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is widely used for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, but it often suffers from advantage collapse: when all rollouts in a group receive the same reward, the group yields zero relative advantage and thus no learning signal. For example, if a question is too hard for the reasoner, all sampled rollouts can be incorrect and receive zero reward. Recent work addresses this issue by adding hints or auxiliary scaffolds to such hard questions so that the reasoner produces mixed outcomes and recovers a non-zero update. However, existing hints are usually fixed rather than adapted to the current reasoner, and a hint that creates learning signal under the hinted input does not necessarily improve the no-hint policy used at test time. To this end, we propose Hint Learning for Reinforcement Learning (HiLL), a framework that jointly trains a hinter policy and a reasoner policy during RL. For each hard question, the hinter generates hints online conditioned on the current reasoner's incorrect rollout, allowing hint generation to adapt to the reasoner's evolving errors. We further introduce hint reliance, which measures how strongly correct hinted trajectories depend on the hint. We derive a transferability result showing that lower hint reliance implies stronger transfer from hinted success to no-hint success, and we use this result to define a transfer-weighted reward for training the hinter. Therefore, HiLL favors hints that not only recover informative GRPO groups, but also produce signals that are more likely to improve the original no-hint policy. Experiments across multiple benchmarks show that HiLL consistently outperforms GRPO and prior hint-based baselines, demonstrating the value of adaptive and transfer-aware hint learning for RL. The code is available at https://github.com/Andree-9/HiLL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中的提示学习
组相对策略优化（GRPO）广泛用于具有可验证奖励的强化学习，但常面临优势坍缩问题：当组内所有轨迹获得相同奖励时，该组产生零相对优势，导致学习信号缺失。例如，若问题对推理器过难，所有采样轨迹可能均错误且获得零奖励。近期研究通过向此类难题添加提示或辅助支架来解决该问题，使推理器产生混合结果并恢复非零更新。然而，现有提示通常是固定的而非适配当前推理器，且在提示输入下产生学习信号的提示未必能提升测试时使用的无提示策略。为此，我们提出强化学习提示学习框架（HiLL），在强化学习过程中联合训练提示器策略与推理器策略。针对每个难题，提示器根据当前推理器的错误轨迹在线生成适配其动态错误的提示。我们进一步提出提示依赖度指标，用于衡量正确提示轨迹对提示的依赖强度。通过推导可迁移性理论证明：较低的提示依赖度意味着从提示成功向无提示成功的更强迁移，并基于此定义用于训练提示器的迁移加权奖励。因此，HiLL倾向于选择既能恢复信息性GRPO分组，又能产生更可能改进原始无提示策略的学习信号的提示。多基准实验表明，HiLL持续优于GRPO及现有基于提示的基线方法，验证了自适应且具备迁移感知的提示学习对强化学习的价值。代码发布于 https://github.com/Andree-9/HiLL。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of advantage collapse in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for reinforcement learning, where hard tasks yield zero learning signal because all rollouts fail equally. To overcome this, the authors propose HiLL, a framework that jointly trains a hinter policy to generate adaptive hints based on the reasoner's current errors and a reasoner policy, while introducing a hint reliance metric to ensure hints improve the no-hint policy via a transfer-weighted reward. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that HiLL consistently outperforms GRPO and prior hint-based methods, validating the effectiveness of adaptive and transfer-aware hint learning.
本文针对强化学习中组相对策略优化（GRPO）的优势崩溃问题，即困难任务因所有轨迹均失败而无法提供学习信号。为解决此问题，作者提出了HiLL框架，联合训练一个提示生成策略（根据推理器当前错误自适应生成提示）和一个推理器策略，并引入提示依赖度指标，通过基于转移的加权奖励确保提示能提升无提示策略。在多个基准测试上的实验结果表明，HiLL持续优于GRPO及先前的基于提示的方法，验证了自适应且关注转移的提示学习的有效性。
Meta-Learning and Meta-Reinforcement Learning -- Tracing the Path towards DeepMind's Adaptive Agent
Authors: Björn Hoppmann, Christoph Scholz
First: 2026-02-23T13:39:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:55:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Humans are highly effective at utilizing prior knowledge to adapt to novel tasks, a capability that standard machine learning models struggle to replicate due to their reliance on task-specific training. Meta-learning overcomes this limitation by allowing models to acquire transferable knowledge from various tasks, enabling rapid adaptation to new challenges with minimal data. This survey provides a rigorous, task-based formalization of meta-learning and meta-reinforcement learning and uses that paradigm to chronicle the landmark algorithms that paved the way for DeepMind's Adaptive Agent, consolidating the essential concepts needed to understand the Adaptive Agent and other generalist approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：元学习与元强化学习——追溯通往DeepMind自适应智能体的演进路径
人类善于利用先验知识适应新任务，而标准机器学习模型因依赖任务特定训练难以复现此能力。元学习通过让模型从多任务中获取可迁移知识，突破这一局限，使其能以少量数据快速适应新挑战。本文基于任务形式化框架，系统梳理元学习与元强化学习的里程碑算法，追溯其促成DeepMind自适应智能体的发展脉络，并整合理解该智能体及其他通用方法所需的核心概念。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the human ability to leverage prior knowledge for quick adaptation, which standard machine learning lacks due to its task-specific nature, this survey formalizes meta-learning and meta-reinforcement learning as frameworks for acquiring transferable knowledge across tasks. The method involves a rigorous task-based formalization to trace the evolution of key algorithms that enable rapid adaptation with minimal data. The main experimental results are not detailed individually, but the work consolidates the conceptual and algorithmic advancements that culminated in DeepMind's Adaptive Agent, highlighting its role as a generalist model built on these meta-learning principles.
本文的动机是人类能够利用先验知识快速适应新任务，而标准机器学习模型因依赖任务特定训练而难以实现这一点，因此通过元学习和元强化学习框架来获取可迁移知识。方法上采用基于任务的严格形式化，追溯了关键算法的发展路径，这些算法使得模型能够以最少数据快速适应新挑战。主要实验结果未具体展开，但该综述整合了理解DeepMind自适应智能体及其他通用方法所需的核心概念，总结了导致该智能体诞生的算法进展。
Full-Gradient Successor Feature Representations
Authors: Ritish Shrirao, Aditya Priyadarshi, Raghuram Bharadwaj Diddigi
First: 2026-04-01T09:44:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:44:13+00:00
Comments: Submitted to IEEE CDC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Successor Features (SF) combined with Generalized Policy Improvement (GPI) provide a robust framework for transfer learning in Reinforcement Learning (RL) by decoupling environment dynamics from reward functions. However, standard SF learning methods typically rely on semi-gradient Temporal Difference (TD) updates. When combined with non-linear function approximation, semi-gradient methods lack robust convergence guarantees and can lead to instability, particularly in the multi-task setting where accurate feature estimation is critical for effective GPI. Inspired by Full Gradient DQN, we propose Full-Gradient Successor Feature Representations Q-Learning (FG-SFRQL), an algorithm that optimizes the successor features by minimizing the full Mean Squared Bellman Error. Unlike standard approaches, our method computes gradients with respect to parameters in both the online and target networks. We provide a theoretical proof of almost-sure convergence for FG-SFRQL and demonstrate empirically that minimizing the full residual leads to superior sample efficiency and transfer performance compared to semi-gradient baselines in both discrete and continuous domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：全梯度后继特征表示
后继特征（SF）与广义策略改进（GPI）相结合，通过解耦环境动态与奖励函数，为强化学习（RL）中的迁移学习提供了稳健框架。然而，标准SF学习方法通常依赖半梯度时序差分（TD）更新。当与非线性函数逼近结合时，半梯度方法缺乏稳健的收敛保证，可能导致不稳定，尤其在多任务场景中——精确的特征估计对有效GPI至关重要。受全梯度DQN启发，我们提出全梯度后继特征表示Q学习算法（FG-SFRQL），该算法通过最小化完整的均方贝尔曼误差来优化后继特征。与标准方法不同，本方法同时计算在线网络和目标网络参数的梯度。我们为FG-SFRQL提供了几乎必然收敛的理论证明，并通过实验验证：在离散与连续域中，最小化完整残差相比半梯度基线方法具有更优的样本效率与迁移性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the instability and lack of convergence guarantees in standard semi-gradient methods for learning Successor Features (SF) with non-linear function approximation, which is critical for robust transfer learning in multi-task RL. The proposed method, Full-Gradient Successor Feature Representations Q-Learning (FG-SFRQL), addresses this by optimizing successor features through minimization of the full Mean Squared Bellman Error, computing gradients with respect to both online and target network parameters. Experimental results demonstrate that FG-SFRQL provides theoretical almost-sure convergence and empirically achieves superior sample efficiency and transfer performance over semi-gradient baselines in discrete and continuous domains.

Large Language Model Guided Incentive Aware Reward Design for Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dogan Urgun, Gokhan Gungor
First: 2026-03-25T14:05:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:31:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing effective auxiliary rewards for cooperative multi-agent systems remains a challenging task. Misaligned incentives risk inducing suboptimal coordination, especially when sparse task feedback fails to provide sufficient grounding. This study introduces an automated reward design framework that leverages large language models to synthesize executable reward programs from environment instrumentation. The procedure constrains candidate programs within a formal validity envelope and evaluates their efficacy by training policies from scratch under a fixed computational budget. Selection across generations depends exclusively on the sparse task return. The framework is evaluated across four distinct Overcooked-AI layouts characterized by varied corridor congestion, handoff dependencies, and structural asymmetries. Iterative search generations consistently yield superior task returns and delivery counts, with the most pronounced gains occurring in environments dominated by interaction bottlenecks. Diagnostic analysis of the synthesized shaping components indicates increased interdependence in action selection and improved signal alignment in coordination-intensive tasks. These results demonstrate that the search for objective-grounded reward programs can mitigate the burden of manual engineering while producing shaping signals compatible with cooperative learning under finite budgets.

标题：大语言模型引导的激励感知奖励设计用于合作多智能体强化学习
为合作多智能体系统设计有效的辅助奖励仍具挑战性。激励错配可能导致次优协调，尤其在稀疏任务反馈无法提供充分依据时。本研究提出一种自动化奖励设计框架，利用大语言模型从环境监测数据中合成可执行的奖励程序。该流程将候选程序约束在形式化有效范围内，并通过在固定计算预算下从头训练策略来评估其效能。代际选择完全依据稀疏任务回报。该框架在四种不同的《Overcooked-AI》场景布局中进行评估，这些布局具有不同的通道拥堵度、交接依赖性和结构不对称性。迭代搜索代次持续产生更优的任务回报与配送数量，在交互瓶颈主导的环境中增益最为显著。对合成塑形组件的诊断分析表明，动作选择的相互依赖性增强，且在协调密集型任务中信号对齐得到改善。这些结果表明，基于目标的奖励程序搜索能减轻人工设计负担，同时生成与有限预算下合作学习兼容的塑形信号。

Motivated by the challenge of designing effective auxiliary rewards for cooperative multi-agent systems, where misaligned incentives can lead to suboptimal coordination, this study introduces an automated reward design framework that leverages large language models to synthesize executable reward programs from environment instrumentation. Klear-Reasoner: Advancing Reasoning Capability via Gradient-Preserving Clipping Policy Optimization
Authors: Zhenpeng Su, Leiyu Pan, Xue Bai, Dening Liu, Guanting Dong, Jiaming Huang, Minxuan Lv, Wenping Hu, Fuzheng Zhang, Kun Gai, Guorui Zhou
First: 2025-08-11T05:17:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:05:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Klear-Reasoner, a model with long reasoning capabilities that demonstrates careful deliberation during problem solving, achieving outstanding performance across multiple benchmarks. Although there are already many excellent works related to inference models in the current community, there are still many problems with reproducing high-performance inference models due to incomplete disclosure of training details. This report provides an in-depth analysis of the reasoning model, covering the entire post-training workflow from data preparation and long Chain-of-Thought supervised fine-tuning (long CoT SFT) to reinforcement learning (RL), along with detailed ablation studies for each experimental component. For SFT data, our experiments show that a small number of high-quality data sources are more effective than a large number of diverse data sources, and that difficult samples can achieve better results without accuracy filtering. In addition, we investigate two key issues with current clipping mechanisms in RL: Clipping suppresses critical exploration signals and ignores suboptimal trajectories. To address these challenges, we propose Gradient-Preserving clipping Policy Optimization (GPPO) that gently backpropagates gradients from clipped tokens. GPPO not only enhances the model's exploration capacity but also improves its efficiency in learning from negative samples. Klear-Reasoner exhibits exceptional reasoning abilities in mathematics and programming, scoring 90.5% on AIME 2024, 83.2% on AIME 2025, 66.0% on LiveCodeBench V5 and 58.1% on LiveCodeBench V6.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Klear-Reasoner：通过梯度保留裁剪策略优化提升推理能力
我们提出Klear-Reasoner，一种具备长程推理能力的模型，在解决问题时展现出审慎的思考过程，并在多个基准测试中取得卓越性能。尽管当前社区已有许多优秀的推理模型相关研究，但由于训练细节披露不完整，复现高性能推理模型仍存在诸多困难。本报告对推理模型进行了深入分析，涵盖从数据准备、长链思维监督微调（长CoT SFT）到强化学习（RL）的完整训练后工作流程，并对每个实验模块进行了详细的消融研究。在SFT数据方面，实验表明少量高质量数据源比大量多样化数据源更有效，且困难样本无需精度过滤即可获得更好效果。此外，我们研究了当前RL裁剪机制的两个关键问题：裁剪抑制关键探索信号并忽略次优轨迹。针对这些挑战，我们提出梯度保留裁剪策略优化（GPPO），可温和地反向传播来自裁剪标记的梯度。GPPO不仅增强了模型的探索能力，还提升了其从负样本中学习的效率。Klear-Reasoner在数学和编程领域展现出卓越推理能力，在AIME 2024得分90.5%、AIME 2025得分83.2%、LiveCodeBench V5得分66.0%、LiveCodeBench V6得分58.1%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the difficulty of reproducing high-performance reasoning models due to insufficient training detail disclosure, this paper introduces Klear-Reasoner, a model designed for long reasoning chains. The method involves a detailed post-training workflow including data preparation, long Chain-of-Thought supervised fine-tuning (SFT), and a novel reinforcement learning component called Gradient-Preserving clipping Policy Optimization (GPPO), which addresses issues in standard clipping by gently backpropagating gradients from clipped tokens to preserve exploration signals and improve learning from negative trajectories. Finite-State Controllers for (Hidden-Model) POMDPs using Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: David Hudák, Maris F. L. Galesloot, Martin Tappler, Martin Kurečka, Nils Jansen, Milan Češka
First: 2026-02-09T14:39:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T08:22:16+00:00
Comments: 17 pages (8 main paper, 2 references, 7 appendix). 3 figures in the main paper, 3 figures in the appendix. Accepted AAMAS'26 submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Solving partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs) requires computing policies under imperfect state information. Despite recent advances, the scalability of existing POMDP solvers remains limited. Moreover, many settings require a policy that is robust across multiple POMDPs, further aggravating the scalability issue. We propose the Lexpop framework for POMDP solving. Lexpop (1) employs deep reinforcement learning to train a neural policy, represented by a recurrent neural network, and (2) constructs a finite-state controller mimicking the neural policy through efficient extraction methods. Crucially, unlike neural policies, such controllers can be formally evaluated, providing performance guarantees. We extend Lexpop to compute robust policies for hidden-model POMDPs (HM-POMDPs), which describe finite sets of POMDPs. We associate every extracted controller with its worst-case POMDP. Using a set of such POMDPs, we iteratively train a robust neural policy and consequently extract a robust controller. Our experiments show that on problems with large state spaces, Lexpop outperforms state-of-the-art solvers for POMDPs as well as HM-POMDPs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的（隐模型）部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程有限状态控制器
求解部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程需要在状态信息不完整的情况下计算策略。尽管近期研究取得进展，现有POMDP求解器的可扩展性仍受限。此外，许多场景要求策略在多个POMDP中保持鲁棒性，进一步加剧了可扩展性问题。我们提出Lexpop框架用于POMDP求解，该框架（1）采用深度强化学习训练由循环神经网络表示的神经策略，（2）通过高效提取方法构建模拟神经策略的有限状态控制器。关键的是，与神经策略不同，此类控制器可进行形式化验证并提供性能保证。我们将Lexpop扩展至隐模型POMDP的鲁棒策略计算，该模型描述有限POMDP集合。我们为每个提取的控制器关联其最差情况POMDP，利用此类POMDP集合迭代训练鲁棒神经策略并提取鲁棒控制器。实验表明，在大状态空间问题上，Lexpop在POMDP及HM-POMDP求解性能上均优于当前最优方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the scalability limitations of existing solvers for partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs) and the need for policies robust across multiple models, this paper introduces the Lexpop framework. The method first trains a neural policy using deep reinforcement learning with a recurrent neural network, then extracts a finite-state controller that mimics this policy, enabling formal evaluation and performance guarantees. The approach is extended to hidden-model POMDPs by iteratively training a robust neural policy against worst-case models and extracting a corresponding robust controller. Experimental results demonstrate that Lexpop outperforms state-of-the-art solvers on problems with large state spaces for both standard POMDPs and HM-POMDPs.
针对现有部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程求解器可扩展性不足以及需要跨多个模型的鲁棒策略的问题，本文提出了Lexpop框架。该方法首先使用深度强化学习和循环神经网络训练神经策略，然后通过高效提取方法构建模仿该策略的有限状态控制器，从而支持形式化验证和性能保证。该框架被扩展到隐模型POMDP，通过迭代训练针对最坏情况模型的鲁棒神经策略并提取相应的鲁棒控制器。实验结果表明，在大状态空间问题上，Lexpop在标准POMDP和隐模型POMDP上的性能均优于当前最先进的求解器。
MemFactory: Unified Inference & Training Framework for Agent Memory
Authors: Ziliang Guo, Ziheng Li, Bo Tang, Feiyu Xiong, Zhiyu Li
First: 2026-03-31T09:38:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T08:16:25+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, Code: https://github.com/Valsure/MemFactory
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Memory-augmented Large Language Models (LLMs) are essential for developing capable, long-term AI agents. Recently, applying Reinforcement Learning (RL) to optimize memory operations, such as extraction, updating, and retrieval, has emerged as a highly promising research direction. However, existing implementations remain highly fragmented and task-specific, lacking a unified infrastructure to streamline the integration, training, and evaluation of these complex pipelines. To address this gap, we present MemFactory, the first unified, highly modular training and inference framework specifically designed for memory-augmented agents. Inspired by the success of unified fine-tuning frameworks like LLaMA-Factory, MemFactory abstracts the memory lifecycle into atomic, plug-and-play components, enabling researchers to seamlessly construct custom memory agents via a "Lego-like" architecture. Furthermore, the framework natively integrates Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to fine-tune internal memory management policies driven by multi-dimensional environmental rewards. MemFactory provides out-of-the-box support for recent cutting-edge paradigms, including Memory-R1, RMM, and MemAgent. We empirically validate MemFactory on the open-source MemAgent architecture using its publicly available training and evaluation data. Across both in-domain and out-of-distribution evaluation sets, MemFactory consistently improves performance over the corresponding base models, with relative gains of up to 14.8%. By providing a standardized, extensible, and easy-to-use infrastructure, MemFactory significantly lowers the barrier to entry, paving the way for future innovations in memory-driven AI agents.

针对现有基于强化学习优化大语言模型智能体记忆操作的实现方案存在碎片化、任务特定性且缺乏统一基础设施的问题，本文提出了MemFactory，一个用于记忆增强智能体的统一、模块化训练与推理框架。该方法将记忆生命周期抽象为即插即用的原子组件，支持通过“乐高式”架构灵活构建定制化记忆智能体，并原生集成了群体相对策略优化（GRPO）来利用多维环境奖励微调内部记忆管理策略。在MemAgent架构上的实验验证表明，该框架在领域内和分布外评估集上均能持续提升基础模型的性能，相对增益最高达14.8%。
On Global Convergence Rates for Federated Softmax Policy Gradient under Heterogeneous Environments
Authors: Safwan Labbi, Paul Mangold, Daniil Tiapkin, Eric Moulines
First: 2025-05-29T14:08:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T07:46:23+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We provide global convergence rates for vanilla and entropy-regularized federated softmax stochastic policy gradient (FedPG) with local training. We show that FedPG converges to a near-optimal policy in terms of the average agent value, with a gap controlled by the level of heterogeneity. Remarkably, we obtain the first convergence rates for entropy-regularized policy gradient with explicit constants, leveraging a projection-like operator. Our results build upon a new analysis of federated averaging for non-convex objectives, based on the observation that the Łojasiewicz-type inequalities from the single-agent setting (Mei et al., 2020) do not hold for the federated objective. This uncovers a fundamental difference between single-agent and federated reinforcement learning: while single-agent optimal policies can be deterministic, federated objectives may inherently require stochastic policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：异构环境下联邦软最大策略梯度的全局收敛速率分析
本文针对本地训练的原始及熵正则化联邦软最大随机策略梯度（FedPG）方法，给出了全局收敛速率。研究表明，FedPG在平均智能体价值意义上收敛至接近最优的策略，其差距受异构程度控制。值得注意的是，通过利用类投影算子，我们首次获得了熵正则化策略梯度具有显式常数的收敛速率。这些结果建立在对联邦平均方法在非凸目标上的新分析基础上，该分析基于以下观察：单智能体设置中的Łojasiewicz型不等式（Mei等人，2020）不适用于联邦目标。这揭示了单智能体与联邦强化学习之间的根本差异：单智能体最优策略可以是确定性的，而联邦目标可能本质上需要随机策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the convergence of federated softmax policy gradient (FedPG) methods in heterogeneous reinforcement learning environments, motivated by the need to understand how policy optimization behaves when data is distributed across multiple agents with differing dynamics. The authors analyze both vanilla and entropy-regularized versions of FedPG with local training, employing a novel analysis of federated averaging for non-convex objectives that addresses the failure of Łojasiewicz-type inequalities in the federated setting. Key experimental results demonstrate that FedPG converges to a near-optimal policy in terms of average agent value, with the performance gap explicitly bounded by the level of environmental heterogeneity, and they provide the first convergence rates with explicit constants for entropy-regularized policy gradient, revealing that federated objectives may inherently require stochastic policies unlike single-agent cases.
本文研究了在异构强化学习环境中联邦软最大值策略梯度（FedPG）方法的收敛性，其动机在于需要理解当数据分布在具有不同动态特性的多个智能体上时策略优化的行为。作者分析了带有局部训练的普通版本和熵正则化版本的FedPG，采用了一种针对非凸目标的联邦平均新分析方法，以解决联邦设置中Łojasiewicz型不等式不成立的问题。主要实验结果表明，FedPG在平均智能体价值方面收敛到接近最优的策略，性能差距由环境异质性水平明确控制，并且首次给出了熵正则化策略梯度具有显式常数的收敛速率，揭示了联邦目标可能本质上需要随机策略，这与单智能体情况不同。
Optimsyn: Influence-Guided Rubrics Optimization for Synthetic Data Generation
Authors: Zhiting Fan, Ruizhe Chen, Tianxiang Hu, Ru Peng, Zenan Huang, Haokai Xu, Yixin Chen, Jian Wu, Junbo Zhao, Zuozhu Liu
First: 2026-04-01T06:28:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T06:28:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong downstream performance largely due to abundant supervised fine-tuning (SFT) data. However, high-quality SFT data in knowledge-intensive domains such as humanities, social sciences, medicine, law, and finance is scarce because expert curation is expensive, privacy constraints are strict, and label consistency is hard to ensure. Recent work uses synthetic data, typically by prompting a generator over domain documents and filtering outputs with handcrafted rubrics. Yet rubric design is expert-dependent, transfers poorly across domains, and is often optimized through a brittle heuristic loop of writing rubrics, synthesizing data, training, inspecting results, and manually guessing revisions. This process lacks reliable quantitative feedback about how a rubric affects downstream performance. We propose evaluating synthetic data by its training utility on the target model and using this signal to guide data generation. Inspired by influence estimation, we adopt an optimizer-aware estimator that uses gradient information to quantify each synthetic sample's contribution to a target model's objective on specific tasks. Our analysis shows that even when synthetic and real samples are close in embedding space, their influence on learning can differ substantially. Based on this insight, we propose an optimization-based framework that adapts rubrics using target-model feedback. We provide lightweight guiding text and use a rubric-specialized model to generate task-conditioned rubrics. Influence score is used as the reward to optimize the rubric generator with reinforcement learning. Experiments across domains, target models, and data generators show consistent improvements and strong generalization without task-specific tuning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Optimsyn：面向合成数据生成的影响引导式评估准则优化
大语言模型（LLMs）在下游任务中的优异表现主要得益于丰富的监督微调（SFT）数据。然而，在人文学科、社会科学、医学、法律和金融等知识密集型领域，高质量SFT数据十分稀缺，原因在于专家标注成本高昂、隐私约束严格且标签一致性难以保证。近期研究采用合成数据方案，通常基于领域文档提示生成器，并用手工设计的评估准则过滤输出。但评估准则设计依赖专家经验，跨领域迁移性差，且常通过脆弱的启发式循环（编写准则→合成数据→训练→检验结果→人工推测修订）进行优化。该过程缺乏关于评估准则如何影响下游性能的可靠量化反馈。我们提出通过合成数据在目标模型上的训练效用进行评估，并利用该信号指导数据生成。受影响估计的启发，我们采用优化器感知的估计器，利用梯度信息量化每个合成样本对目标模型在特定任务目标上的贡献。分析表明，即使合成样本与真实样本在嵌入空间中相近，它们对学习过程的影响也可能存在显著差异。基于此洞见，我们提出基于优化的框架，利用目标模型反馈自适应调整评估准则。我们提供轻量级引导文本，并采用准则专用模型生成任务条件化评估准则。以影响分数作为奖励，通过强化学习优化准则生成器。跨领域、目标模型与数据生成器的实验表明，该方法无需任务特定调优即可实现持续改进与强大泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of generating high-quality synthetic data for supervised fine-tuning of large language models in knowledge-intensive domains where expert-curated data is scarce and expensive. The proposed method, Optimsyn, introduces an influence-guided optimization framework that uses gradient-based influence estimation to quantify each synthetic sample's contribution to the target model's performance on specific tasks, enabling data evaluation based on training utility rather than manual rubric design. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach consistently improves downstream performance across various domains, target models, and data generators, offering strong generalization without requiring task-specific tuning.
本文针对知识密集型领域中高质量监督微调数据稀缺且昂贵的问题，提出了一种影响引导的合成数据生成优化方法。该方法名为Optimsyn，采用基于梯度的影响估计来量化每个合成样本对目标模型在特定任务上性能的贡献，从而依据训练效用而非人工设计的评分标准来评估数据。实验结果表明，该方法在不同领域、目标模型和数据生成器上均能持续提升下游性能，并展现出强大的泛化能力，无需针对具体任务进行调优。
MOON3.0: Reasoning-aware Multimodal Representation Learning for E-commerce Product Understanding
Authors: Junxian Wu, Chenghan Fu, Zhanheng Nie, Daoze Zhang, Bowen Wan, Wanxian Guan, Chuan Yu, Jian Xu, Bo Zheng
First: 2026-04-01T05:55:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T05:55:25+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the rapid growth of e-commerce, exploring general representations rather than task-specific ones has attracted increasing attention. Although recent multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have driven significant progress in product understanding, they are typically employed as feature extractors that implicitly encode product information into global embeddings, thereby limiting their ability to capture fine-grained attributes. Therefore, we argue that leveraging the reasoning capabilities of MLLMs to explicitly model fine-grained product attributes holds significant potential. Nevertheless, achieving this goal remains non-trivial due to several key challenges: (i) long-context reasoning tends to dilute the model's attention to salient information in the raw input; (ii) supervised fine-tuning (SFT) primarily encourages rigid imitation, limiting the exploration of effective reasoning strategies; and (iii) fine-grained details are progressively attenuated during forward propagation. To address these issues, we propose MOON3.0, the first reasoning-aware MLLM-based model for product representation learning. Our method (1) employs a multi-head modality fusion module to adaptively integrate raw signals; (2) incorporates a joint contrastive and reinforcement learning framework to autonomously explore more effective reasoning strategies; and (3) introduces a fine-grained residual enhancement module to progressively preserve local details throughout the network. Additionally, we release a large-scale multimodal e-commerce benchmark MBE3.0. Experimentally, our model demonstrates state-of-the-art zero-shot performance across various downstream tasks on both our benchmark and public datasets.

随着电子商务的快速发展，探索通用表征而非任务特定表征日益受到关注。尽管近期多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在商品理解领域取得显著进展，但它们通常被用作特征提取器，将商品信息隐式编码为全局嵌入，从而限制了捕捉细粒度属性的能力。因此，我们认为利用MLLMs的推理能力显式建模细粒度商品属性具有重要潜力。然而，实现这一目标仍面临关键挑战：（i）长上下文推理易稀释模型对原始输入显著信息的注意力；（ii）监督微调（SFT）主要鼓励机械模仿，限制了有效推理策略的探索；（iii）细粒度细节在前向传播过程中逐渐衰减。为解决这些问题，我们提出MOON3.0——首个基于MLLM的推理感知商品表征学习模型。我们的方法（1）采用多头模态融合模块自适应整合原始信号；（2）结合联合对比与强化学习框架自主探索更有效的推理策略；（3）引入细粒度残差增强模块在网络中渐进式保留局部细节。此外，我们发布了大规模多模态电商基准MBE3.0。实验表明，该模型在我们的基准及公共数据集上，跨多种下游任务均实现了最先进的零样本性能。
