The method addresses key challenges by adaptively integrating raw signals via a multi-head modality fusion module, exploring effective reasoning strategies through a joint contrastive and reinforcement learning framework, and preserving local details with a fine-grained residual enhancement module. Main experimental results show that the model achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot performance across various downstream tasks on both the newly released MBE3.0 benchmark and public datasets.
本文的动机源于电子商务领域对通用产品表征的需求，以及当前多模态大语言模型作为隐式特征提取器在捕捉细粒度属性方面的局限性。为此，作者提出了MOON3.0，一个用于产品表征学习的推理感知多模态大语言模型。该方法通过多头模态融合模块自适应整合原始信号，利用联合对比与强化学习框架自主探索更有效的推理策略，并引入细粒度残差增强模块在网络中逐步保留局部细节，以解决关键挑战。主要实验结果表明，该模型在新发布的大规模多模态基准MBE3.0以及公共数据集上的多种下游任务中，均实现了最先进的零样本性能。
Generalized Heavy-tailed Mutation for Evolutionary Algorithms
Authors: Anton V. Eremeev, Dmitri V. Silaev, Valentin A. Topchii
First: 2026-04-01T05:33:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T05:33:12+00:00
Comments: Presented at the international conference dedicated to mathematics in artificial intelligence (MathAI-2026). Translated from the publication in Russian: A.V. Eremeev, D.V. Silaev, and Topchii V.A. Generalized heavy-tailed mutation for evolutionary algorithms. Sibirskie Elektronnye Matematicheskie Izvestiya [Siberian Electronic Mathematical Reports], 21:940-959, 2024. DOI: 10.33048/semi.2024.21.062
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The heavy-tailed mutation operator, proposed by Doerr, Le, Makhmara, and Nguyen (2017) for evolutionary algorithms, is based on the power-law assumption of mutation rate distribution. Here we generalize the power-law assumption using a regularly varying constraint on the distribution function of mutation rate. In this setting, we generalize the upper bounds on the expected optimization time of the $(1+(λ,λ))$ genetic algorithm obtained by Antipov, Buzdalov and Doerr (2022) for the OneMax function class parametrized by the problem dimension $n$. In particular, it is shown that, on this function class, the sufficient conditions of Antipov, Buzdalov and Doerr (2022) on the heavy-tailed mutation, ensuring the $O(n)$ optimization time in expectation, may be generalized as well. This optimization time is known to be asymptotically smaller than what can be achieved by the $(1+(λ,λ))$ genetic algorithm with any static mutation rate. A new version of the heavy-tailed mutation operator is proposed, satisfying the generalized conditions, and promising results of computational experiments are presented.
中文标题/摘要
标题：进化算法的广义重尾变异算子
重尾变异算子由Doerr、Le、Makhmara和Nguyen（2017）提出，其基于变异率分布的幂律假设。本文通过对变异率分布函数施加正则变化约束，推广了该幂律假设。在此框架下，我们推广了Antipov、Buzdalov和Doerr（2022）针对以问题维度n参数化的OneMax函数类所得到的$(1+(λ,λ))$遗传算法期望优化时间上界。特别地，研究表明在该函数类上，Antipov等人（2022）提出的保证期望$O(n)$优化时间的重尾变异充分条件亦可被推广。该优化时间已知渐近小于采用任意静态变异率的$(1+(λ,λ))$遗传算法所能达到的最优值。本文提出了一种满足广义条件的新版重尾变异算子，并展示了具有前景的计算实验结果。
Summary / 总结
This paper aims to generalize the theoretical foundation of the heavy-tailed mutation operator in evolutionary algorithms, moving beyond the original power-law assumption to a broader class of distributions defined by regular variation. The method involves analyzing the (1+(λ,λ)) genetic algorithm on the OneMax function, deriving generalized sufficient conditions on the mutation rate distribution to achieve a linear expected optimization time of O(n). The main experimental results confirm that the proposed generalized heavy-tailed mutation operator satisfies these conditions and demonstrates promising performance, theoretically outperforming algorithms using any static mutation rate.

A Reasoning-Enabled Vision-Language Foundation Model for Chest X-ray Interpretation
Authors: Yabin Zhang, Chong Wang, Yunhe Gao, Jiaming Liu, Maya Varma, Justin Xu, Sophie Ostmeier, Jin Long, Sergios Gatidis, Seena Dehkharghani, Arne Michalson, Eun Kyoung Hong, Christian Bluethgen, Haiwei Henry Guo, Alexander Victor Ortiz, Stephan Altmayer, Sandhya Bodapati, Joseph David Janizek, Ken Chang, Jean-Benoit Delbrouck, Akshay S. Chaudhari, Curtis P. Langlotz
First: 2026-04-01T05:19:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T05:19:09+00:00
Comments: Codes: https://github.com/YBZh/CheXOne Models: https://huggingface.co/StanfordAIMI/CheXOne
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Chest X-rays (CXRs) are among the most frequently performed imaging examinations worldwide, yet rising imaging volumes increase radiologist workload and the risk of diagnostic errors. Although artificial intelligence (AI) systems have shown promise for CXR interpretation, most generate only final predictions, without making explicit how visual evidence is translated into radiographic findings and diagnostic predictions. We present CheXOne, a reasoning-enabled vision-language model for CXR interpretation. CheXOne jointly generates diagnostic predictions and explicit, clinically grounded reasoning traces that connect visual evidence, radiographic findings, and these predictions. The model is trained on 14.7 million instruction and reasoning samples curated from 30 public datasets spanning 36 CXR interpretation tasks, using a two-stage framework that combines instruction tuning with reinforcement learning to improve reasoning quality. We evaluate CheXOne in zero-shot settings across visual question answering, report generation, visual grounding and reasoning assessment, covering 17 evaluation settings. CheXOne outperforms existing medical and general-domain foundation models and achieves strong performance on independent public benchmarks. A clinical reader study demonstrates that CheXOne-drafted reports are comparable to or better than resident-written reports in 55% of cases, while effectively addressing clinical indications and enhancing both report writing and CXR interpretation efficiency. Further analyses involving radiologists reveal that the generated reasoning traces show high clinical factuality and provide causal support for the final predictions, offering a plausible explanation for the performance gains. These results suggest that explicit reasoning can improve model performance, interpretability and clinical utility in AI-assisted CXR interpretation.

本研究旨在减轻放射科医生的工作负担并减少胸片诊断错误，提出了CheXOne这一能够生成诊断预测及明确推理轨迹的视觉语言模型。该方法采用两阶段训练框架，结合指令微调和强化学习，基于30个公共数据集的1470万样本进行训练。实验结果表明，CheXOne在17个零样本评估设置中优于现有模型，临床阅读研究显示其生成的报告在55%的情况下达到或超过住院医师报告水平，同时提升了效率并提供了临床事实性强的推理支持。
Analysis of On-policy Policy Gradient Methods under the Distribution Mismatch
Authors: Weizhen Wang, Jianping He, Xiaoming Duan
First: 2025-03-28T08:52:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T04:30:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Policy gradient methods are one of the most successful approaches for solving challenging reinforcement learning problems. Despite their empirical successes, many state-of-the-art policy gradient algorithms for discounted problems deviate from the theoretical policy gradient theorem due to the existence of a distribution mismatch. In this work, we analyze the impact of this mismatch on policy gradient methods. Specifically, we first show that in the case of tabular parameterizations, the biased gradient induced by the mismatch still yields a valid first-order characterization of global optimality. Then, we extend this analysis to more general parameterizations by deriving explicit bounds on both the state distribution mismatch and the resulting gradient mismatch in episodic and continuing MDPs, which are shown to vanish at least linearly as the discount factor approaches one. Building on these bounds, we further establish guarantees for the biased policy gradient iterates, showing that they approach approximate stationary points with respect to the exact gradient, with asymptotic residuals depending on the discount factor. Our findings offer insights into the robustness of policy gradient methods as well as the gap between theoretical foundations and practical implementations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布失配下同策略策略梯度方法分析
策略梯度方法是解决复杂强化学习问题最成功的途径之一。尽管经验上取得了成功，但由于分布失配的存在，许多针对折扣问题的最先进策略梯度算法偏离了理论上的策略梯度定理。本研究分析了这种失配对策略梯度方法的影响。具体而言，我们首先证明在表格化参数化情况下，由失配引起的偏置梯度仍能有效表征全局最优性的一阶特性。随后，我们将分析扩展到更一般的参数化情形，通过推导片段式和持续性马尔可夫决策过程中状态分布失配及梯度失配的显式边界，证明这些边界在折扣因子趋近于一时至少以线性速度收敛至零。基于这些边界，我们进一步建立了偏置策略梯度迭代的收敛保证，证明其能逼近精确梯度意义下的近似驻点，且渐近残差取决于折扣因子。本研究为理解策略梯度方法的鲁棒性以及理论基础与实际实现之间的差距提供了新的视角。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the robustness of policy gradient methods in reinforcement learning when a distribution mismatch exists between the state visitation distribution used for gradient estimation and the true discounted state distribution, a common deviation in practical algorithms. The method involves a theoretical analysis showing that, for tabular parameterizations, the biased gradient still provides a valid first-order optimality condition, and it extends to general parameterizations by deriving explicit bounds on the distribution and gradient mismatch in both episodic and continuing MDPs, which vanish linearly as the discount factor approaches one. The main experimental results, derived analytically, demonstrate that the biased policy gradient iterates converge to approximate stationary points relative to the exact gradient, with asymptotic residuals controlled by the discount factor, offering insights into the gap between theory and practice.
本文研究了强化学习中策略梯度方法在存在分布不匹配时的鲁棒性，这种不匹配指梯度估计使用的状态访问分布与真实折扣状态分布之间的偏差，这是实际算法中的常见现象。方法上，通过理论分析表明，在表格化参数化下，有偏梯度仍能提供有效的一阶最优性条件，并扩展到一般参数化，推导了在回合式和持续MDP中分布不匹配和梯度不匹配的显式边界，这些边界随折扣因子趋近于一而线性消失。主要实验结果通过分析得出，显示有偏策略梯度迭代会收敛到相对于精确梯度的近似驻点，其渐近残差由折扣因子控制，从而为理论与实践之间的差距提供了见解。
FIRE: Frobenius-Isometry Reinitialization for Balancing the Stability-Plasticity Tradeoff
Authors: Isaac Han, Sangyeon Park, Seungwon Oh, Donghu Kim, Hojoon Lee, Kyung-Joong Kim
Venue: ICLR oral
First: 2026-02-08T16:17:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T04:00:21+00:00
Comments: ICLR'26 (oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep neural networks trained on nonstationary data must balance stability (i.e., retaining prior knowledge) and plasticity (i.e., adapting to new tasks). Standard reinitialization methods, which reinitialize weights toward their original values, are widely used but difficult to tune: conservative reinitializations fail to restore plasticity, while aggressive ones erase useful knowledge. We propose FIRE, a principled reinitialization method that explicitly balances the stability-plasticity tradeoff. FIRE quantifies stability through Squared Frobenius Error (SFE), measuring proximity to past weights, and plasticity through Deviation from Isometry (DfI), reflecting weight isotropy. The reinitialization point is obtained by solving a constrained optimization problem, minimizing SFE subject to DfI being zero, which is efficiently approximated by Newton-Schulz iteration. FIRE is evaluated on continual visual learning (CIFAR-10 with ResNet-18), language modeling (OpenWebText with GPT-0.1B), and reinforcement learning (HumanoidBench with SAC and Atari games with DQN). Across all domains, FIRE consistently outperforms both naive training without intervention and standard reinitialization methods, demonstrating effective balancing of the stability-plasticity tradeoff.

标题：FIRE：基于Frobenius等距重初始化的稳定性-可塑性权衡平衡方法

The paper addresses the challenge of balancing stability and plasticity in deep neural networks trained on nonstationary data, where standard reinitialization methods are difficult to tune effectively. The authors propose FIRE, a method that quantifies stability via Squared Frobenius Error and plasticity via Deviation from Isometry, then solves a constrained optimization problem to find a reinitialization point that minimizes stability loss while ensuring plasticity. Execution-Verified Reinforcement Learning for Optimization Modeling
Authors: Runda Guan, Xiangqing Shen, Jiajun Zhang, Yifan Zhang, Jian Cheng, Rui Xia
First: 2026-04-01T03:39:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T03:39:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automating optimization modeling with LLMs is a promising path toward scalable decision intelligence, but existing approaches either rely on agentic pipelines built on closed-source LLMs with high inference latency, or fine-tune smaller LLMs using costly process supervision that often overfits to a single solver API. Inspired by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, we propose Execution-Verified Optimization Modeling (EVOM), an execution-verified learning framework that treats a mathematical programming solver as a deterministic, interactive verifier. Given a natural-language problem and a target solver, EVOM generates solver-specific code, executes it in a sandboxed harness, and converts execution outcomes into scalar rewards, optimized with GRPO and DAPO in a closed-loop generate-execute-feedback-update process. This outcome-only formulation removes the need for process-level supervision, and enables cross-solver generalization by switching the verification environment rather than reconstructing solver-specific datasets. Experiments on NL4OPT, MAMO, IndustryOR, and OptiBench across Gurobi, OR-Tools, and COPT show that EVOM matches or outperforms process-supervised SFT, supports zero-shot solver transfer, and achieves effective low-cost solver adaptation by continuing training under the target solver backend.

标题：面向优化建模的执行验证强化学习
利用大语言模型自动化优化建模是实现可扩展决策智能的重要途径，但现有方法要么依赖基于闭源大语言模型的高延迟推理智能体流程，要么采用成本高昂的过程监督微调较小模型，且常过度适配单一求解器接口。受可验证奖励的强化学习启发，我们提出执行验证优化建模框架，将数学规划求解器视为确定性交互验证器。该框架针对自然语言问题与目标求解器生成专用代码，在沙箱环境中执行，并将执行结果转化为标量奖励，通过GRPO与DAPO算法在生成-执行-反馈-更新的闭环流程中进行优化。这种仅依赖结果的范式无需过程级监督，通过切换验证环境而非重建求解器专用数据集，实现了跨求解器泛化能力。在NL4OPT、MAMO、IndustryOR和OptiBench数据集上，针对Gurobi、OR-Tools和COPT求解器的实验表明：该框架性能匹配或超越过程监督监督微调方法，支持零样本求解器迁移，并能通过目标求解器后端持续训练实现高效低成本适配。

The paper addresses the challenge of automating optimization modeling with large language models (LLMs), where existing methods either depend on slow, closed-source LLMs or require costly process supervision that limits solver generalization. To overcome this, the authors propose Execution-Verified Optimization Modeling (EVOM), a reinforcement learning framework that uses a mathematical programming solver as a verifier: it generates solver-specific code from natural-language problems, executes it in a sandbox, and converts execution outcomes into rewards for optimization via GRPO and DAPO in a closed-loop process. Internal State-Based Policy Gradient Methods for Partially Observable Markov Potential Games
Authors: Wonseok Yang, Thinh T. Doan
First: 2026-04-01T03:25:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T03:25:21+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 2 figures. Submitted to IEEE Control Systems Letters (L-CSS) with CDC option
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This letter studies multi-agent reinforcement learning in partially observable Markov potential games. Solving this problem is challenging due to partial observability, decentralized information, and the curse of dimensionality. First, to address the first two challenges, we leverage the common information framework, which allows agents to act based on both shared and local information. Second, to ensure tractability, we study an internal state that compresses accumulated information, preventing it from growing unboundedly over time. We then implement an internal state-based natural policy gradient method to find Nash equilibria of the Markov potential game. Our main contribution is to establish a non-asymptotic convergence bound for this method. Our theoretical bound decomposes into two interpretable components: a statistical error term that also arises in standard Markov potential games, and an approximation error capturing the use of finite-state controllers. Finally, simulations across multiple partially observable environments demonstrate that the proposed method using finite-state controllers achieves consistent improvements in performance compared to the setting where only the current observation is used.

标题：基于内部状态的部分可观测马尔可夫势博弈策略梯度方法

This paper addresses the challenge of multi-agent reinforcement learning in partially observable Markov potential games, where agents face difficulties due to partial observability, decentralized information, and high dimensionality. They implement an internal state-based natural policy gradient method to find Nash equilibria, establishing a non-asymptotic convergence bound that decomposes into a statistical error term and an approximation error from using finite-state controllers. Experimental simulations across various partially observable environments show that the proposed method with finite-state controllers consistently outperforms approaches relying solely on current observations.

ARCS: Autoregressive Circuit Synthesis with Topology-Aware Graph Attention and Spec Conditioning
Authors: Tushar Dhananjay Pathak
First: 2026-03-30T23:14:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T02:40:31+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 6 figures, 11 tables. Code available at https://github.com/tusharpathaknyu/ARCS
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This paper presents ARCS (Autoregressive Circuit Synthesis), a system for amortized analog circuit generation that produces complete, SPICE-simulatable designs (topology and component values) in milliseconds rather than the minutes required by search-based methods. A hybrid pipeline combining two learned generators (a graph VAE and a flow-matching model) with SPICE-based ranking achieves 99.9% simulation validity (reward 6.43/8.0) across 32 topologies using only 8 SPICE evaluations, 40x fewer than genetic algorithms. For single-model inference, a topology-aware Graph Transformer with Best-of-3 candidate selection reaches 85% simulation validity in 97ms, over 600x faster than random search. The key technical contribution adapts Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to multi-topology circuit reinforcement learning, resolving a critical failure mode of REINFORCE (cross-topology reward distribution mismatch) through per-topology advantage normalization. This improves simulation validity by +9.6 percentage points over REINFORCE in only 500 RL steps (10x fewer). Grammar-constrained decoding additionally guarantees 100% structural validity by construction via topology-aware token masking.

GUIDE: Reinforcement Learning for Behavioral Action Support in Type 1 Diabetes
Authors: Saman Khamesian, Sri Harini Balaji, Di Yang Shi, Stephanie M. Carpenter, Daniel E. Rivera, W. Bradley Knox, Peter Stone, Hassan Ghasemzadeh
First: 2026-04-01T02:14:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T02:14:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Type 1 Diabetes (T1D) management requires continuous adjustment of insulin and lifestyle behaviors to maintain blood glucose within a safe target range. Although automated insulin delivery (AID) systems have improved glycemic outcomes, many patients still fail to achieve recommended clinical targets, warranting new approaches to improve glucose control in patients with T1D. While reinforcement learning (RL) has been utilized as a promising approach, current RL-based methods focus primarily on insulin-only treatment and do not provide behavioral recommendations for glucose control. To address this gap, we propose GUIDE, an RL-based decision-support framework designed to complement AID technologies by providing behavioral recommendations to prevent abnormal glucose events. GUIDE generates structured actions defined by intervention type, magnitude, and timing, including bolus insulin administration and carbohydrate intake events. GUIDE integrates a patient-specific glucose level predictor trained on real-world continuous glucose monitoring data and supports both offline and online RL algorithms within a unified environment. We evaluate both off-policy and on-policy methods across 25 individuals with T1D using standardized glycemic metrics. Among the evaluated approaches, the CQL-BC algorithm demonstrates the highest average time-in-range, reaching 85.49% while maintaining low hypoglycemia exposures. Behavioral similarity analysis further indicates that the learned CQL-BC policy preserves key structural characteristics of patient action patterns, achieving a mean cosine similarity of 0.87 $\pm$ 0.09 across subjects. These findings suggest that conservative offline RL with a structured behavioral action space can provide clinically meaningful and behaviorally plausible decision support for personalized diabetes management.

Fundamental Limits of Man-in-the-Middle Attack Detection in Model-Free Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Rishi Rani, Massimo Franceschetti
First: 2026-03-29T09:18:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T02:10:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider the problem of learning-based man-in-the-middle (MITM) attacks in cyber-physical systems (CPS), and extend our previously proposed Bellman Deviation Detection (BDD) framework for model-free reinforcement learning (RL). We refine the standard MDP attack model by allowing the reward function to depend on both the current and subsequent states, thereby capturing reward variations induced by errors in the adversary's transition estimate. We also derive an optimal system-identification strategy for the adversary that minimizes detectable value deviations. Further, we prove that the agent's asymptotic learning time required to secure the system scales linearly with the adversary's learning time, and that this matches the optimal lower bound. Hence, the proposed detection scheme is order-optimal in detection efficiency. Finally, we extend the framework to asynchronous and intermittent attack scenarios, where reliable detection is preserved.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无模型强化学习中中间人攻击检测的基本极限
本文研究信息物理系统中基于学习的中间人攻击问题，将先前提出的贝尔曼偏差检测框架扩展至无模型强化学习场景。我们改进了标准马尔可夫决策过程攻击模型，允许奖励函数同时依赖当前状态与后续状态，从而捕捉因攻击者转移概率估计误差引发的奖励变化。同时推导出攻击者最小化可检测价值偏差的最优系统辨识策略。进一步证明：智能体保障系统安全所需的渐近学习时间与攻击者学习时间呈线性关系，且该关系达到理论最优下界，故所提检测方案在检测效率上具备阶次最优性。最后将框架扩展至异步与间歇攻击场景，仍能保持可靠检测能力。

This paper addresses the challenge of detecting man-in-the-middle (MITM) attacks in cyber-physical systems using model-free reinforcement learning, motivated by the need to secure learning-based control against adversaries. The method extends a Bellman Deviation Detection framework by refining the attack model to include reward dependencies on consecutive states and deriving an optimal adversary strategy that minimizes detectable value deviations. Experimental results show that the agent's required learning time scales linearly with the adversary's, matching an optimal lower bound, and the framework maintains reliable detection even in asynchronous and intermittent attack scenarios, proving its order-optimal efficiency.
本文针对网络物理系统中基于学习的中间人攻击检测问题，旨在保护强化学习控制免受对手威胁。方法上扩展了贝尔曼偏差检测框架，通过改进攻击模型以包含奖励对连续状态的依赖，并推导出最小化可检测值偏差的最优对手策略。实验结果表明，智能体所需的学习时间与对手的学习时间呈线性比例，达到了最优下界，且该框架在异步和间歇攻击场景下仍能保持可靠检测，证明了其检测效率的阶次最优性。
Autonomous Adaptive Solver Selection for Chemistry Integration via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Eloghosa Ikponmwoba, Opeoluwa Owoyele
First: 2026-03-31T21:44:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T21:44:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The computational cost of stiff chemical kinetics remains a dominant bottleneck in reacting-flow simulation, yet hybrid integration strategies are typically driven by hand-tuned heuristics or supervised predictors that make myopic decisions from instantaneous local state. We introduce a constrained reinforcement learning (RL) framework that autonomously selects between an implicit BDF integrator (CVODE) and a quasi-steady-state (QSS) solver during chemistry integration. Solver selection is cast as a Markov decision process. The agent learns trajectory-aware policies that account for how present solver choices influence downstream error accumulation, while minimizing computational cost under a user-prescribed accuracy tolerance enforced through a Lagrangian reward with online multiplier adaptation. Across sampled 0D homogeneous reactor conditions, the RL-adaptive policy achieves a mean speedup of approximately $3\times$, with speedups ranging from $1.11\times$ to $10.58\times$, while maintaining accurate ignition delays and species profiles for a 106-species \textit{n}-dodecane mechanism and adding approximately $1\%$ inference overhead. Without retraining, the 0D-trained policy transfers to 1D counterflow diffusion flames over strain rates $10$--$2000~\mathrm{s}^{-1}$, delivering consistent $\approx 2.2\times$ speedup relative to CVODE while preserving near-reference temperature accuracy and selecting CVODE at only $12$--$15\%$ of space-time points. Overall, the results demonstrate the potential of the proposed reinforcement learning framework to learn problem-specific integration strategies while respecting accuracy constraints, thereby opening a pathway toward adaptive, self-optimizing workflows for multiphysics systems with spatially heterogeneous stiffness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的化学积分自主自适应求解器选择方法
刚性化学动力学的计算成本始终是反应流模拟的主要瓶颈，而混合积分策略通常依赖人工调优的启发式方法或基于瞬时局部状态做出短视决策的监督预测器。本文提出一种约束强化学习框架，能在化学积分过程中自主选择隐式BDF积分器（CVODE）与准稳态求解器。求解器选择被构建为马尔可夫决策过程，智能体学习具有轨迹感知能力的策略，既能考虑当前求解器选择对下游误差累积的影响，又能在用户指定的精度容差（通过带在线乘子自适应调整的拉格朗日奖励函数实现）约束下最小化计算成本。在采样的0维均相反应器工况中，强化学习自适应策略实现了约3倍的平均加速（加速范围1.11-10.58倍），同时为106组分正十二烷机理保持了准确的点火延迟与组分分布，仅增加约1%的推理开销。未经重新训练，该0维训练策略可迁移至应变率10-2000 s⁻¹的1维对冲扩散火焰，在保持接近参考温度精度的前提下，相对CVODE实现约2.2倍的稳定加速，且仅在12-15%的时空点选择CVODE求解器。总体而言，该研究证明了所提强化学习框架在遵循精度约束条件下学习特定问题积分策略的潜力，为具有空间异构刚度的多物理场系统开辟了自适应自优化工作流程的新途径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost of stiff chemical kinetics in reacting-flow simulations, which are typically limited by hand-tuned or myopic supervised solvers, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning (RL) framework to autonomously select between an implicit BDF integrator and a quasi-steady-state solver during chemistry integration. The method formulates solver selection as a constrained Markov decision process, where an agent learns trajectory-aware policies that minimize computational cost while enforcing a user-prescribed accuracy tolerance via a Lagrangian reward with online multiplier adaptation. Experimental results on a 106-species n-dodecane mechanism in 0D homogeneous reactors show the RL policy achieves a mean speedup of approximately 3× (ranging from 1.11× to 10.58×) with accurate ignition delays and minimal inference overhead, and without retraining, it transfers to 1D counterflow flames, delivering about 2.2× speedup while preserving temperature accuracy and using the expensive solver at only 12–15% of points.
针对反应流模拟中刚性化学动力学计算成本高昂且现有混合积分策略依赖人工启发式或短视监督预测器的问题，本文提出了一种强化学习框架，用于在化学积分过程中自主选择隐式BDF积分器或准稳态求解器。该方法将求解器选择构建为约束马尔可夫决策过程，智能体学习轨迹感知策略，通过带有在线乘子适应的拉格朗日奖励，在满足用户指定精度容限的前提下最小化计算成本。在106物种正十二烷机理的0D均相反应器实验中，强化学习策略实现了约3倍的平均加速（范围1.11–10.58倍），并准确保持了点火延迟和物种分布，推理开销仅约1%；未经重新训练，该策略可迁移至1D对冲扩散火焰，在不同应变率下保持约2.2倍加速，温度精度接近参考解，且仅在12–15%的时空点上调用昂贵求解器。
REM-CTX: Automated Peer Review via Reinforcement Learning with Auxiliary Context
Authors: Pawin Taechoyotin, Daniel E. Acuna
First: 2026-03-31T21:19:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T21:19:05+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Most automated peer review systems rely on textual manuscript content alone, leaving visual elements such as figures and external scholarly signals underutilized. We introduce REM-CTX, a reinforcement-learning system that incorporates auxiliary context into the review generation process via correspondence-aware reward functions. REM-CTX trains an 8B-parameter language model with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) and combines a multi-aspect quality reward with two correspondence rewards that explicitly encourage alignment with auxiliary context. Experiments on manuscripts across Computer, Biological, and Physical Sciences show that REM-CTX achieves the highest overall review quality among six baselines, outperforming other systems with substantially larger commercial models, and surpassing the next-best RL baseline across both quality and contextual grounding metrics. Ablation studies confirm that the two correspondence rewards are complementary: each selectively improves its targeted correspondence reward while preserving all quality dimensions, and the full model outperforms all partial variants. Analysis of training dynamics reveals that the criticism aspect is negatively correlated with other metrics during training, suggesting that future studies should group multi-dimension rewards for review generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：REM-CTX：基于强化学习与辅助上下文的自动化同行评审系统
现有自动化同行评审系统大多仅依赖稿件文本内容，未能充分利用图表等视觉元素及外部学术信号。本文提出REM-CTX系统，通过相关性感知奖励函数将辅助上下文融入评审生成过程。该系统采用组相对策略优化（GRPO）训练80亿参数语言模型，结合多维度质量奖励与两项显式促进辅助上下文对齐的相关性奖励。在计算机、生物和物理科学领域的稿件实验中，REM-CTX在六种基线方法中获得最高综合评审质量，其表现超越采用更大规模商业模型的系统，并在质量与上下文锚定指标上均优于次优强化学习基线。消融实验证实两项相关性奖励具有互补性：各自能针对性提升目标相关性指标且保持所有质量维度，完整模型优于所有部分变体。训练动态分析显示批评维度与其他指标呈负相关，表明未来研究应将多维度奖励分组处理以优化评审生成。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that most automated peer review systems primarily use textual manuscript content, neglecting visual elements like figures and external scholarly signals. The method introduces REM-CTX, a reinforcement learning system that incorporates auxiliary context via correspondence-aware reward functions, training an 8B-parameter language model with Group Relative Policy Optimization and combining multi-aspect quality rewards with two correspondence rewards to align with context. Offline Constrained RLHF with Multiple Preference Oracles
Authors: Brenden Latham, Mehrdad Moharrami
First: 2026-03-31T20:06:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T20:06:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study offline constrained reinforcement learning from human feedback with multiple preference oracles. Motivated by applications that trade off performance with safety or fairness, we aim to maximize target population utility subject to a minimum protected group welfare constraint. From pairwise comparisons collected under a reference policy, we estimate oracle-specific rewards via maximum likelihood and analyze how statistical uncertainty propagates through the dual program. We cast the constrained objective as a KL-regularized Lagrangian whose primal optimizer is a Gibbs policy, reducing learning to a convex dual problem. We propose a dual-only algorithm that ensures high-probability constraint satisfaction and provide the first finite-sample performance guarantees for offline constrained preference learning. Finally, we extend our theoretical analysis to accommodate multiple constraints and general f-divergence regularization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于多偏好神谕的离线约束RLHF研究
本研究探讨了基于多偏好神谕的离线约束人类反馈强化学习。针对需权衡性能与安全性或公平性的应用场景，我们的目标是在满足受保护群体最低福利约束的前提下，最大化目标群体效用。通过参考策略下收集的成对比较数据，我们采用极大似然法估计各神谕特定奖励，并分析统计不确定性在二元规划中的传播机制。我们将约束目标构建为KL正则化的拉格朗日函数，其原始优化器为吉布斯策略，从而将学习问题简化为凸对偶问题。提出了一种仅需对偶操作的算法，确保高概率约束满足，并为离线约束偏好学习提供了首个有限样本性能保证。最后，我们将理论分析扩展至多约束场景及广义f-散度正则化框架。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by applications requiring trade-offs between performance and safety or fairness, this paper studies offline constrained reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) with multiple preference orcles. The method aims to maximize a target utility subject to a minimum protected group welfare constraint, using pairwise comparisons from a reference policy to estimate oracle-specific rewards via maximum likelihood and analyzing statistical uncertainty in a dual program. The constrained objective is formulated as a KL-regularized Lagrangian, whose primal optimizer is a Gibbs policy, reducing learning to a convex dual problem; a dual-only algorithm is proposed to ensure high-probability constraint satisfaction. The main experimental results provide the first finite-sample performance guarantees for offline constrained preference learning, with theoretical extensions to multiple constraints and general f-divergence regularization.

Finite-Time Analysis of Projected Two-Time-Scale Stochastic Approximation
Authors: Yitao Bai, Thinh T. Doan, Justin Romberg
First: 2026-03-31T19:30:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T19:30:36+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the finite-time convergence of projected linear two-time-scale stochastic approximation with constant step sizes and Polyak--Ruppert averaging. We establish an explicit mean-square error bound, decomposing it into two interpretable components, an approximation error determined by the constrained subspace and a statistical error decaying at a sublinear rate, with constants expressed through restricted stability margins and a coupling invertibility condition. These constants cleanly separate the effect of subspace choice (approximation errors) from the effect of the averaging horizon (statistical errors). We illustrate our theoretical results through a number of numerical experiments on both synthetic and reinforcement learning problems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：投影双时间尺度随机逼近的有限时间分析
我们研究了具有恒定步长和Polyak–Ruppert平均的投影线性双时间尺度随机逼近的有限时间收敛性。我们建立了一个显式的均方误差界，将其分解为两个可解释的分量：一个由约束子空间决定的近似误差，以及一个以次线性速率衰减的统计误差，其中常数通过受限稳定裕度和耦合可逆性条件表示。这些常数清晰地将子空间选择（近似误差）的影响与平均时域（统计误差）的影响分离开来。我们通过在合成数据和强化学习问题上的若干数值实验，阐释了理论结果。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to understand the finite-time convergence behavior of two-time-scale stochastic approximation algorithms, which are widely used in reinforcement learning and other areas but whose theoretical guarantees are often asymptotic. The method involves analyzing a projected linear two-time-scale stochastic approximation with constant step sizes and Polyak-Ruppert averaging, establishing an explicit mean-square error bound that decomposes into an approximation error from the constrained subspace and a statistical error decaying sublinearly, with constants expressed via restricted stability margins and a coupling invertibility condition. The main experimental results, illustrated through numerical experiments on synthetic and reinforcement learning problems, demonstrate that the derived bounds effectively separate the effects of subspace choice from the averaging horizon, validating the theoretical analysis.
本文的动机源于需要理解双时间尺度随机逼近算法的有限时间收敛行为，这类算法在强化学习等领域广泛应用，但其理论保证通常是渐近的。研究方法分析了采用恒定步长和Polyak-Ruppert平均的投影线性双时间尺度随机逼近，建立了一个显式的均方误差界，将其分解为由约束子空间决定的近似误差和以次线性速率衰减的统计误差，常数通过受限稳定裕度和耦合可逆条件表示。主要实验结果通过合成数据和强化学习问题的数值实验展示，表明推导的误差界有效分离了子空间选择与平均时长的影响，验证了理论分析。
Polychromic Objectives for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jubayer Ibn Hamid, Ifdita Hasan Orney, Ellen Xu, Chelsea Finn, Dorsa Sadigh
First: 2025-09-29T19:32:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T18:26:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning fine-tuning (RLFT) is a dominant paradigm for improving pretrained policies for downstream tasks. These pretrained policies, trained on large datasets, produce generations with a broad range of promising but unrefined behaviors. Often, a critical failure mode of RLFT arises when policies lose this diversity and collapse into a handful of easily exploitable outputs. This convergence hinders exploration, which is essential for expanding the capabilities of the pretrained policy and for amplifying the benefits of test-time compute scaling. To address this, we introduce an objective for policy gradient methods that explicitly enforces the exploration and refinement of diverse generations, which we call a polychromic objective. We then show how proximal policy optimization (PPO) can be adapted to optimize this objective. Our method (1) employs vine sampling to collect on-policy rollouts and (2) modifies the advantage function to reflect the advantage under our new objective. Experiments on BabyAI, Minigrid, and Algorithmic Creativity show that our method improves success rates by reliably solving a larger set of environment configurations and generalizes better under large perturbations. Moreover, when given multiple attempts in pass@$k$ experiments, the policy achieves substantially higher coverage, demonstrating its ability to maintain and exploit a diverse repertoire of strategies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习的多色目标
强化学习微调（RLFT）是改进下游任务预训练策略的主导范式。这些基于大规模数据集训练的预训练策略能生成广泛但未经优化的行为。RLFT的一个关键失败模式常出现在策略失去多样性、坍缩为少数易被利用的输出时，这种收敛阻碍了探索——这对扩展预训练策略能力及放大测试时计算扩展的效益至关重要。为此，我们提出一种策略梯度方法目标，明确强制对多样化生成进行探索与优化，称为多色目标。我们随后展示如何调整近端策略优化（PPO）以优化此目标。我们的方法（1）采用藤蔓采样收集同策略轨迹，（2）修改优势函数以反映新目标下的优势。在BabyAI、Minigrid和算法创造力上的实验表明，该方法通过可靠解决更多环境配置提升成功率，并在强扰动下表现更优泛化能力。此外，在pass@$k$实验中给予多次尝试时，策略实现了显著更高的覆盖率，证明其保持并利用多样化策略库的能力。

Hybrid Framework for Robotic Manipulation: Integrating Reinforcement Learning and Large Language Models
Authors: Md Saad, Sajjad Hussain, Mohd Suhaib
First: 2026-03-31T17:19:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T17:19:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces a new hybrid framework that combines Reinforcement Learning (RL) and Large Language Models (LLMs) to improve robotic manipulation tasks. By utilizing RL for accurate low-level control and LLMs for high level task planning and understanding of natural language, the proposed framework effectively connects low-level execution with high-level reasoning in robotic systems. This integration allows robots to understand and carry out complex, human-like instructions while adapting to changing environments in real time. The framework is tested in a PyBullet-based simulation environment using the Franka Emika Panda robotic arm, with various manipulation scenarios as benchmarks. The results show a 33.5% decrease in task completion time and enhancements of 18.1% and 36.4% in accuracy and adaptability, respectively, when compared to systems that use only RL. These results underscore the potential of LLM-enhanced robotic systems for practical applications, making them more efficient, adaptable, and capable of interacting with humans. Future research will aim to explore sim-to-real transfer, scalability, and multi-robot systems to further broaden the framework's applicability.

Motivated by the need to enhance robotic manipulation with natural language understanding and adaptive planning, this paper proposes a hybrid framework integrating Reinforcement Learning (RL) for low-level control and Large Language Models (LLMs) for high-level task planning. The method leverages RL's precision in execution and LLMs' ability to interpret complex instructions, enabling real-time adaptation in dynamic environments. Scalable AI-assisted Workflow Management for Detector Design Optimization Using Distributed Computing
Authors: Derek Anderson, Amit Bashyal, Markus Diefenthaler, Cristiano Fanelli, Wen Guan, Tanja Horn, Alex Jentsch Meifeng Lin, Tadashi Maeno, Kei Nagai, Hemalata Nayak, Connor Pecar, Karthik Suresh, Fang-Ying Tsai, Anselm Vossen, Tianle Wang, Torre Wenaus
First: 2026-03-31T17:11:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T17:11:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Production and Distributed Analysis (PanDA) system, originally developed for the ATLAS experiment at the CERN Large Hadron Collider (LHC), has evolved into a robust platform for orchestrating large-scale workflows across distributed computing resources. Coupled with its intelligent Distributed Dispatch and Scheduling (iDDS) component, PanDA supports AI/ML-driven workflows through a scalable and flexible workflow engine. We present an AI-assisted framework for detector design optimization that integrates multi-objective Bayesian optimization with the PanDA--iDDS workflow engine to coordinate iterative simulations across heterogeneous resources. The framework addresses the challenge of exploring high-dimensional parameter spaces inherent in modern detector design. We demonstrate the framework using benchmark problems and realistic studies of the ePIC and dRICH detectors for the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC). Results show improved automation, scalability, and efficiency in multi-objective optimization. This work establishes a flexible and extensible paradigm for AI-driven detector design and other computationally intensive scientific applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于分布式计算的可扩展AI辅助工作流管理在探测器设计优化中的应用
最初为欧洲核子研究中心大型强子对撞机ATLAS实验开发的分布式生产与分析系统，已发展成为跨分布式计算资源协调大规模工作流的稳健平台。结合其智能分布式调度组件，该系统通过可扩展且灵活的工作流引擎支持人工智能/机器学习驱动的工作流。 我们提出一种用于探测器设计优化的AI辅助框架，该框架将多目标贝叶斯优化与工作流引擎集成，以协调跨异构资源的迭代模拟。该框架解决了现代探测器设计中固有的高维参数空间探索难题。 我们通过电子-离子对撞机的基准问题和实际案例研究展示了该框架的应用效果。结果表明，多目标优化的自动化程度、可扩展性和效率均得到提升。本研究为AI驱动的探测器设计及其他计算密集型科学应用建立了灵活可扩展的范式。

The method leverages the scalable PanDA system, originally from ATLAS at CERN, to manage AI/ML-driven workflows for detector optimization. Phyelds: A Pythonic Framework for Aggregate Computing
Authors: Gianluca Aguzzi, Davide Domini, Nicolas Farabegoli, Mirko Viroli
First: 2026-03-31T16:57:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T16:57:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aggregate programming is a field-based coordination paradigm with over a decade of exploration and successful applications across domains including sensor networks, robotics, and IoT, with implementations in various programming languages, such as Protelis, ScaFi (Scala), and FCPP (C++). A recent research direction integrates machine learning with aggregate computing, aiming to support large-scale distributed learning and provide new abstractions for implementing learning algorithms. However, existing implementations do not target data science practitioners, who predominantly work in Python--the de facto language for data science and machine learning, with a rich and mature ecosystem. Python also offers advantages for other use cases, such as education and robotics (e.g., via ROS). To address this gap, we present Phyelds, a Python library for aggregate programming. Phyelds offers a fully featured yet lightweight implementation of the field calculus model of computation, featuring a Pythonic API and an architecture designed for seamless integration with Python's machine learning ecosystem. We describe the design and implementation of Phyelds and illustrate its versatility across domains, from well-known aggregate computing patterns to federated learning coordination and integration with a widely used multi-agent reinforcement learning simulator.
中文标题/摘要

聚合编程是一种基于场的协调范式，经过十余年探索，已在传感器网络、机器人物联网等领域成功应用，现有Protelis、ScaFi（Scala）和FCPP（C++）等多种语言实现。近期研究方向将机器学习与聚合计算结合，旨在支持大规模分布式学习并提供算法实现新抽象。然而现有实现未覆盖以Python为主要工具的数据科学从业者——Python作为数据科学与机器学习领域事实标准语言，拥有丰富成熟的生态系统，同时在教育、机器人（如ROS）等场景具备优势。为填补此空白，我们推出聚合编程Python库Phyelds。该库完整实现了轻量级场演算计算模型，提供符合Python风格的API架构，可实现与Python机器学习生态的无缝集成。本文阐述Phyelds的设计实现，并通过经典聚合计算模式、联邦学习协调及主流多智能体强化学习模拟器集成等案例，展示其跨领域适用性。

Motivated by the need to make aggregate computing accessible to data science practitioners who predominantly use Python, this paper introduces Phyelds, a Python library that implements the field calculus model with a Pythonic API designed for integration with Python's machine learning ecosystem. The method involves creating a lightweight, fully featured framework that supports seamless interoperability with tools like federated learning and multi-agent reinforcement learning simulators. Experimental results demonstrate Phyelds' versatility across domains, successfully applying it to classic aggregate computing patterns, federated learning coordination, and integration with a widely used multi-agent reinforcement learning simulator.
本文的动机是使主要使用Python的数据科学从业者能够便捷地进行聚合计算，因此提出了Phyelds，这是一个实现了场演算模型的Python库，其Pythonic API设计旨在与Python机器学习生态系统集成。方法上，该框架采用轻量级但功能完整的设计，支持与联邦学习和多智能体强化学习模拟器等工具的无缝互操作。实验结果表明，Phyelds在多个领域展现出广泛适用性，成功应用于经典聚合计算模式、联邦学习协调以及广泛使用的多智能体强化学习模拟器的集成。
Learning to Play Blackjack: A Curriculum Learning Perspective
Authors: Amirreza Alasti, Efe Erdal, Yücel Celik, Theresa Eimer
First: 2026-03-31T15:54:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T15:54:39+00:00
Comments: Accepted as an oral presentation at the International Conference on Distributed Artificial Intelligence (DAI 2025). 16 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents often struggle with efficiency and performance in complex environments. We propose a novel framework that uses a Large Language Model (LLM) to dynamically generate a curriculum over available actions, enabling the agent to incorporate each action individually. We apply this framework to the game of Blackjack, where the LLM creates a multi-stage training path that progressively introduces complex actions to a Tabular Q-Learning and a Deep Q-Network (DQN) agent. Our evaluation in a realistic 8-deck simulation over 10 independent runs demonstrates significant performance gains over standard training methods. The curriculum-based approach increases the DQN agent's average win rate from 43.97% to 47.41%, reduces the average bust rate from 32.9% to 28.0%, and accelerates the overall workflow by over 74%, with the agent's full training completing faster than the baseline's evaluation phase alone. These results validate that LLM-guided curricula can build more effective, robust, and efficient RL agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习玩二十一点：课程学习的视角

ShapE-GRPO: Shapley-Enhanced Reward Allocation for Multi-Candidate LLM Training
Authors: Rui Ai, Yu Pan, David Simchi-Levi, Chonghuan Wang
First: 2026-03-31T15:24:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T15:24:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In user-agent interaction scenarios such as recommendation, brainstorming, and code suggestion, Large Language Models (LLMs) often generate sets of candidate recommendations where the objective is to maximize the collective utility of the entire set rather than individual candidates independently. However, existing reinforcement learning post-training paradigms, such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), typically assign the same set-level scalar reward to every candidate in the set. This leads to noisy training signals where poor candidates free-ride on the high reward produced by a single strong peer, resulting in suboptimal exploration. To address this, we propose Shapley-Enhanced GRPO (ShapE-GRPO). By leveraging the permutation-invariant nature of set-level utility, we derive a Shapley-enhanced formulation from cooperative game theory to decompose set-level rewards into granular, candidate-specific signals. We show that our formulation preserves the fundamental axioms of the Shapley value while remaining computationally efficient with polynomial-time complexity. Empirically, ShapE-GRPO consistently outperforms standard GRPO across diverse datasets with accelerated convergence during training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ShapE-GRPO：基于Shapley值增强的多候选大语言模型训练奖励分配方法
在推荐、头脑风暴和代码建议等用户-智能体交互场景中，大语言模型常生成候选推荐集合，其目标在于最大化整个集合的集体效用而非单个候选的独立表现。然而，现有强化学习后训练范式（如组相对策略优化）通常为集合中所有候选分配相同的集合级标量奖励，导致训练信号存在噪声：劣质候选会因单个优质同伴产生的高奖励而“搭便车”，造成次优探索。为此，我们提出Shapley增强型GRPO方法。通过利用集合级效用的排列不变性，我们从合作博弈论中推导出Shapley增强公式，将集合级奖励分解为细粒度的候选专属信号。该公式在保持Shapley值基本公理的同时，仍具备多项式时间复杂度的计算效率。实验表明，ShapE-GRPO在多种数据集上均稳定优于标准GRPO，且训练收敛速度显著提升。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem in multi-candidate LLM training where existing methods like GRPO assign identical set-level rewards to all candidates, allowing poor candidates to benefit undeservedly from strong peers and hindering effective exploration. To solve this, the authors propose ShapE-GRPO, which uses cooperative game theory to decompose set-level utility into granular, candidate-specific rewards via a Shapley value formulation that is permutation-invariant and computationally efficient. Experimental results show that ShapE-GRPO consistently outperforms standard GRPO across various datasets and achieves faster convergence during training.
本文针对多候选大语言模型训练中现有方法如GRPO为所有候选分配相同集合级奖励所导致的问题，即较差候选会搭便车从强候选处获益，从而影响有效探索。为解决此问题，作者提出ShapE-GRPO，利用合作博弈论中的沙普利值公式，将集合级效用分解为细粒度的候选特定奖励，该公式保持置换不变性且计算高效。实验结果表明，ShapE-GRPO在多个数据集上均优于标准GRPO，并在训练中实现了更快的收敛速度。
LeLaR: The First In-Orbit Demonstration of an AI-Based Satellite Attitude Controller
Authors: Kirill Djebko, Tom Baumann, Erik Dilger, Frank Puppe, Sergio Montenegro
Venue: IEEE Access, vol. 14, 2026
First: 2025-12-22T17:00:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T15:21:43+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication in IEEE Access (DOI: 10.1109/ACCESS.2026.3678816). This is the author's version which has not been fully edited and content may change prior to final publication. 20 pages, 15 figures, 18 tables. The maneuver telemetry datasets are available in the GitHub repository under https://github.com/kdjebko/lelar-in-orbit-data
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Attitude control is essential for many satellite missions. Classical controllers, however, are time-consuming to design and sensitive to model uncertainties and variations in operational boundary conditions. Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) offers a promising alternative by learning adaptive control strategies through autonomous interaction with a simulation environment. Overcoming the Sim2Real gap, which involves deploying an agent trained in simulation onto the real physical satellite, remains a significant challenge. In this work, we present the first successful in-orbit demonstration of an AI-based attitude controller for inertial pointing maneuvers. The controller was trained entirely in simulation and deployed to the InnoCube 3U nanosatellite, which was developed by the Julius-Maximilians-Universität Würzburg in cooperation with the Technische Universität Berlin, and launched in January 2025. We present the AI agent design, the methodology of the training procedure, the discrepancies between the simulation and the observed behavior of the real satellite, and a comparison of the AI-based attitude controller with the classical PD controller of InnoCube. Steady-state metrics confirm the robust performance of the AI-based controller during repeated in-orbit maneuvers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LeLaR：首个基于人工智能的卫星姿态控制器在轨演示验证
姿态控制对多数卫星任务至关重要。然而，传统控制器设计耗时，且对模型不确定性及运行边界条件变化敏感。深度强化学习通过在与仿真环境的自主交互中学习自适应控制策略，提供了有前景的替代方案。克服仿真到现实的差距——即将仿真训练的智能体部署至真实物理卫星——仍是重大挑战。本研究首次成功演示了基于人工智能的姿态控制器在惯性指向机动中的在轨应用。该控制器完全在仿真环境中训练，并部署至由维尔茨堡大学与柏林工业大学合作研制、于2025年1月发射的InnoCube 3U纳卫星。我们介绍了人工智能智能体设计、训练流程方法、仿真与真实卫星观测行为间的差异，以及基于人工智能的姿态控制器与InnoCube传统PD控制器的对比。稳态指标证实了基于人工智能的控制器在重复在轨机动中的鲁棒性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of classical satellite attitude controllers, which are labor-intensive to design and vulnerable to model errors and changing conditions, this work demonstrates the first in-orbit use of a Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL)-based controller. The method involved training an AI agent entirely in simulation and then deploying it on the InnoCube nanosatellite to perform inertial pointing maneuvers, directly addressing the Sim2Real transfer challenge. Experimental results from orbit showed robust performance during repeated maneuvers, with steady-state metrics confirming that the AI controller performed comparably to or better than the satellite's classical PD controller.
针对传统卫星姿态控制器设计耗时、对模型不确定性和工况变化敏感的问题，本研究首次在轨演示了基于深度强化学习（DRL）的控制器。该方法通过在仿真环境中完全训练AI智能体，并将其部署至InnoCube立方星上执行惯性指向机动，直接应对了从仿真到实际（Sim2Real）的迁移挑战。在轨实验结果表明，该AI控制器在重复机动中表现稳健，稳态性能指标证实其性能与卫星传统的PD控制器相当或更优。
$R_\text{dm}$: Re-conceptualizing Distribution Matching as a Reward for Diffusion Distillation
Authors: Linqian Fan, Peiqin Sun, Tiancheng Wen, Shun Lu, Chengru Song
First: 2026-03-30T14:01:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T14:28:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion models achieve state-of-the-art generative performance but are fundamentally bottlenecked by their slow, iterative sampling process. While diffusion distillation techniques enable high-fidelity, few-step generation, traditional objectives often restrict the student's performance by anchoring it solely to the teacher. Recent approaches have attempted to break this ceiling by integrating Reinforcement Learning (RL), typically through a simple summation of distillation and RL objectives. In this work, we propose a novel paradigm by re-conceptualizing distribution matching as a reward, denoted as $R_\text{dm}$. This unified perspective bridges the algorithmic gap between Diffusion Matching Distillation (DMD) and RL, providing several primary benefits. (1) Enhanced Optimization Stability: We introduce Group Normalized Distribution Matching (GNDM), which adapts standard RL group normalization to stabilize $R_\text{dm}$ estimation. By leveraging group-mean statistics, GNDM establishes a more robust and effective optimization direction. (2) Seamless Reward Integration: Our reward-centric formulation inherently supports adaptive weighting mechanisms, allowing for the fluid combination of DMD with external reward models. (3) Improved Sampling Efficiency: By aligning with RL principles, the framework readily incorporates Importance Sampling (IS), leading to a significant boost in sampling efficiency. Extensive experiments demonstrate that GNDM outperforms vanilla DMD, reducing the FID by 1.87. Furthermore, our multi-reward variant, GNDMR, surpasses existing baselines by striking an optimal balance between aesthetic quality and fidelity, achieving a peak HPS of 30.37 and a low FID-SD of 12.21. Ultimately, $R_\text{dm}$ provides a flexible, stable, and efficient framework for real-time, high-fidelity synthesis. Codes are coming soon.
中文标题/摘要
标题：$R_\text{dm}$：将分布匹配重构为扩散蒸馏的奖励函数
扩散模型虽能实现最先进的生成性能，但其缓慢的迭代采样过程构成根本瓶颈。扩散蒸馏技术虽能实现高保真度的少步生成，但传统目标常通过将学生模型仅锚定于教师模型而限制其性能。近期研究尝试通过强化学习（RL）突破此限制，通常采用蒸馏目标与RL目标的简单叠加。本研究提出一种新范式：将分布匹配重构为奖励函数$R_\text{dm}$。这一统一视角弥合了扩散匹配蒸馏（DMD）与RL间的算法鸿沟，并带来三大优势：（1）增强优化稳定性：提出组归一化分布匹配（GNDM），将标准RL组归一化技术适配于$R_\text{dm}$估计的稳定化。通过利用组均值统计量，GNDM建立了更稳健有效的优化方向。（2）无缝奖励集成：以奖励为核心的公式天然支持自适应加权机制，可实现DMD与外部奖励模型的灵活组合。（3）提升采样效率：基于RL原则的框架可直接引入重要性采样（IS），显著提升采样效率。大量实验表明，GNDM优于原始DMD，将FID降低1.87。此外，我们的多奖励变体GNDMR通过在美学质量与保真度间取得最优平衡，以30.37的峰值HPS和12.21的低FID-SD超越现有基线。最终，$R_\text{dm}$为实时高保真合成提供了灵活、稳定且高效的框架。代码即将发布。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the slow sampling of diffusion models by proposing a novel distillation paradigm that re-conceptualizes distribution matching as a reward, termed R_dm, to bridge diffusion matching distillation (DMD) and reinforcement learning (RL). The method introduces Group Normalized Distribution Matching (GNDM) to stabilize reward estimation and leverages RL principles like importance sampling for efficiency, enabling seamless integration with external rewards. Experimental results show GNDM reduces FID by 1.87 over vanilla DMD, and its multi-reward variant, GNDMR, achieves superior aesthetic quality and fidelity with a peak HPS of 30.37 and low FID-SD of 12.21, offering a stable framework for real-time synthesis.
本文针对扩散模型采样速度慢的问题，提出了一种新的蒸馏范式，将分布匹配重新概念化为一种奖励（R_dm），以弥合扩散匹配蒸馏（DMD）与强化学习（RL）之间的算法差距。该方法引入了组归一化分布匹配（GNDM）来稳定奖励估计，并利用重要性采样等RL原理提高效率，从而支持与外部奖励模型的无缝集成。实验结果表明，GNDM相比原始DMD将FID降低了1.87，其多奖励变体GNDMR在美学质量和保真度之间取得了最佳平衡，实现了30.37的峰值HPS和12.21的低FID-SD，为实时高保真合成提供了一个灵活稳定的框架。
Reasoning-Driven Synthetic Data Generation and Evaluation
Authors: Tim R. Davidson, Benoit Seguin, Enrico Bacis, Cesar Ilharco, Hamza Harkous
First: 2026-03-31T14:26:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T14:26:33+00:00
Comments: Accepted to TMLR 2026, J2C Certification
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Although many AI applications of interest require specialized multi-modal models, relevant data to train such models is inherently scarce or inaccessible. Filling these gaps with human annotators is prohibitively expensive, error-prone, and time-consuming, leading model builders to increasingly consider synthetic data as a scalable alternative. However, existing synthetic data generation methods often rely on manual prompts, evolutionary algorithms, or extensive seed data from the target distribution - limiting their scalability, explainability, and control. In this paper, we introduce Simula: a novel reasoning-driven framework for data generation and evaluation. It employs a seedless, agentic approach to generate synthetic datasets at scale, allowing users to define desired dataset characteristics through an explainable and controllable process that enables fine-grained resource allocation. We show the efficacy of our approach on a variety of datasets, rigorously testing both intrinsic and downstream properties. Our work (1) offers guidelines for synthetic data mechanism design, (2) provides insights into generating and evaluating synthetic data at scale, and (3) unlocks new opportunities for developing and deploying AI in domains where data scarcity or privacy concerns are paramount.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推理驱动的合成数据生成与评估
尽管许多备受关注的AI应用需要专业的多模态模型，但训练此类模型所需的相关数据本质上稀缺或难以获取。通过人工标注填补这些空白成本极高、易出错且耗时，促使模型构建者日益将合成数据视为可扩展的替代方案。然而，现有的合成数据生成方法通常依赖人工提示、进化算法或来自目标分布的大量种子数据——这限制了其可扩展性、可解释性和可控性。本文提出Simula：一种新颖的推理驱动数据生成与评估框架。它采用无种子的智能体方法大规模生成合成数据集，允许用户通过可解释且可控的流程定义期望的数据集特性，实现细粒度资源分配。我们在多种数据集上验证了该方法的有效性，严格测试了其内在特性与下游性能。本工作（1）为合成数据机制设计提供指导原则，（2）为大规模生成与评估合成数据提供洞见，（3）为在数据稀缺或隐私问题至关重要的领域开发和部署AI开辟新机遇。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the scarcity and inaccessibility of specialized multi-modal training data, and the high cost and limitations of human annotation and existing synthetic methods, this paper introduces Simula, a reasoning-driven framework for synthetic data generation and evaluation. The method employs a seedless, agentic approach that allows users to define dataset characteristics through an explainable and controllable process for fine-grained resource allocation. Experimental results on various datasets demonstrate the framework's efficacy in testing intrinsic and downstream properties, offering design guidelines, insights for scalable generation and evaluation, and enabling AI development in data-scarce or privacy-sensitive domains.
本文的动机在于专业多模态训练数据稀缺且难以获取，而人工标注和现有合成方法成本高、可扩展性和可控性有限。为此，论文提出了Simula，一种基于推理的合成数据生成与评估框架，其方法采用无种子、智能体驱动的方式，允许用户通过可解释、可控的过程定义数据集特征，实现细粒度资源分配。在多种数据集上的实验结果表明，该框架能有效测试数据的内在和下游性能，为合成数据机制设计提供了指导，为大规模生成和评估提供了见解，并在数据稀缺或隐私敏感的领域为AI开发部署开辟了新机会。
Associative Constructive Evolution: Enhancing Metaheuristics through Hebbian-Learned Generative Guidance
Authors: Shanxian Lin, Yuichi Nagata, Haichuan Yang
First: 2026-03-31T14:14:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T14:14:40+00:00
Comments: 4 pages, accepted as a short paper (poster) at GECCO 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Metaheuristic algorithms such as Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO) and Evolutionary Algorithms (EA) excel at exploring solution spaces but lack mechanisms to accumulate and reuse procedural knowledge from successful search trajectories. This paper proposes Associative Constructive Evolution (ACE), a framework that enhances metaheuristics through learned generative guidance. ACE introduces a Generative Construction Automaton (GCA) -- a probabilistic model over operation sequences -- coupled with the base metaheuristic in a synergistic loop: the metaheuristic explores and provides trajectory samples, while the GCA consolidates successful patterns and guides future exploration. Three mechanisms realize this cooperation: Hebbian weight consolidation that strengthens associations between co-successful operations, guided sampling that biases search toward learned high-quality regions, and symbolic abstraction that extracts frequent patterns into reusable macro-operations. Experiments integrating ACE with EA and PSO on molecular design and maze navigation demonstrate consistent improvements. ACE-PSO achieves a 27.5% increase in success rate while reducing convergence time by 49.6%. In molecular design, ACE-EA improves fitness by 10.1% with 126 chemically interpretable macro-operations automatically discovered.
中文标题/摘要
标题：关联构造进化：通过赫布学习生成式引导增强元启发式算法
粒子群优化（PSO）和进化算法（EA）等元启发式算法擅长探索解空间，但缺乏积累和重用成功搜索轨迹中过程性知识的机制。本文提出关联构造进化（ACE）框架，通过学习生成式引导增强元启发式算法。ACE引入生成构造自动机（GCA）——一种基于操作序列的概率模型，与基础元启发式算法形成协同循环：元启发式算法负责探索并提供轨迹样本，而GCA则整合成功模式并引导未来探索。该协作通过三种机制实现：强化共成功操作间关联的赫布权重巩固、引导搜索偏向已学习高质量区域的引导采样，以及将频繁模式提取为可重用宏操作的符号抽象。在分子设计和迷宫导航任务中将ACE与EA、PSO结合的实验显示出一致的性能提升：ACE-PSO成功率提高27.5%，收敛时间减少49.6%；在分子设计中，ACE-EA适应度提升10.1%，并自动发现126个具有化学可解释性的宏操作。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inability of standard metaheuristics like PSO and EA to accumulate and reuse procedural knowledge from successful searches, this paper proposes the Associative Constructive Evolution (ACE) framework to enhance them with learned generative guidance. The method introduces a Generative Construction Automaton (GCA), a probabilistic model of operation sequences, which works synergistically with a base metaheuristic in a loop: the metaheuristic provides trajectory samples, and the GCA consolidates successful patterns via Hebbian weight consolidation, guided sampling, and symbolic abstraction into macro-operations. Experimental results on molecular design and maze navigation show consistent improvements, with ACE-PSO achieving a 27.5% higher success rate and 49.6% faster convergence, while ACE-EA improves fitness by 10.1% and discovers 126 interpretable macro-operations.
针对粒子群优化和进化算法等元启发式算法无法积累和重用成功搜索轨迹中的过程知识这一问题，本文提出了关联构造进化框架，通过学习生成式指导来增强这些算法。该方法引入了生成构造自动机，这是一个操作序列的概率模型，它与基础元启发式算法协同工作：元启发式算法进行探索并提供轨迹样本，而生成构造自动机则通过赫布权重巩固、引导采样和符号抽象提取可重用宏操作来整合成功模式。在分子设计和迷宫导航上的实验结果表明了性能的持续提升，其中ACE-PSO的成功率提高了27.5%，收敛时间减少了49.6%，而ACE-EA的适应度提高了10.1%，并自动发现了126个化学可解释的宏操作。
Principal Prototype Analysis on Manifold for Interpretable Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Bodla Krishna Vamshi, Haizhao Yang
First: 2026-03-30T02:48:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T14:11:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent years have witnessed the widespread adoption of reinforcement learning (RL), from solving real-time games to fine-tuning large language models using human preference data significantly improving alignment with user expectations. However, as model complexity grows exponentially, the interpretability of these systems becomes increasingly challenging. While numerous explainability methods have been developed for computer vision and natural language processing to elucidate both local and global reasoning patterns, their application to RL remains limited. Direct extensions of these methods often struggle to maintain the delicate balance between interpretability and performance within RL settings. Prototype-Wrapper Networks (PW-Nets) have recently shown promise in bridging this gap by enhancing explainability in RL domains without sacrificing the efficiency of the original black-box models. However, these methods typically require manually defined reference prototypes, which often necessitate expert domain knowledge. In this work, we propose a method that removes this dependency by automatically selecting optimal prototypes from the available data. Preliminary experiments on standard Gym environments demonstrate that our approach matches the performance of existing PW-Nets, while remaining competitive with the original black-box models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向可解释强化学习的流形主原型分析
近年来，强化学习（RL）得到广泛应用，从解决实时游戏到利用人类偏好数据微调大语言模型，显著提升了与用户期望的对齐度。然而，随着模型复杂度呈指数级增长，这些系统的可解释性日益成为挑战。尽管计算机视觉和自然语言处理领域已发展出众多可解释性方法来阐明局部和全局推理模式，但它们在RL中的应用仍有限。这些方法的直接扩展往往难以在RL环境中保持可解释性与性能间的微妙平衡。原型封装网络（PW-Nets）近期展现出潜力，能在不牺牲原始黑盒模型效率的前提下增强RL领域的可解释性。但这类方法通常需要人工定义参考原型，往往依赖专家领域知识。本研究提出一种方法，通过从可用数据中自动选择最优原型来消除这种依赖。在标准Gym环境中的初步实验表明，我们的方法在保持与原始黑盒模型竞争力的同时，达到了现有PW-Nets的性能水平。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance interpretability in complex reinforcement learning (RL) systems without sacrificing performance, this paper proposes a method that automatically selects optimal prototypes from data to explain RL decisions, eliminating the dependency on manually defined prototypes. The approach builds upon Prototype-Wrapper Networks (PW-Nets) by introducing a data-driven prototype selection mechanism, aiming to maintain model efficiency while improving explainability. Experimental results on standard Gym environments show that the method achieves performance comparable to existing PW-Nets and remains competitive with the original black-box models.
本文旨在解决强化学习系统因模型复杂化而可解释性不足的问题，同时避免性能损失，提出了一种从数据中自动选择最优原型的方法，以消除对人工定义原型的依赖。该方法基于原型包装网络，通过数据驱动的原型选择机制来增强可解释性，同时保持模型效率。在标准Gym环境中的初步实验表明，该方法与现有原型包装网络的性能相当，并与原始黑盒模型保持竞争力。
Beyond Hard Constraints: Budget-Conditioned Reachability For Safe Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Janaka Chathuranga Brahmanage, Akshat Kumar
First: 2026-03-08T11:09:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T13:32:58+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the 36th International Conference on Automated Planning and Scheduling (ICAPS 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sequential decision making using Markov Decision Process underpins many realworld applications. Both model-based and model free methods have achieved strong results in these settings. However, real-world tasks must balance reward maximization with safety constraints, often conflicting objectives, that can lead to unstable min/max, adversarial optimization. A promising alternative is safety reachability analysis, which precomputes a forward-invariant safe state, action set, ensuring that an agent starting inside this set remains safe indefinitely. Yet, most reachability based methods address only hard safety constraints, and little work extends reachability to cumulative cost constraints. To address this, first, we define a safetyconditioned reachability set that decouples reward maximization from cumulative safety cost constraints. Second, we show how this set enforces safety constraints without unstable min/max or Lagrangian optimization, yielding a novel offline safe RL algorithm that learns a safe policy from a fixed dataset without environment interaction. Finally, experiments on standard offline safe RL benchmarks, and a real world maritime navigation task demonstrate that our method matches or outperforms state of the art baselines while maintaining safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越硬约束：面向安全离线强化学习的预算条件可达性分析
基于马尔可夫决策过程的序列决策方法支撑着众多现实应用，模型驱动与无模型方法在此类场景中均取得显著成果。然而，实际任务需在奖励最大化与安全约束间取得平衡，这两者常存在冲突，可能导致不稳定的极小极大对抗优化。安全可达性分析作为一种有前景的替代方案，通过预计算前向不变的安全状态与动作集合，确保智能体从该集合出发后可永久保持安全。但现有可达性方法多局限于硬安全约束，鲜有研究将其扩展至累积成本约束。为此，本文首先定义了一种安全条件可达集，将奖励最大化与累积安全成本约束解耦；其次，论证该集合如何在不依赖不稳定极小极大优化或拉格朗日方法的前提下强制执行安全约束，进而提出一种新型离线安全强化学习算法，可从固定数据集中学习安全策略而无需环境交互；最后，在标准离线安全强化学习基准及真实海事导航任务上的实验表明，本方法在保持安全性的同时达到或超越了当前最优基线性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of balancing reward maximization with cumulative safety constraints in offline reinforcement learning, moving beyond traditional hard constraints that often lead to unstable adversarial optimization. The authors propose a novel method that defines a safety-conditioned reachability set, which decouples reward objectives from safety costs, thereby avoiding the need for min/max or Lagrangian optimization. Experimental results on standard offline safe RL benchmarks and a real-world maritime navigation task show that the method matches or outperforms state-of-the-art baselines while consistently maintaining safety.
本文针对离线强化学习中奖励最大化与累积安全约束平衡的挑战，超越了传统硬约束方法常导致的不稳定对抗优化问题。作者提出了一种新方法，通过定义安全条件可达集，将奖励目标与安全成本解耦，从而避免了最小/最大或拉格朗日优化。在标准离线安全强化学习基准和真实世界海上导航任务上的实验结果表明，该方法在保持安全性的同时，达到或超越了现有先进基线的性能。
mlr3mbo: Bayesian Optimization in R
Authors: Marc Becker, Lennart Schneider, Martin Binder, Lars Kotthoff, Bernd Bischl
First: 2026-03-31T13:28:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T13:28:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present mlr3mbo, a comprehensive and modular toolbox for Bayesian optimization in R. mlr3mbo supports single- and multi-objective optimization, multi-point proposals, batch and asynchronous parallelization, input and output transformations, and robust error handling. While it can be used for many standard Bayesian optimization variants in applied settings, researchers can also construct custom BO algorithms from its flexible building blocks. In addition to an introduction to the software, its design principles, and its building blocks, the paper presents two extensive empirical evaluations of the software on the surrogate-based benchmark suite YAHPO Gym. To identify robust default configurations for both numeric and mixed-hierarchical optimization regimes, and to gain further insights into the respective impacts of individual settings, we run a coordinate descent search over the mlr3mbo configuration space and analyze its results. Furthermore, we demonstrate that mlr3mbo achieves state-of-the-art performance by benchmarking it against a wide range of optimizers, including HEBO, SMAC3, Ax, and Optuna.
中文标题/摘要
标题：mlr3mbo：R语言中的贝叶斯优化工具箱
本文介绍mlr3mbo，这是一个用于R语言中贝叶斯优化的全面模块化工具箱。mlr3mbo支持单目标与多目标优化、多点提议、批处理与异步并行化、输入输出转换以及鲁棒的错误处理。该工具既适用于应用场景中的多种标准贝叶斯优化变体，研究人员也可基于其灵活构建模块定制专属的BO算法。除介绍软件的设计原理与核心模块外，本文还通过基于代理模型的基准测试套件YAHPO Gym对软件进行了两项详尽的实证评估：为确定数值优化与混合层次优化场景下的鲁棒默认配置，并深入探究各参数设置的具体影响，我们在mlr3mbo配置空间上执行坐标下降搜索并分析结果；同时，通过将mlr3mbo与HEBO、SMAC3、Ax、Optuna等多种优化器进行基准对比，验证了其具备业界领先的性能表现。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind mlr3mbo is to provide a flexible and comprehensive toolbox for Bayesian optimization in R, addressing the need for both applied use and customizable research algorithms. The method involves a modular design that supports single- and multi-objective optimization, multi-point proposals, parallelization, transformations, and error handling, allowing users to build custom algorithms from its components. Experimental results from evaluations on the YAHPO Gym benchmark suite show that mlr3mbo achieves state-of-the-art performance when benchmarked against optimizers like HEBO, SMAC3, Ax, and Optuna, with coordinate descent searches identifying robust default configurations for numeric and mixed-hierarchical optimization regimes.
mlr3mbo 的开发动机是为 R 语言提供一个灵活且全面的贝叶斯优化工具箱，以满足实际应用和可定制研究算法的需求。该方法采用模块化设计，支持单目标和多目标优化、多点提议、并行化、数据转换和错误处理，用户可利用其组件构建自定义算法。在 YAHPO Gym 基准测试套件上的实验结果表明，mlr3mbo 在与 HEBO、SMAC3、Ax 和 Optuna 等优化器的对比中达到了先进性能，并通过坐标下降搜索为数值和混合层次优化场景确定了稳健的默认配置。
Precision autotuning for linear solvers via contextual bandit-based RL
Authors: Erin Carson, Xinye Chen
First: 2026-01-02T15:59:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T13:27:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose a reinforcement learning (RL) framework for adaptive precision tuning for linear solvers, which can be extended to general algorithms. The framework is formulated as a contextual bandit problem and solved using incremental action-value estimation with a discretized state space to select optimal precision configurations for computational steps, balancing precision and computational efficiency. To verify its effectiveness, we apply the framework to iterative refinement for solving linear systems $Ax = b$. In this application, our approach dynamically chooses precisions based on calculated features from the system while maintaining acceptable accuracy and convergence. In detail, an action-value estimator takes discretized features (e.g., approximate condition number and matrix norm) as input and outputs estimated action values, from which a policy selects the actions (chosen precision configurations for specific steps), optimized via an $ε$-greedy strategy to maximize a multi-objective reward to balance accuracy and computational cost. Empirical results demonstrate effective precision selection, reducing computational cost while maintaining accuracy comparable to double-precision baselines. The framework generalizes to diverse out-of-sample data and provides insights into applying RL precision selection to other numerical algorithms, advancing mixed-precision numerical methods in scientific computing. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work on precision autotuning with RL with verification on unseen datasets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于上下文老虎机强化学习的线性求解器精度自动调优
我们提出了一种用于线性求解器自适应精度调优的强化学习框架，该框架可扩展至通用算法。该框架被建模为上下文老虎机问题，通过离散化状态空间下的增量动作价值估计来求解，以选择计算步骤的最优精度配置，从而平衡精度与计算效率。为验证其有效性，我们将该框架应用于求解线性方程组 $Ax = b$ 的迭代精化过程。在此应用中，我们的方法基于系统计算特征动态选择精度，同时保持可接受的精度与收敛性。具体而言，动作价值估计器以离散化特征（如近似条件数与矩阵范数）为输入，输出估计的动作价值，策略据此选择动作（特定步骤的精度配置），并通过 $ε$-贪心策略优化，以最大化平衡精度与计算成本的多目标奖励。实证结果表明，该方法能有效选择精度，在保持与双精度基准相当精度的同时降低计算成本。该框架可泛化至多样化的样本外数据，并为将强化学习精度选择应用于其他数值算法提供了思路，推动了科学计算中混合精度数值方法的发展。据我们所知，这是首个基于强化学习进行精度自动调优并在未见数据集上验证的工作。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to balance computational efficiency and numerical accuracy in scientific computing, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning framework for adaptive precision tuning in linear solvers, formulated as a contextual bandit problem. The method employs incremental action-value estimation with a discretized state space, using features like approximate condition number and matrix norm to select optimal precision configurations via an ε-greedy policy that maximizes a multi-objective reward combining accuracy and cost. Experimental results on iterative refinement for linear systems show that the approach effectively reduces computational cost while maintaining accuracy comparable to double-precision baselines, generalizing well to unseen datasets and offering a pathway for extending RL-based precision autotuning to other numerical algorithms.
本文旨在解决科学计算中计算效率与数值精度平衡的问题，提出了一个基于强化学习的自适应精度调优框架，用于线性求解器，并将其建模为上下文赌博机问题。该方法采用离散化状态空间的增量动作值估计，利用近似条件数和矩阵范数等特征，通过ε-贪婪策略选择最优精度配置，以最大化兼顾精度与成本的多目标奖励。在线性系统迭代精化应用的实验中，该方法在保持与双精度基线相当精度的同时，有效降低了计算成本，并能泛化到未见数据集，为将强化学习精度选择扩展到其他数值算法提供了见解。
Reinforced Reasoning for End-to-End Retrosynthetic Planning
Authors: Chenyang Zuo, Siqi Fan, Yizhen Luo, Zaiqing Nie
First: 2026-03-31T13:22:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T13:22:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrosynthetic planning is a fundamental task in organic chemistry, yet remains challenging due to its combinatorial complexity. To address this, conventional approaches typically rely on hybrid frameworks that combine single-step predictions with external search heuristics, inevitably fracturing the logical coherence between local molecular transformations and global planning objectives. To bridge this gap and embed sophisticated strategic foresight directly into the model's chemical reasoning, we introduce ReTriP, an end-to-end generative framework that reformulates retrosynthesis as a direct Chain-of-Thought reasoning task. We establish a path-coherent molecular representation and employ a progressive training curriculum that transitions from reasoning distillation to reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, effectively aligning stepwise generation with practical route utility. Empirical evaluation on RetroBench demonstrates that ReTriP achieves state-of-the-art performance, exhibiting superior robustness in long-horizon planning compared to hybrid baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：端到端逆合成规划的强化推理方法
逆合成规划是有机化学中的基础任务，但其组合复杂性使其仍具挑战性。传统方法通常依赖混合框架，将单步预测与外部搜索启发式结合，这不可避免地割裂了局部分子转化与全局规划目标间的逻辑连贯性。为弥合此差距并将复杂战略预见直接嵌入模型的化学推理中，我们提出ReTriP——一种端到端生成框架，将逆合成重构为直接的思维链推理任务。我们建立了路径连贯的分子表示，并采用渐进式训练策略，从推理蒸馏过渡到基于可验证奖励的强化学习，有效将逐步生成与实际路线效用对齐。在RetroBench上的实证评估表明，ReTriP实现了最先进的性能，相比混合基线方法，在长程规划中展现出更优的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the combinatorial complexity and fractured logic of conventional hybrid frameworks in retrosynthetic planning by embedding strategic foresight directly into the model's reasoning. The method introduces ReTriP, an end-to-end generative framework that reformulates retrosynthesis as a Chain-of-Thought reasoning task, using a path-coherent molecular representation and a progressive training curriculum combining reasoning distillation with reinforcement learning. The main experimental results on RetroBench show that ReTriP achieves state-of-the-art performance, demonstrating superior robustness in long-horizon planning compared to existing hybrid baselines.
本研究的动机是克服传统混合框架在逆合成规划中的组合复杂性和逻辑割裂问题，旨在将战略预见性直接嵌入模型的化学推理中。方法上提出了ReTriP，这是一个端到端的生成框架，将逆合成重新定义为思维链推理任务，采用路径一致的分子表示和从推理蒸馏过渡到强化学习的渐进式训练课程。在RetroBench上的主要实验结果表明，ReTriP实现了最先进的性能，与混合基线相比，在长程规划中表现出更优的鲁棒性。
6GAgentGym: Tool Use, Data Synthesis, and Agentic Learning for Network Management
Authors: Jiao Chen, Jianhua Tang, Xiaotong Yang, Zuohong Lv
First: 2026-03-31T12:21:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T12:21:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous 6G network management requires agents that can execute tools, observe the resulting state changes, and adapt their decisions accordingly. Existing benchmarks based on static questions or scripted episode replay, however, do not support such closed-loop interaction, limiting agents to passive evaluation without the ability to learn from environmental feedback. This paper presents 6GAgentGym to provide closed-loop capability. The framework provides an interactive environment with 42 typed tools whose effect classification distinguishes read-only observation from state-mutating configuration, backed by a learned Experiment Model calibrated on NS-3 simulation data. 6G-Forge bootstraps closed-loop training trajectories from NS-3 seeds via iterative Self-Instruct generation with execution verification against the Experiment Model. Supervised fine-tuning on the resulting corpus followed by reinforcement learning with online closed-loop interaction enables an 8B open-source model to achieve comparable overall success rate to GPT-5 on the accompanying 6GAgentBench, with stronger performance on long-horizon tasks. Together, these components provide a viable path toward autonomous, closed-loop network management.
中文标题/摘要
标题：6GAgentGym：面向网络管理的工具使用、数据合成与智能体学习
自主6G网络管理需要智能体能够执行工具、观察状态变化并相应调整决策。然而，现有基于静态问题或脚本化场景回放的基准测试无法支持此类闭环交互，限制了智能体仅能被动评估而无法从环境反馈中学习。本文提出6GAgentGym以提供闭环能力。该框架提供包含42种类型工具的交互环境，其效果分类区分只读观察与状态变更配置，并依托基于NS-3仿真数据校准的学习型实验模型。6G-Forge通过迭代式自指令生成与实验模型执行验证，从NS-3种子数据中构建闭环训练轨迹。对生成语料进行监督微调后，结合在线闭环交互的强化学习，使一个80亿参数开源模型在配套的6GAgentBench上达到与GPT-5相当的整体成功率，且在长周期任务中表现更优。这些组件共同为自主闭环网络管理提供了可行路径。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces 6GAgentGym, a framework designed to address the lack of closed-loop interaction in existing benchmarks for autonomous 6G network management, where agents must use tools and learn from environmental feedback. The method features an interactive environment with 42 typed tools and a learned Experiment Model, using a data synthesis pipeline called 6G-Forge to generate training trajectories from NS-3 simulation seeds via Self-Instruct with execution verification. Experimental results show that supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning on this corpus enable an 8B open-source model to match GPT-5's overall success rate on the 6GAgentBench benchmark, with superior performance on long-horizon tasks, demonstrating a viable path toward autonomous network operation.

ASI-Evolve: AI Accelerates AI
Authors: Weixian Xu, Tiantian Mi, Yixiu Liu, Yang Nan, Zhimeng Zhou, Lyumanshan Ye, Lin Zhang, Yu Qiao, Pengfei Liu
First: 2026-03-31T12:04:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T12:04:17+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 6 figures, 6 tables. Code available at https://github.com/GAIR-NLP/ASI-Evolve
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Can AI accelerate the development of AI itself? While recent agentic systems have shown strong performance on well-scoped tasks with rapid feedback, it remains unclear whether they can tackle the costly, long-horizon, and weakly supervised research loops that drive real AI progress. We present ASI-Evolve, an agentic framework for AI-for-AI research that closes this loop through a learn-design-experiment-analyze cycle. ASI-Evolve augments standard evolutionary agents with two key components: a cognition base that injects accumulated human priors into each round of exploration, and a dedicated analyzer that distills complex experimental outcomes into reusable insights for future iterations. To our knowledge, ASI-Evolve is the first unified framework to demonstrate AI-driven discovery across three central components of AI development: data, architectures, and learning algorithms. In neural architecture design, it discovered 105 SOTA linear attention architectures, with the best discovered model surpassing DeltaNet by +0.97 points, nearly 3x the gain of recent human-designed improvements. In pretraining data curation, the evolved pipeline improves average benchmark performance by +3.96 points, with gains exceeding 18 points on MMLU. In reinforcement learning algorithm design, discovered algorithms outperform GRPO by up to +12.5 points on AMC32, +11.67 points on AIME24, and +5.04 points on OlympiadBench. We further provide initial evidence that this AI-for-AI paradigm can transfer beyond the AI stack through experiments in mathematics and biomedicine. Together, these results suggest that ASI-Evolve represents a promising step toward enabling AI to accelerate AI across the foundational stages of development, offering early evidence for the feasibility of closed-loop AI research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ASI-Evolve：人工智能加速人工智能发展
人工智能能否加速其自身发展？近期智能体系统虽在反馈迅速的明确任务中表现优异，但其能否应对推动真实AI进展所需的高成本、长周期、弱监督的研究闭环仍存疑问。我们提出ASI-Evolve——一个面向AI-for-AI研究的智能体框架，通过“学习-设计-实验-分析”循环实现闭环研究。该框架在标准进化智能体中融入两大核心组件：认知库（向每轮探索注入累积的人类先验知识）与专用分析器（将复杂实验结果提炼为可复用的迭代洞见）。据我们所知，ASI-Evolve是首个在AI开发的三大核心领域（数据、架构、学习算法）均实现AI驱动发现的统一框架。在神经架构设计中，它发现了105个SOTA线性注意力架构，最优模型超越DeltaNet达0.97分，增益接近近期人工设计改进的3倍；在预训练数据构建中，进化流程将基准性能平均提升3.96分，MMLU任务增益超18分；在强化学习算法设计中，新算法在AMC32、AIME24和OlympiadBench上分别超越GRPO达12.5分、11.67分和5.04分。我们通过数学与生物医学实验进一步证明，该AI-for-AI范式可迁移至AI技术栈之外。这些结果表明，ASI-Evolve为实现AI在基础研发阶段自我加速迈出关键一步，为闭环AI研究的可行性提供了早期实证。
