Motivated by the question of whether AI can accelerate its own development, particularly for costly and long-horizon research tasks, this paper introduces ASI-Evolve, an agentic framework that implements a learn-design-experiment-analyze cycle. The method enhances evolutionary agents with a cognition base to incorporate human priors and an analyzer to distill experimental outcomes into reusable insights. Experimentally, ASI-Evolve demonstrated AI-driven discovery across three key areas: it found 105 state-of-the-art linear attention architectures, with the best model outperforming DeltaNet by +0.97 points; evolved a pretraining data curation pipeline that improved average benchmark performance by +3.96 points; and designed reinforcement learning algorithms that surpassed GRPO by up to +12.5 points on specific benchmarks, showing initial transferability to mathematics and biomedicine.
本文旨在探索人工智能能否加速其自身发展，特别是针对成本高昂、周期漫长的研究任务，提出了ASI-Evolve这一智能体框架，通过一个学习-设计-实验-分析的闭环来实现。该方法在标准进化智能体基础上，引入了认知库以注入人类先验知识，并配备专用分析器将复杂实验结果提炼为可复用的见解。实验结果表明，ASI-Evolve在人工智能开发的三个核心领域实现了AI驱动的发现：在神经架构设计中发现了105个先进的线性注意力架构，最佳模型性能超越DeltaNet达0.97分；在预训练数据策展中，进化出的流程将平均基准性能提升了3.96分；在强化学习算法设计中，发现的算法在特定基准上优于GRPO高达12.5分，并在数学和生物医学领域初步展现了可迁移性。
Operator-Theoretic Foundations and Policy Gradient Methods for General MDPs with Unbounded Costs
Authors: Abhishek Gupta, Aditya Mahajan
First: 2026-03-18T16:01:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T11:58:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Markov decision processes (MDPs) is viewed as an optimization of an objective function over certain linear operators over general function spaces. A new existence result is established for the existence of optimal policies in general MDPs, which differs from the existence result derived previously in the literature. Using the well-established perturbation theory of linear operators, policy difference lemma is established for general MDPs and the Gauteaux derivative of the objective function as a function of the policy operator is derived. By upper bounding the policy difference via the theory of integral probability metric, a new majorization-minimization type policy gradient algorithm for general MDPs is derived. This leads to generalization of many well-known algorithms in reinforcement learning to cases with general state and action spaces. Further, by taking the integral probability metric as maximum mean discrepancy, a low-complexity policy gradient algorithm is derived for finite MDPs. The new algorithm, called MM-RKHS, appears to be superior to PPO algorithm due to low computational complexity, low sample complexity, and faster convergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一般马尔可夫决策过程无界成本的算子理论基础与策略梯度方法
马尔可夫决策过程（MDPs）被视作在一般函数空间上对特定线性算子的目标函数优化。本文针对一般MDPs建立了新的最优策略存在性结果，与文献中已有结论存在差异。基于成熟的线性算子摄动理论，推导了一般MDPs的策略差分引理，并得到目标函数作为策略算子的Gauteaux导数。通过积分概率度量理论对策略差异进行上界估计，提出了一种适用于一般MDPs的新型主控最小化策略梯度算法，从而将强化学习中诸多经典算法推广至具有一般状态与动作空间的场景。进一步地，通过将积分概率度量取为最大均值差异，为有限MDPs设计出低复杂度策略梯度算法MM-RKHS。该算法凭借较低的计算复杂度、样本复杂度及更快的收敛速度，表现出优于PPO算法的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the need for robust theoretical foundations and efficient algorithms in Markov decision processes (MDPs) with unbounded costs and general state-action spaces. The method employs operator-theoretic analysis, using perturbation theory of linear operators to establish a policy difference lemma and derive the Gâteaux derivative of the objective function, then integrates integral probability metrics to bound policy differences and develop a majorization-minimization policy gradient algorithm. Experimental results show that the derived algorithm, particularly the low-complexity MM-RKHS variant for finite MDPs, outperforms PPO in computational efficiency, sample complexity, and convergence speed, generalizing many reinforcement learning algorithms to broader settings.
本文针对具有无界成本和一般状态-动作空间的马尔可夫决策过程，旨在建立坚实的理论基础并开发高效算法。方法上采用算子理论分析，利用线性算子的扰动理论建立了策略差异引理并推导了目标函数的Gâteaux导数，进而结合积分概率度量来约束策略差异，提出了一种基于最大化-最小化的策略梯度算法。实验结果表明，所提出的算法，特别是针对有限MDP的低复杂度MM-RKHS变体，在计算效率、样本复杂度和收敛速度上均优于PPO算法，并将许多强化学习算法推广至更一般的场景。
Evolution Strategies for Deep RL pretraining
Authors: Adrian Martínez, Ananya Gupta, Hanka Goralija, Mario Rico, Saúl Fenollosa, Tamar Alphaidze
First: 2026-03-31T11:30:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T11:30:20+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 3 figures, 2 algorithms; EE-568 Reinforcement learning course project
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Although Deep Reinforcement Learning has proven highly effective for complex decision-making problems, it demands significant computational resources and careful parameter adjustment in order to develop successful strategies. Evolution strategies offer a more straightforward, derivative-free approach that is less computationally costly and simpler to deploy. However, ES generally do not match the performance levels achieved by DRL, which calls into question their suitability for more demanding scenarios. This study examines the performance of ES and DRL across tasks of varying difficulty, including Flappy Bird, Breakout and Mujoco environments, as well as whether ES could be used for initial training to enhance DRL algorithms. The results indicate that ES do not consistently train faster than DRL. When used as a preliminary training step, they only provide benefits in less complex environments (Flappy Bird) and show minimal or no improvement in training efficiency or stability across different parameter settings when applied to more sophisticated tasks (Breakout and MuJoCo Walker).
中文标题/摘要
标题：深度强化学习预训练的进化策略研究
尽管深度强化学习在复杂决策问题上表现出色，但其需要大量计算资源与精细参数调整才能形成有效策略。进化策略提供了一种更直接、无需梯度的替代方案，计算成本更低且部署更简单。然而，进化策略通常难以达到深度强化学习的性能水平，这使其在要求更高的场景中的适用性受到质疑。本研究通过Flappy Bird、Breakout和MuJoCo等不同难度任务，对比了进化策略与深度强化学习的表现，并探讨了进化策略作为初始训练阶段提升深度强化学习算法的可能性。结果表明：进化策略并未持续展现出比深度强化学习更快的训练速度；作为预训练手段时，仅在简单环境（Flappy Bird）中显现优势，而在复杂任务（Breakout与MuJoCo Walker）中，对不同参数配置下的训练效率或稳定性改善甚微甚至无改善。

Experimental results show that ES do not consistently train faster than DRL, and when used for pretraining, they only provide benefits in simpler environments like Flappy Bird, offering minimal or no improvement in training efficiency or stability for more complex tasks such as Breakout and MuJoCo Walker.

Sample-Efficient Hypergradient Estimation for Decentralized Bi-Level Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mikoto Kudo, Takumi Tanabe, Akifumi Wachi, Youhei Akimoto
First: 2026-03-16T06:11:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T10:34:35+00:00
Comments: 26 pages. Accepted at ICAPS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many strategic decision-making problems, such as environment design for warehouse robots, can be naturally formulated as bi-level reinforcement learning (RL), where a leader agent optimizes its objective while a follower solves a Markov decision process (MDP) conditioned on the leader's decisions. In many situations, a fundamental challenge arises when the leader cannot intervene in the follower's optimization process; it can only observe the optimization outcome. We address this decentralized setting by deriving the hypergradient of the leader's objective, i.e., the gradient of the leader's strategy that accounts for changes in the follower's optimal policy. Unlike prior hypergradient-based methods that require extensive data for repeated state visits or rely on gradient estimators whose complexity can increase substantially with the high-dimensional leader's decision space, we leverage the Boltzmann covariance trick to derive an alternative hypergradient formulation. This enables efficient hypergradient estimation solely from interaction samples, even when the leader's decision space is high-dimensional. Additionally, to our knowledge, this is the first method that enables hypergradient-based optimization for 2-player Markov games in decentralized settings. Experiments highlight the impact of hypergradient updates and demonstrate our method's effectiveness in both discrete and continuous state tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：去中心化双层强化学习中的样本高效超梯度估计方法
许多战略决策问题（如仓库机器人的环境设计）可自然建模为双层强化学习：领导者智能体优化其目标函数，而跟随者在领导者决策条件下求解马尔可夫决策过程。当领导者无法干预跟随者优化过程、仅能观测优化结果时，便面临核心挑战。本文通过推导领导者目标函数的超梯度（即考虑跟随者最优策略变化的领导者策略梯度）来解决这一去中心化场景。相较于现有需要大量状态重复访问数据、或梯度估计复杂度随高维决策空间急剧增加的超梯度方法，我们利用玻尔兹曼协方差技巧推导出替代的超梯度形式，仅通过交互样本即可实现高效估计，且适用于高维决策空间。据我们所知，这是首个支持去中心化场景下双人马尔可夫博弈超梯度优化的方法。实验验证了超梯度更新的有效性，并在离散与连续状态任务中证明了方法的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of decentralized bi-level reinforcement learning, where a leader agent must optimize its objective based only on observing the outcomes of a follower's independent optimization process, without direct intervention. To tackle this, the authors derive a hypergradient formulation for the leader's objective by employing the Boltzmann covariance trick, which allows for efficient estimation of the hypergradient using only interaction samples, even in high-dimensional decision spaces. Experimental results demonstrate that the hypergradient updates are impactful and the method is effective across both discrete and continuous state tasks, marking it as the first hypergradient-based approach applicable to decentralized 2-player Markov games.
本文针对去中心化双层强化学习中的挑战，即领导者智能体只能观察跟随者独立优化过程的结果，而无法直接干预，需据此优化自身目标。为解决此问题，作者利用玻尔兹曼协方差技巧推导了领导者目标的超梯度公式，使得仅通过交互样本即可高效估计超梯度，即使在高维决策空间中也能实现。实验结果表明，超梯度更新具有显著影响，且该方法在离散和连续状态任务中均表现有效，这使其成为首个适用于去中心化双人马尔可夫博弈的超梯度优化方法。
Target-Aligned Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Leonard S. Pleiss, James Harrison, Maximilian Schiffer
First: 2026-03-31T09:42:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T09:42:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many reinforcement learning algorithms rely on target networks - lagged copies of the online network - to stabilize training. While effective, this mechanism introduces a fundamental stability-recency tradeoff: slower target updates improve stability but reduce the recency of learning signals, hindering convergence speed. We propose Target-Aligned Reinforcement Learning (TARL), a framework that emphasizes transitions for which the target and online network estimates are highly aligned. By focusing updates on well-aligned targets, TARL mitigates the adverse effects of stale target estimates while retaining the stabilizing benefits of target networks. We provide a theoretical analysis demonstrating that target alignment correction accelerates convergence, and empirically demonstrate consistent improvements over standard reinforcement learning algorithms across various benchmark environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：目标对齐强化学习
许多强化学习算法依赖目标网络——在线网络的滞后副本——来稳定训练。虽然有效，但该机制引入了稳定性与时效性的根本权衡：较慢的目标更新能提升稳定性，却会降低学习信号的时效性，阻碍收敛速度。我们提出目标对齐强化学习框架，该框架强调目标网络与在线网络估计高度对齐的转移过程。通过聚焦于对齐良好的目标进行更新，TARL在保留目标网络稳定优势的同时，缓解了陈旧目标估计的不利影响。我们通过理论分析证明目标对齐校正能加速收敛，并在多种基准环境中通过实验验证其相对于标准强化学习算法的持续改进。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the stability-recency tradeoff inherent in using target networks for reinforcement learning, where slower updates stabilize training but reduce the recency of learning signals, slowing convergence. The authors propose Target-Aligned Reinforcement Learning (TARL), a method that prioritizes updates for transitions where the target and online network estimates are highly aligned, thereby mitigating the negative impact of stale targets while preserving stability. Theoretical analysis shows this alignment accelerates convergence, and experiments across benchmark environments confirm consistent improvements over standard reinforcement learning algorithms.
本文针对强化学习中目标网络带来的稳定性与时效性权衡问题展开研究，即较慢的目标更新虽能稳定训练但会降低学习信号的时效性，从而减缓收敛速度。作者提出了目标对齐强化学习方法，该方法通过优先更新目标网络与在线网络估计高度对齐的转移样本，在保留目标网络稳定优势的同时减轻了陈旧目标的不利影响。理论分析表明目标对齐校正能加速收敛，且在多种基准环境中的实验验证了该方法相对于标准强化学习算法的持续改进。
Learning to Generate Formally Verifiable Step-by-Step Logic Reasoning via Structured Formal Intermediaries
Authors: Luoxin Chen, Yichi Zhou, Huishuai Zhang
First: 2026-03-31T09:42:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T09:42:13+00:00
Comments: 19 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have recently demonstrated impressive performance on complex, multi-step reasoning tasks, especially when post-trained with outcome-rewarded reinforcement learning Guo et al. 2025. However, it has been observed that outcome rewards often overlook flawed intermediate steps, leading to unreliable reasoning steps even when final answers are correct. To address this unreliable reasoning, we propose PRoSFI (Process Reward over Structured Formal Intermediates), a novel reward method that enhances reasoning reliability without compromising accuracy. Instead of generating formal proofs directly, which is rarely accomplishable for a modest-sized (7B) model, the model outputs structured intermediate steps aligned with its natural language reasoning. Each step is then verified by a formal prover. Only fully validated reasoning chains receive high rewards. The integration of formal verification guides the model towards generating step-by-step machine-checkable proofs, thereby yielding more credible final answers. PRoSFI offers a simple and effective approach to training trustworthy reasoning models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过结构化形式中介学习生成可形式验证的逐步逻辑推理
大语言模型（LLMs）近期在复杂多步推理任务上展现出优异性能，尤其是在经过结果奖励强化学习后（Guo等人，2025）。然而研究发现，结果奖励常忽略有缺陷的中间步骤，导致即使最终答案正确，推理步骤仍不可靠。为解决此问题，我们提出PRoSFI（基于结构化形式中间步骤的过程奖励），这是一种在不牺牲准确性的前提下提升推理可靠性的新型奖励方法。模型不直接生成形式化证明（这对中等规模7B参数模型通常难以实现），而是输出与其自然语言推理对齐的结构化中间步骤。每一步均由形式化证明器验证，仅完全通过验证的推理链获得高奖励。形式验证的整合引导模型生成可机器检查的逐步证明，从而产生更可信的最终答案。PRoSFI为训练可信推理模型提供了一种简洁有效的途径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that outcome-rewarded reinforcement learning for large language models often overlooks flawed intermediate steps, leading to unreliable reasoning even when final answers are correct, this paper proposes PRoSFI, a novel reward method that enhances reasoning reliability. The method involves the model generating structured intermediate steps aligned with its natural language reasoning, which are then verified step-by-step by a formal prover, with high rewards given only to fully validated reasoning chains. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach successfully guides the model to produce more credible, machine-checkable proofs without compromising accuracy, offering a simple and effective way to train trustworthy reasoning models.
本文的动机是观察到基于结果奖励的强化学习常忽视大语言模型推理中的错误中间步骤，导致即使最终答案正确，推理过程也不可靠。为此，论文提出了PRoSFI方法，通过让模型生成与其自然语言推理对齐的结构化中间步骤，并利用形式化证明器对每一步进行验证，仅对完全验证通过的推理链给予高奖励。实验结果表明，该方法能有效引导模型生成更可信、可机器验证的逐步证明，且不损害准确性，为训练可信推理模型提供了一种简单有效的方法。
CoMaTrack: Competitive Multi-Agent Game-Theoretic Tracking with Vision-Language-Action Models
Authors: Youzhi Liu, Li Gao, Liu Liu, Mingyang Lv, Yang Cai
First: 2026-03-24T06:35:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T09:31:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Embodied Visual Tracking (EVT), a core dynamic task in embodied intelligence, requires an agent to precisely follow a language-specified target. Yet most existing methods rely on single-agent imitation learning, suffering from costly expert data and limited generalization due to static training environments. Inspired by competition-driven capability evolution, we propose CoMaTrack, a competitive game-theoretic multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that trains agents in a dynamic adversarial setting with competitive subtasks, yielding stronger adaptive planning and interference-resilient strategies. We further introduce CoMaTrack-Bench, the first open-source Habitat-based benchmark protocol and episode set for language-conditioned competitive EVT featuring dynamic dueling, featuring game scenarios between a tracker and adaptive opponents across diverse environments and instructions, enabling standardized robustness evaluation under active adversarial interactions. Experiments show that CoMaTrack achieves state-of-the-art results on both standard benchmarks and CoMaTrack-Bench. Notably, a 3B VLM trained with our framework surpasses previous single-agent imitation learning methods based on 7B models on the challenging EVT-Bench, achieving 92.1% in STT, 74.2% in DT, and 57.5% in AT. The benchmark code will be available at https://github.com/wlqcode/CoMaTrack-Bench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoMaTrack：基于视觉-语言-动作模型的竞争性多智能体博弈论追踪框架
具身视觉追踪（EVT）作为具身智能的核心动态任务，要求智能体精确跟随语言指定的目标。然而现有方法多依赖单智能体模仿学习，受限于高成本专家数据与静态训练环境导致的泛化瓶颈。受竞争驱动能力演化的启发，我们提出CoMaTrack——一种基于博弈论的竞争性多智能体强化学习框架，通过在动态对抗环境中设置竞争性子任务训练智能体，形成更具适应性的规划能力与抗干扰策略。我们进一步推出首个基于Habitat的开源基准协议CoMaTrack-Bench，包含语言条件化竞争性EVT的动态对抗场景数据集，涵盖追踪器与自适应对手在多环境多指令下的博弈情境，支持主动对抗交互下的标准化鲁棒性评估。实验表明CoMaTrack在标准基准与CoMaTrack-Bench上均达到最先进性能。值得注意的是，采用本框架训练的30亿参数视觉语言模型在挑战性EVT-Bench上超越此前基于70亿参数模型的单智能体模仿学习方法，在STT、DT、AT指标上分别达到92.1%、74.2%和57.5%。基准代码将发布于https://github.com/wlqcode/CoMaTrack-Bench。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of single-agent imitation learning in Embodied Visual Tracking (EVT), which suffers from costly expert data and poor generalization, this paper introduces CoMaTrack, a competitive multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that trains agents in adversarial settings with competitive subtasks to develop adaptive planning and interference-resilient strategies. The method includes CoMaTrack-Bench, a new benchmark for language-conditioned competitive EVT featuring dynamic dueling between a tracker and adaptive opponents across diverse environments. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, where a 3B vision-language model trained with CoMaTrack outperforms prior 7B model-based single-agent methods on EVT-Bench, achieving 92.1% in STT, 74.2% in DT, and 57.5% in AT.
针对具身视觉跟踪任务中单智能体模仿学习依赖昂贵专家数据且泛化能力有限的问题，本文提出了CoMaTrack，一种基于竞争性博弈论的多智能体强化学习框架，通过在对抗环境中训练智能体执行竞争性子任务，以提升自适应规划和抗干扰策略能力。该方法还引入了CoMaTrack-Bench，首个基于Habitat的开源基准协议，用于语言条件竞争性具身视觉跟踪，包含追踪器与自适应对手在多样环境中的动态对抗场景。实验结果表明，CoMaTrack在标准基准和CoMaTrack-Bench上均取得最优性能，其中使用该框架训练的30亿参数视觉语言模型在挑战性EVT-Bench上超越了此前基于70亿参数模型的单智能体模仿学习方法，在STT、DT和AT指标上分别达到92.1%、74.2%和57.5%。
QuestA: Expanding Reasoning Capacity in LLMs via Question Augmentation
Authors: Jiazheng Li, Hongzhou Lin, Hong Lu, Kaiyue Wen, Zaiwen Yang, Jiaxuan Gao, Yi Wu, Jingzhao Zhang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-07-17T16:21:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T09:22:36+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 18 figures, ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a central paradigm for training large language models (LLMs) in reasoning tasks. Yet recent studies question RL's ability to incentivize reasoning capacity beyond the base model. This raises a key challenge: how can RL be adapted to solve harder reasoning problems more effectively? To address this challenge, we propose a simple yet effective strategy via Question Augmentation: introduce partial solutions during training to reduce problem difficulty and provide more informative learning signals. Our method, QuestA, when applied during RL training on math reasoning tasks, not only improves pass@1 but also pass@k-particularly on problems where standard RL struggles to make progress. This enables continual improvement over strong open-source models such as DeepScaleR and OpenMath Nemotron, further enhancing their reasoning capabilities. We achieve new state-of-the-art results on math benchmarks using 1.5B-parameter models: 72.50% (+10.73%) on AIME24, 62.29% (+12.79%) on AIME25, and 41.67% (+10.11%) on HMMT25. Code, data and model are available at https://github.com/foreverlasting1202/QuestA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QuestA：通过问题增强扩展大语言模型的推理能力
强化学习已成为训练大语言模型进行推理任务的核心范式。然而，近期研究质疑强化学习能否激励超越基础模型的推理能力。这提出了一个关键挑战：如何调整强化学习以更有效地解决更难的推理问题？为应对这一挑战，我们通过问题增强提出一种简单而有效的策略：在训练中引入部分解决方案以降低问题难度，并提供更具信息量的学习信号。我们的方法QuestA在数学推理任务的强化学习训练中应用时，不仅提升了pass@1，还显著提升了pass@k——尤其是在标准强化学习难以取得进展的问题上。这使得DeepScaleR和OpenMath Nemotron等强大开源模型能够持续改进，进一步增强其推理能力。我们使用15亿参数模型在数学基准测试中取得了新的最先进成果：AIME24达到72.50%（提升10.73%）、AIME25达到62.29%（提升12.79%）、HMMT25达到41.67%（提升10.11%）。代码、数据和模型发布于https://github.com/foreverlasting1202/QuestA。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of reinforcement learning (RL) in enhancing the reasoning capacity of large language models (LLMs) beyond their base capabilities. The proposed method, QuestA, introduces a question augmentation strategy that incorporates partial solutions during RL training to reduce problem difficulty and provide more informative learning signals. Experimental results on math reasoning tasks demonstrate that QuestA significantly improves both pass@1 and pass@k performance, enabling continual improvement over strong open-source models like DeepScaleR and OpenMath Nemotron, and achieving new state-of-the-art results on benchmarks such as AIME24, AIME25, and HMMT25 with 1.5B-parameter models.
本文针对强化学习在提升大语言模型推理能力方面的局限性，提出了一种名为QuestA的方法。该方法通过问题增强策略，在强化学习训练中引入部分解决方案，以降低问题难度并提供更具信息量的学习信号。在数学推理任务上的实验结果表明，QuestA显著提升了pass@1和pass@k性能，使模型在DeepScaleR和OpenMath Nemotron等强开源模型基础上持续改进，并在AIME24、AIME25和HMMT25等基准测试上使用15亿参数模型取得了新的最先进结果。
ReAG: Reasoning-Augmented Generation for Knowledge-based Visual Question Answering
Authors: Alberto Compagnoni, Marco Morini, Sara Sarto, Federico Cocchi, Davide Caffagni, Marcella Cornia, Lorenzo Baraldi, Rita Cucchiara
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-11-27T19:01:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T08:45:37+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026 - Project page: https://aimagelab.github.io/ReAG/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown impressive capabilities in jointly understanding text, images, and videos, often evaluated via Visual Question Answering (VQA). However, even state-of-the-art MLLMs struggle with domain-specific or knowledge-intensive queries, where relevant information is underrepresented in pre-training data. Knowledge-based VQA (KB-VQA) addresses this by retrieving external documents to condition answer generation, but current retrieval-augmented approaches suffer from low precision, noisy passages, and limited reasoning. To address this, we propose ReAG, a novel Reasoning-Augmented Multimodal RAG approach that combines coarse- and fine-grained retrieval with a critic model that filters irrelevant passages, ensuring high-quality additional context. The model follows a multi-stage training strategy leveraging reinforcement learning to enhance reasoning over retrieved content, while supervised fine-tuning serves only as a cold start. Extensive experiments on Encyclopedic-VQA and InfoSeek demonstrate that ReAG significantly outperforms prior methods, improving answer accuracy and providing interpretable reasoning grounded in retrieved evidence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReAG：面向知识型视觉问答的推理增强生成
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在联合理解文本、图像和视频方面展现出卓越能力，通常通过视觉问答（VQA）进行评估。然而，即使是当前最先进的MLLMs在处理领域特定或知识密集型查询时仍面临挑战，这类信息在预训练数据中表征不足。知识型视觉问答（KB-VQA）通过检索外部文档来辅助答案生成，但现有检索增强方法存在精度低、段落噪声大、推理能力有限等问题。为此，我们提出ReAG——一种新颖的推理增强多模态检索增强生成方法，其结合粗粒度与细粒度检索，并引入评判模型过滤无关段落，确保高质量补充语境。该模型采用多阶段训练策略，利用强化学习增强对检索内容的推理能力，而监督微调仅作为冷启动。在Encyclopedic-VQA和InfoSeek数据集上的大量实验表明，ReAG显著优于现有方法，在提升答案准确率的同时，提供基于检索证据的可解释推理过程。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) often fail on domain-specific or knowledge-intensive visual questions due to limited pre-training data, and existing retrieval-augmented methods for knowledge-based VQA suffer from imprecise retrieval and poor reasoning. The proposed method, ReAG, introduces a reasoning-augmented generation framework that employs a two-stage retrieval process (coarse and fine-grained) coupled with a critic model to filter noisy passages, and it uses a multi-stage training strategy involving reinforcement learning to enhance reasoning over the retrieved evidence. The main experimental results, validated on Encyclopedic-VQA and InfoSeek datasets, show that ReAG significantly outperforms previous methods, achieving higher answer accuracy and providing interpretable reasoning grounded in the retrieved context.
本研究的动机在于，多模态大语言模型在处理领域特定或知识密集型的视觉问题时，由于预训练数据不足常表现不佳，而现有的基于检索增强的知识视觉问答方法存在检索不精确和推理能力有限的问题。所提出的方法ReAG是一种推理增强的生成框架，它结合了粗粒度与细粒度检索，并利用一个评判模型来过滤无关段落，同时采用包含强化学习的多阶段训练策略来提升对检索证据的推理能力。在Encyclopedic-VQA和InfoSeek数据集上的主要实验结果表明，ReAG显著优于先前方法，提高了答案准确性，并能基于检索到的证据提供可解释的推理过程。
Multi-AUV Cooperative Target Tracking Based on Supervised Diffusion-Aided Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jiaao Ma, Chuan Lin, Guangjie Han, Shengchao Zhu, Zhenyu Wang, Chen An
First: 2026-03-31T08:32:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T08:32:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In recent years, advances in underwater networking and multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) have significantly expanded multi-autonomous underwater vehicle (AUV) applications in marine exploration and target tracking. However, current MARL-driven cooperative tracking faces three critical challenges: 1) non-stationarity in decentralized coordination, where local policy updates destabilize teammates' observation spaces, preventing convergence; 2) sparse-reward exploration inefficiency from limited underwater visibility and constrained sensor ranges, causing high-variance learning; and 3) water disturbance fragility combined with handcrafted reward dependency that degrades real-world robustness under unmodeled hydrodynamic conditions. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a hierarchical MARL architecture comprising four layers: global training scheduling, multi-agent coordination, local decision-making, and real-time execution. This architecture optimizes task allocation and inter-AUV coordination through hierarchical decomposition. Building on this foundation, we propose the Supervised Diffusion-Aided MARL (SDA-MARL) algorithm featuring three innovations: 1) a dual-decision architecture with segregated experience pools mitigating nonstationarity through structured experience replay; 2) a supervised learning mechanism guiding the diffusion model's reverse denoising process to generate high-fidelity training samples that accelerate convergence; and 3) disturbance-robust policy learning incorporating behavioral cloning loss to guide the Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient network update using high-quality replay actions, eliminating handcrafted reward dependency. The tracking algorithm based on SDA-MARL proposed in this paper achieves superior precision compared to state-of-the-art methods in comprehensive underwater simulations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于监督扩散辅助多智能体强化学习的多AUV协同目标跟踪
近年来，水下网络与多智能体强化学习（MARL）的进展显著拓展了多自主水下航行器（AUV）在海洋勘探与目标跟踪中的应用。然而，当前基于MARL的协同跟踪面临三大关键挑战：1）分散协调中的非平稳性，局部策略更新会破坏队友观测空间的稳定性，阻碍收敛；2）因水下能见度有限与传感器范围受限导致的稀疏奖励探索效率低下，引发高方差学习；3）水流扰动敏感性与手工设计奖励依赖性相结合，在未建模水动力条件下削弱了实际应用的鲁棒性。为应对这些挑战，本文提出一种分层MARL架构，包含全局训练调度、多智能体协调、局部决策与实时执行四层，通过层次化分解优化任务分配与AUV间协调。在此基础上，我们提出监督扩散辅助MARL（SDA-MARL）算法，具备三项创新：1）采用分离经验池的双决策架构，通过结构化经验回放缓解非平稳性；2）监督学习机制引导扩散模型的反向去噪过程，生成高保真训练样本以加速收敛；3）融合行为克隆损失的扰动鲁棒策略学习，利用高质量回放动作指导深度确定性策略梯度网络更新，消除手工奖励依赖性。本文提出的基于SDA-MARL的跟踪算法在综合水下仿真中相比前沿方法实现了更优的精度。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses key challenges in multi-AUV cooperative target tracking, including non-stationarity in decentralized coordination, sparse-reward exploration inefficiency, and fragility to water disturbances. It proposes a hierarchical MARL architecture and a novel Supervised Diffusion-Aided MARL (SDA-MARL) algorithm, which features a dual-decision architecture with segregated experience pools, a supervised learning mechanism to guide a diffusion model for sample generation, and disturbance-robust policy learning with behavioral cloning. Experimental results from underwater simulations demonstrate that the proposed tracking algorithm achieves superior precision compared to state-of-the-art methods.
本文针对多自主水下航行器协同目标跟踪中的关键挑战，包括分散协调的非平稳性、稀疏奖励探索的低效性以及对水流扰动的脆弱性，提出了一种分层多智能体强化学习架构和新型的监督扩散辅助多智能体强化学习算法。该算法采用双决策架构与隔离经验池，通过监督学习引导扩散模型生成高质量样本，并结合行为克隆损失实现抗干扰策略学习。水下综合仿真实验表明，基于该算法的跟踪方法在精度上优于现有先进方法。
AP-DRL: A Synergistic Algorithm-Hardware Framework for Automatic Task Partitioning of Deep Reinforcement Learning on Versal ACAP
Authors: Enlai Li, Zhe Lin, Sharad Sinha, Wei Zhang
First: 2026-03-31T07:41:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T07:41:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep reinforcement learning has demonstrated remarkable success across various domains. However, the tight coupling between training and inference processes makes accelerating DRL training an essential challenge for DRL optimization. Two key issues hinder efficient DRL training: (1) the significant variation in computational intensity across different DRL algorithms and even among operations within the same algorithm complicates hardware platform selection, while (2) DRL's wide dynamic range could lead to substantial reward errors with conventional FP16+FP32 mixed-precision quantization. While existing work has primarily focused on accelerating DRL for specific computing units or optimizing inference-stage quantization, we propose AP-DRL to address the above challenges. AP-DRL is an automatic task partitioning framework that harnesses the heterogeneous architecture of AMD Versal ACAP (integrating CPUs, FPGAs, and AI Engines) to accelerate DRL training through intelligent hardware-aware optimization. Our approach begins with bottleneck analysis of CPU, FPGA, and AIE performance across diverse DRL workloads, informing the design principles for AP-DRL's inter-component task partitioning and quantization optimization. The framework then addresses the challenge of platform selection through design space exploration-based profiling and ILP-based partitioning models that match operations to optimal computing units based on their computational characteristics. For the quantization challenge, AP-DRL employs a hardware-aware algorithm coordinating FP32 (CPU), FP16 (FPGA/DSP), and BF16 (AI Engine) operations by leveraging Versal ACAP's native support for these precision formats. Comprehensive experiments indicate that AP-DRL can achieve speedup of up to 4.17$\times$ over programmable logic and up to 3.82$\times$ over AI Engine baselines while maintaining training convergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AP-DRL：面向Versal ACAP上深度强化学习自动任务划分的算法-硬件协同框架
深度强化学习已在多个领域取得显著成功，但训练与推理过程的紧密耦合使得加速DRL训练成为优化关键难题。两大核心问题制约着DRL训练效率：(1) 不同DRL算法乃至同一算法内部操作的计算强度差异显著，增加了硬件平台选择复杂度；(2) DRL的宽动态范围特性在传统FP16+FP32混合精度量化下可能导致显著奖励误差。现有研究多聚焦于特定计算单元的DRL加速或推理阶段量化优化，本文提出AP-DRL框架应对上述挑战。AP-DRL是基于AMD Versal ACAP异构架构（集成CPU、FPGA与AI引擎）的自动任务划分框架，通过硬件感知的智能优化加速DRL训练。我们首先分析多类DRL工作负载在CPU、FPGA和AI引擎上的性能瓶颈，据此构建AP-DRL跨组件任务划分与量化优化的设计准则。该框架通过基于设计空间探索的性能剖析与基于整数线性规划的划分模型，依据计算特征将操作映射至最优计算单元，解决平台选择难题；针对量化挑战，AP-DRL利用Versal ACAP原生支持的精度格式，协调FP32（CPU）、FP16（FPGA/DSP）与BF16（AI引擎）的硬件感知算法。综合实验表明，AP-DRL在保持训练收敛性的同时，相比可编程逻辑基准实现最高4.17倍加速，相比AI引擎基准实现最高3.82倍加速。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of accelerating deep reinforcement learning (DRL) training, which is hindered by the varying computational intensity across algorithms and the reward errors from conventional mixed-precision quantization. It proposes AP-DRL, an automatic task partitioning framework that leverages the heterogeneous architecture of AMD Versal ACAP, using design space exploration and integer linear programming to assign operations to optimal computing units (CPU, FPGA, AI Engine) and coordinates FP32, FP16, and BF16 precision formats for quantization. Experimental results show that AP-DRL achieves speedups of up to 4.17× over programmable logic and 3.82× over AI Engine baselines while maintaining training convergence.
本文针对深度强化学习训练加速的挑战，即算法间计算强度差异大和传统混合精度量化导致的奖励误差问题，提出了AP-DRL框架。该方法利用AMD Versal ACAP的异构架构，通过设计空间探索和整数线性规划将操作分配到最优计算单元（CPU、FPGA、AI引擎），并协调FP32、FP16和BF16精度格式进行量化优化。实验结果表明，AP-DRL在保持训练收敛的同时，相比可编程逻辑和AI引擎基线分别实现了最高4.17倍和3.82倍的加速。
A Machine Learning Based Explainability Framework for Interpreting Swarm Intelligence
Authors: Nitin Gupta, Bapi Dutta, Anupam Yadav
First: 2025-09-08T01:39:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T07:38:35+00:00
Comments: Upated: 31-03-26
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Swarm based optimization algorithms have demonstrated remarkable success in solving complex optimization problems. However, their widespread adoption remains sceptical due to limited transparency in how different algorithmic components influence the overall performance of the algorithm. This work presents a multi-faceted interpretability related investigations of Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO). Through this work, we provide a framework that makes the PSO interpretable and explainable using novel machine learning approach. We first developed a comprehensive landscape characterization framework using Exploratory Landscape Analysis to quantify problem difficulty and identify critical features in the problem that affects the optimization performance of PSO. Secondly, we develop an explainable benchmarking framework for PSO. The work successfully decodes how swarm topologies affect information flow, diversity, and convergence. Through systematic experimentation across 24 benchmark functions in multiple dimensions, we establish practical guidelines for topology selection and parameter configuration. A systematic design of decision tree is developed to identify the decision making inside PSO. These findings uncover the black-box nature of PSO, providing more transparency and interpretability to swarm intelligence systems. The source code is available at https://github.com/GitNitin02/ioh_pso.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于机器学习的群体智能可解释性框架
群体优化算法在解决复杂优化问题方面已展现出显著成效，但其广泛应用仍因算法各组件如何影响整体性能缺乏透明度而受到质疑。本研究对粒子群优化算法进行了多方面的可解释性探究，提出了一种基于新型机器学习方法的可解释PSO框架。首先，我们利用探索性景观分析构建了全面的景观特征框架，以量化问题难度并识别影响PSO优化性能的关键特征。其次，开发了PSO的可解释基准测试框架，成功揭示了群体拓扑结构如何影响信息流、多样性与收敛性。通过对24个多维基准函数的系统实验，为拓扑选择与参数配置建立了实用指南。此外，设计了系统化的决策树模型以识别PSO内部的决策机制。这些发现揭示了PSO的黑箱本质，为群体智能系统提供了更高的透明度与可解释性。源代码发布于https://github.com/GitNitin02/ioh_pso。

The method employs a machine learning framework that integrates Exploratory Landscape Analysis to characterize problem difficulty and an explainable benchmarking approach to analyze how swarm topologies influence information flow and convergence. Experimental results on 24 benchmark functions across multiple dimensions successfully decode the effects of topologies, provide guidelines for parameter configuration, and use decision trees to reveal internal decision-making, thereby demystifying PSO's black-box nature.

Value Gradient Sampler: Learning Invariant Value Functions for Equivariant Diffusion Sampling
Authors: Himchan Hwang, Hyeokju Jeong, Dong Kyu Shin, Che-Sang Park, Sehee Kweon, Sangwoong Yoon, Frank Chongwoo Park
First: 2025-02-18T21:02:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T07:24:17+00:00
Comments: AISTATS 2026. Code: https://github.com/swyoon/value-gradient-sampler/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We propose the Value Gradient Sampler (VGS), a diffusion sampler parameterized by value functions. VGS generates samples from an unnormalized target density (i.e., energy) by evolving randomly initialized particles along the gradient of the value function. In many sampling problems where the target density exhibits invariant symmetries, value functions provide a novel approach to leveraging invariant networks for sampling by inducing an equivariant gradient flow, without requiring more complex equivariant networks. The value networks are trained via temporal difference learning, which supports off-policy training and other established reinforcement learning (RL) techniques. By combining advanced RL methods with efficient invariant networks, VGS achieves both the highest sample quality and the fastest sampling speed among our baselines on the 55-particle Lennard-Jones system.
中文标题/摘要
标题：价值梯度采样器：学习用于等变扩散采样的不变价值函数
我们提出价值梯度采样器（VGS），一种由价值函数参数化的扩散采样器。VGS通过沿价值函数梯度演化随机初始化的粒子，从未归一化的目标密度（即能量）中生成样本。在许多目标密度具有不变对称性的采样问题中，价值函数通过诱导等变梯度流，为利用不变网络进行采样提供了新方法，无需更复杂的等变网络。价值网络通过时序差分学习训练，支持离策略训练及其他成熟的强化学习技术。通过将先进强化学习方法与高效不变网络结合，VGS在55粒子Lennard-Jones系统基准测试中实现了最优样本质量和最快采样速度。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces the Value Gradient Sampler (VGS), motivated by the need for efficient sampling from complex, invariant target densities, such as those in molecular systems. The method parameterizes a diffusion sampler using value functions, which guide particles along gradient flows; by leveraging invariant networks to model these value functions, VGS induces an equivariant sampling process without requiring more intricate equivariant architectures, and it employs temporal difference learning for off-policy training. Experimental results on a 55-particle Lennard-Jones system demonstrate that VGS outperforms baselines in both sample quality and sampling speed.
本文提出了价值梯度采样器（VGS），其动机在于需要对复杂、具有不变对称性的目标密度（如分子系统）进行高效采样。该方法通过价值函数参数化扩散采样器，引导粒子沿梯度流演化；利用不变网络建模价值函数，VGS在不需更复杂等变网络的情况下实现了等变采样流程，并采用时序差分学习进行离策略训练。在55粒子Lennard-Jones系统上的实验结果表明，VGS在采样质量和速度上均优于基线方法。
ARROW: An Adaptive Rollout and Routing Method for Global Weather Forecasting
Authors: Jindong Tian, Yifei Ding, Ronghui Xu, Hao Miao, Chenjuan Guo, Bin Yang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-10T14:00:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T07:14:26+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 16 figures, ICLR 2026 Camera Ready
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Weather forecasting is a fundamental task in spatiotemporal data analysis, with broad applications across a wide range of domains. Existing data-driven forecasting methods typically model atmospheric dynamics over a fixed short time interval, e.g., 6 hours, and rely on naive autoregression-based rollout for long-term forecasting, e.g., 5 days. However, this paradigm suffers from two key limitations: (1) it often inadequately models the spatial and multi-scale temporal dependencies inherent in global weather systems, and (2) the rollout strategy struggles to balance error accumulation with the capture of fine-grained atmospheric variations. In this study, we propose ARROW, an Adaptive-Rollout Multi-scale temporal Routing method for Global Weather Forecasting. To contend with the first limitation, we construct a multi-interval forecasting model that forecasts weather across different time intervals. Within the model, the Shared-Private Mixture-of-Experts captures both shared patterns and specific characteristics of atmospheric dynamics across different time scales, while Ring Positional Encoding accurately encodes the circular latitude structure of the Earth when representing spatial information. For the second limitation, we develop an adaptive rollout scheduler based on reinforcement learning, which selects the most suitable time interval to forecast according to the current weather state. Experimental results demonstrate that ARROW achieves state-of-the-art performance in global weather forecasting, establishing a promising paradigm in this field.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARROW：面向全球天气预报的自适应推演与路由方法
天气预报是时空数据分析中的基础任务，在各领域具有广泛应用。现有数据驱动预测方法通常基于固定短时间间隔（如6小时）建模大气动力学，并依赖朴素自回归推演进行长期预测（如5天）。然而，该范式存在两个关键局限：（1）难以充分建模全球天气系统固有的空间与多尺度时间依赖性；（2）推演策略难以平衡误差累积与精细大气变化的捕捉。本研究提出ARROW——一种面向全球天气预报的自适应推演多尺度时间路由方法。针对第一项局限，我们构建了多间隔预测模型，可跨不同时间间隔预测天气。模型中，共享-私有专家混合模块能捕捉不同时间尺度下大气动力学的共享模式与特定特征，而环形位置编码在表征空间信息时能精确编码地球的环形纬度结构。针对第二项局限，我们开发了基于强化学习的自适应推演调度器，可根据当前天气状态选择最适宜预测的时间间隔。实验结果表明，ARROW在全球天气预报中实现了最先进的性能，为该领域建立了有前景的范式。
Summary / 总结

The method employs a multi-interval forecasting model with a Shared-Private Mixture-of-Experts to capture scale-specific dynamics and Ring Positional Encoding for Earth's spatial structure, alongside a reinforcement learning-based adaptive scheduler to intelligently select forecast intervals during rollout. Experimental results show that ARROW achieves state-of-the-art performance in global weather forecasting, offering a new paradigm for the field.
本研究针对现有数据驱动天气预报方法使用固定短时距和简单自回归推演、难以建模多尺度依赖且误差累积严重的问题，提出了自适应推演与路由方法ARROW。该方法构建了一个多时距预测模型，采用共享-私有专家混合模块捕捉不同时间尺度的动力学特征，并使用环形位置编码准确表示地球空间结构；同时设计了一个基于强化学习的自适应推演调度器，根据当前天气状态动态选择预测时距。实验结果表明，ARROW在全局天气预报任务上取得了最先进的性能，为该领域建立了一个有前景的新范式。
Scaling Whole-Body Human Musculoskeletal Behavior Emulation for Specificity and Diversity
Authors: Yunyue Wei, Chenhui Zuo, Shanning Zhuang, Haixin Gong, Yaming Liu, Yanan Sui
First: 2026-03-31T06:55:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T06:55:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
The embodied learning of human motor control requires whole-body neuro-actuated musculoskeletal dynamics, while the internal muscle-driven processes underlying movement remain inaccessible to direct measurement. Computational modeling offers an alternative, but inverse dynamics methods struggled to resolve redundant control from observed kinematics in the high-dimensional, over-actuated system. Forward imitation approaches based on deep reinforcement learning exhibited inadequate tracking performance due to the curse of dimensionality in both control and reward design. Here we introduce a large-scale parallel musculoskeletal computation framework for biomechanically grounded whole-body motion reproduction. By integrating large-scale parallel GPU simulation with adversarial reward aggregation and value-guided flow exploration, the MS-Emulator framework overcomes key optimization bottlenecks in high-dimensional reinforcement learning for musculoskeletal control, which accurately reproduces a broad repertoire of motions in a whole-body human musculoskeletal system actuated by approximately 700 muscles. It achieved high joint angle accuracy and body position alignment for highly dynamic tasks such as dance, cartwheel, and backflip. The framework was also used to explore the musculoskeletal control solution space, identifying distinct musculoskeletal control policies that converge to nearly identical external kinematic and mechanical measurements. This work establishes a tractable computational route to analyzing the specificity and diversity underlying human embodied control of movement. Project page: https://lnsgroup.cc/research/MS-Emulator.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向特异性和多样性的大规模全身人体肌肉骨骼行为仿真
人体运动控制的具身学习需要全身神经驱动的肌肉骨骼动力学，而运动背后的内部肌肉驱动过程无法直接测量。计算建模提供了替代方案，但逆向动力学方法难以从高维度、过驱动系统中观测到的运动学数据解析冗余控制。基于深度强化学习的正向模仿方法因控制和奖励设计中的维度灾难而表现出不足的跟踪性能。本文提出了一种基于生物力学的大规模并行肌肉骨骼计算框架，用于全身运动复现。通过将大规模并行GPU模拟与对抗性奖励聚合及价值引导流探索相结合，MS-Emulator框架克服了肌肉骨骼控制高维强化学习中的关键优化瓶颈，在由约700块肌肉驱动的全身人体肌肉骨骼系统中精确复现了广泛的动作库。该框架在舞蹈、侧手翻和后空翻等高动态任务中实现了高关节角度精度和身体位置对齐。该框架还被用于探索肌肉骨骼控制解空间，识别出能收敛至几乎相同外部运动学和力学测量的不同肌肉骨骼控制策略。本研究为分析人体运动具身控制的特异性和多样性建立了可行的计算路径。项目页面：https://lnsgroup.cc/research/MS-Emulator。

The authors introduce the MS-Emulator framework, which integrates large-scale parallel GPU simulation with adversarial reward aggregation and value-guided flow exploration to overcome optimization bottlenecks in reinforcement learning for musculoskeletal control. Experimental results demonstrate that the framework accurately reproduces a broad repertoire of highly dynamic motions, such as dance and backflips, achieving high joint angle and body position accuracy, while also revealing distinct muscle control policies that yield nearly identical external kinematics, thereby enabling analysis of movement specificity and diversity.

When Rubrics Fail: Error Enumeration as Reward in Reference-Free RL Post-Training for Virtual Try-On
Authors: Wisdom Ikezogwo, Mehmet Saygin Seyfioglu, Ranjay Krishna, Karim Bouyarmane
First: 2026-03-05T20:20:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T06:07:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) and Rubrics as Rewards (RaR) have driven strong gains in domains with clear correctness signals and even in subjective domains by synthesizing evaluation criteria from ideal reference answers. But many real-world tasks admit multiple valid outputs and lack the single ideal answer that rubric generation depends on. We identify this reference-free setting as a gap in current post-training methods and propose Implicit Error Counting (IEC) to fill it. Instead of checking what a response gets right against a rubric, IEC enumerates what it gets wrong, applying severity-weighted scores across task-relevant axes and converting them into calibrated per-aspect rewards. We show that naïve explicit enumeration is too noisy for stable optimization, and that two design choices: implicit score emission and group calibration are necessary to make error counting a reliable reward. As a case study, we validate IEC on virtual try-on (VTO), a domain that is simultaneously too constrained for holistic scoring and too permissive for rubric-based evaluation: subtle garment errors are unacceptable, yet many output variations are correct. We introduce Cascaded Error Counting (CEC) as an evaluation metric, which tracks human preferences well (60% top-1 vs. 30% others), and curate Mismatch-DressCode (MDressBench), a benchmark with maximal attribute mismatch to stress-test reward designs. On MDressBench, IEC outperforms RaR across all metrics (CEC: 5.31 vs. 5.60 on flat references; 5.20 vs. 5.53 on non-flat). On VITON-HD and DressCode, IEC matches or surpasses six baselines on 6 of 8 perceptual metrics. These results suggest that when ideal answers are unavailable, counting errors provide a stronger signal than constructing rubrics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当评分标准失效时：虚拟试穿无参考强化学习后训练中的错误枚举奖励机制
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）和评分标准即奖励（RaR）方法在具有明确正确性信号的领域，甚至通过理想参考答案合成评估标准的主观领域取得了显著进展。然而许多现实任务允许多种有效输出，缺乏评分标准生成所依赖的单一理想答案。我们指出这种无参考场景是当前后训练方法的空白，并提出隐式错误计数（IEC）作为解决方案。IEC不再依据评分标准核对回答的正确部分，而是枚举其错误之处，在任务相关维度上应用严重性加权评分，并将其转化为校准后的分项奖励。研究表明，朴素的显式枚举噪声过大无法稳定优化，而隐式分数发射和组校准两项设计是使错误计数成为可靠奖励的必要条件。以虚拟试穿（VTO）为案例验证IEC：该领域既因约束过多难以整体评分，又因自由度太高无法适用基于评分标准的评估——细微的服装错误不可接受，但多种输出变体均属正确。我们提出级联错误计数（CEC）作为评估指标，其与人类偏好高度吻合（60%首选率 vs. 其他方法30%），并构建了具有最大属性错配的基准测试集Mismatch-DressCode（MDressBench）以压力测试奖励设计。在MDressBench上，IEC在所有指标上超越RaR（CEC：平面参考5.31 vs. 5.60；非平面5.20 vs. 5.53）。在VITON-HD和DressCode数据集上，IEC在8项感知指标中的6项达到或超越六个基线模型。这些结果表明，当理想答案不可得时，错误计数比构建评分标准能提供更强的优化信号。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of rubric-based reinforcement learning post-training in tasks lacking a single ideal reference answer, proposing Implicit Error Counting (IEC) as a reward mechanism that enumerates and weights errors across task-specific axes instead of matching a rubric. The method introduces implicit score emission and group calibration to stabilize optimization, validated in the virtual try-on domain where it outperforms Rubrics as Rewards on a curated benchmark with attribute mismatches and matches or exceeds six baselines on perceptual metrics.
本文针对缺乏单一理想参考答案的任务中基于量规的强化学习后训练的局限性，提出了隐式错误计数（IEC）作为奖励机制，通过枚举和加权任务特定轴上的错误而非匹配量规来生成奖励。该方法采用隐式分数发射和组校准以稳定优化，在虚拟试穿领域得到验证，在属性不匹配的基准测试中优于基于量规的奖励，并在感知指标上匹配或超越了六个基线方法。
A General Control-Theoretic Approach for Reinforcement Learning: Theory and Algorithms
Authors: Weiqin Chen, Mark S. Squillante, Chai Wah Wu, Santiago Paternain
First: 2024-06-20T21:50:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T05:48:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We devise a control-theoretic reinforcement learning approach to support direct learning of the optimal policy. We establish various theoretical properties of our approach, such as convergence and optimality of our analog of the Bellman operator and Q-learning, a new control-policy-variable gradient theorem, and a specific gradient ascent algorithm based on this theorem within the context of a specific control-theoretic framework. We empirically evaluate the performance of our control theoretic approach on several classical reinforcement learning tasks, demonstrating significant improvements in solution quality, sample complexity, and running time of our approach over state-of-the-art methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种通用的控制论强化学习方法：理论与算法
我们设计了一种控制论强化学习方法，以支持直接学习最优策略。我们建立了该方法的多种理论性质，例如贝尔曼算子与Q学习的类比收敛性与最优性、新的控制策略变量梯度定理，以及在该控制论框架下基于此定理的具体梯度上升算法。我们在多个经典强化学习任务上实证评估了该控制论方法的性能，结果表明其在解质量、样本复杂度和运行时间上相比现有先进方法均有显著提升。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for more efficient and theoretically grounded reinforcement learning methods, this paper introduces a control-theoretic framework for directly learning optimal policies. The method establishes theoretical foundations, including convergence and optimality properties analogous to Bellman operators and Q-learning, and derives a novel control-policy-variable gradient theorem, which informs a specific gradient ascent algorithm. Experimental results on classical reinforcement learning tasks demonstrate that this approach yields significant improvements in solution quality, sample efficiency, and computational speed compared to state-of-the-art methods.
本文的动机是寻求更高效且理论坚实的强化学习方法，提出了一种基于控制理论框架来直接学习最优策略的途径。该方法建立了包括与贝尔曼算子和Q学习类似的收敛性与最优性在内的理论性质，并推导出一个新的控制策略变量梯度定理，基于此定理在特定控制理论框架内设计了一种梯度上升算法。在多个经典强化学习任务上的实验结果表明，该方法在解的质量、样本复杂度和运行时间方面均优于现有先进方法，取得了显著提升。
Downsides of Smartness Across Edge-Cloud Continuum in Modern Industry
Authors: Akhil Gupta Chigullapally, Sharvan Vittala, Razin Farhan Hussian, Mohsen Amini Salehi
First: 2026-03-31T05:46:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T05:46:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The fast pace of modern AI is rapidly transforming traditional industrial systems into vast, intelligent and potentially unmanned autonomous operational environments driven by AI-based solutions. These solutions leverage various forms of machine learning, reinforcement learning, and generative AI. The introduction of such smart capabilities has pushed the envelope in multiple industrial domains, enabling predictive maintenance, optimized performance, and streamlined workflows. These solutions are often deployed across the Industrial Internet of Things (IIoT) and supported by the Edge-Fog-Cloud computing continuum to enable urgent (i.e., real-time or near real-time) decision-making. Despite the current trend of aggressively adopting these smart industrial solutions to increase profit, quality, and efficiency, large-scale integration and deployment also bring serious hazards that if ignored can undermine the benefits of smart industries. These hazards include unforeseen interoperability side-effects and heightened vulnerability to cyber threats, particularly in environments operating with a plethora of heterogeneous IIoT systems. The goal of this study is to shed light on the potential consequences of industrial smartness, with a particular focus on security implications, including vulnerabilities, side effects, and cyber threats. We distinguish software-level downsides stemming from both traditional AI solutions and generative AI from those originating in the infrastructure layer, namely IIoT and the Edge-Cloud continuum. At each level, we investigate potential vulnerabilities, cyber threats, and unintended side effects. As industries continue to become smarter, understanding and addressing these downsides will be crucial to ensure secure and sustainable development of smart industrial systems.

The main experimental results involve a detailed investigation of vulnerabilities, cyber threats, and interoperability side-effects at each level, highlighting that large-scale deployment heightens systemic vulnerability, particularly in heterogeneous environments.

ECHO-2: A Large-Scale Distributed Rollout Framework for Cost-Efficient Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jie Xiao, Meng Chen, Qingnan Ren, Jingwei Song, Jiaqi Huang, Yangshen Deng, Chris Tong, Wanyi Chen, Suli Wang, Ziqian Bi, Shuo Lu, Yiqun Duan, Xu Wang, Rymon Yu, Ween Yang, Lynn Ai, Eric Yang, Bill Shi
First: 2026-02-02T14:57:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T05:22:03+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) is a critical stage in post-training large language models (LLMs), involving repeated interaction between rollout generation, reward evaluation, and centralized learning. Distributing rollout execution offers opportunities to leverage more cost-efficient inference resources, but introduces challenges in wide-area coordination and policy dissemination. We present ECHO-2, a distributed RL framework for post-training with remote inference workers and non-negligible dissemination latency. ECHO-2 combines centralized learning with distributed rollouts and treats bounded policy staleness as a user-controlled parameter, enabling rollout generation, dissemination, and training to overlap. We introduce an overlap-based capacity model that relates training time, dissemination latency, and rollout throughput, yielding a practical provisioning rule for sustaining learner utilization. To mitigate dissemination bottlenecks and lower cost, ECHO-2 employs peer-assisted pipelined broadcast and cost-aware activation of heterogeneous workers. Experiments on GRPO post-training of 4B and 8B models under real wide-area bandwidth regimes show that ECHO-2 significantly improves cost efficiency while preserving RL reward comparable to strong baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ECHO-2：面向成本高效强化学习的大规模分布式推演框架
强化学习（RL）是大语言模型（LLM）后训练的关键阶段，涉及推演生成、奖励评估与集中式学习的反复交互。分布式推演执行为利用更具成本效益的推理资源提供了可能，但引入了广域协调与策略传播的挑战。本文提出ECHO-2——一个面向后训练的分布式RL框架，支持远程推理工作节点且能处理不可忽略的传播延迟。ECHO-2将集中式学习与分布式推演相结合，将有界策略陈旧度作为用户可控参数，实现推演生成、传播与训练的重叠执行。我们提出基于重叠的容量模型，关联训练时间、传播延迟与推演吞吐量，形成维持学习器利用率的实用资源配置规则。为缓解传播瓶颈并降低成本，ECHO-2采用对等辅助流水线广播及异构工作节点的成本感知激活机制。在真实广域带宽环境下对4B与8B模型进行GRPO后训练的实验中，ECHO-2在保持与强基线相当的RL奖励的同时，显著提升了成本效益。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for ECHO-2 is to reduce the cost of reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models by distributing rollout generation to remote, cost-efficient inference resources, while addressing the coordination and policy dissemination challenges this introduces. The method combines centralized learning with distributed rollouts, explicitly treating policy staleness as a tunable parameter to overlap rollout, dissemination, and training phases; it also employs an overlap-based capacity model for provisioning and techniques like peer-assisted pipelined broadcast to mitigate dissemination bottlenecks. Experimental results from GRPO post-training of 4B and 8B models under real wide-area bandwidth conditions demonstrate that ECHO-2 significantly improves cost efficiency while maintaining RL reward performance comparable to strong baselines.
ECHO-2的动机是通过将强化学习中的策略执行（rollout）分发到远程、成本效益高的推理资源上，以降低大语言模型后训练的成本，同时解决由此带来的广域协调和策略传播延迟的挑战。该方法将集中式学习与分布式策略执行相结合，将策略过时性作为可调参数，使策略生成、传播和训练能够重叠进行；并引入基于重叠的容量模型进行资源调配，以及采用对等辅助的流水线广播等技术来缓解传播瓶颈。在真实广域带宽环境下对4B和8B模型进行GRPO后训练的实验结果表明，ECHO-2在保持与强基线相当的强化学习奖励性能的同时，显著提高了成本效率。
FIPO: Eliciting Deep Reasoning with Future-KL Influenced Policy Optimization
Authors: Chiyu Ma, Shuo Yang, Kexin Huang, Jinda Lu, Haoming Meng, Shangshang Wang, Bolin Ding, Soroush Vosoughi, Guoyin Wang, Jingren Zhou
First: 2026-03-20T10:24:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T04:49:52+00:00
Comments: Move related work to main paper, and add one more background information in Preliminary section
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Future-KL Influenced Policy Optimization (FIPO), a reinforcement learning algorithm designed to overcome reasoning bottlenecks in large language models. While GRPO style training scales effectively, it typically relies on outcome-based rewards (ORM) that distribute a global advantage uniformly across every token in a trajectory. We argue that this coarse-grained credit assignment imposes a performance ceiling by failing to distinguish critical logical pivots from trivial tokens. FIPO addresses this by incorporating discounted future-KL divergence into the policy update, creating a dense advantage formulation that re-weights tokens based on their influence on subsequent trajectory behavior. Empirically, FIPO enables models to break through the length stagnation seen in standard baselines. Evaluated on Qwen2.5-32B, FIPO extends the average chain-of-thought length from roughly 4,000 to over 10,000 tokens and increases AIME 2024 Pass@1 accuracy from 50.0% to a peak of 58.0% (converging at approximately 56.0\%). This outperforms both DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Math-32B (around 47.0%) and o1-mini (approximately 56.0%). Our results suggest that establishing dense advantage formulations is a vital path for evolving ORM-based algorithms to unlock the full reasoning potential of base models. We open-source our training system, built on the verl framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FIPO：基于未来KL散度影响策略优化的深度推理激发方法
本文提出未来KL散度影响策略优化（FIPO），一种旨在克服大语言模型推理瓶颈的强化学习算法。虽然GRPO式训练能有效扩展，但其通常依赖基于结果的奖励模型（ORM），将全局优势均匀分配给轨迹中的每个词元。我们认为这种粗粒度的信用分配因未能区分关键逻辑支点与次要词元而形成了性能瓶颈。FIPO通过将折现的未来KL散度纳入策略更新来解决该问题，构建了一种密集优势表达机制，根据词元对后续轨迹行为的影响重新分配权重。实验表明，FIPO使模型能够突破标准基线中出现的长度停滞现象。在Qwen2.5-32B上的评估显示，FIPO将平均思维链长度从约4000词元扩展至超10000词元，并将AIME 2024 Pass@1准确率从50.0%提升至峰值58.0%（最终收敛于约56.0%），优于DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Math-32B（约47.0%）和o1-mini（约56.0%）。结果表明，建立密集优势表达机制是推动基于ORM的算法演进、释放基础模型完整推理潜力的关键路径。我们开源了基于verl框架构建的训练系统。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Future-KL Influenced Policy Optimization (FIPO), a reinforcement learning algorithm motivated by the need to overcome reasoning bottlenecks in large language models, as standard outcome-based reward methods suffer from coarse-grained credit assignment that fails to distinguish critical logical tokens. The method incorporates discounted future-KL divergence into policy updates to create a dense advantage formulation that re-weights tokens based on their influence on subsequent trajectory behavior. Experimental results on Qwen2.5-32B show that FIPO extends average chain-of-thought length from about 4,000 to over 10,000 tokens and increases AIME 2024 Pass@1 accuracy from 50.0% to a peak of 58.0%, outperforming baselines like DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Math-32B and matching or exceeding o1-mini.
本文提出了未来KL影响策略优化（FIPO），其动机是解决大语言模型中的推理瓶颈问题，因为标准的基于结果的奖励方法存在粗粒度信用分配缺陷，无法区分关键逻辑标记与无关标记。该方法通过将折扣后的未来KL散度纳入策略更新，创建了一种密集优势公式，根据标记对后续轨迹行为的影响重新加权。在Qwen2.5-32B上的实验结果表明，FIPO将平均思维链长度从约4000标记扩展到超过10000标记，并将AIME 2024 Pass@1准确率从50.0%提升至峰值58.0%，优于DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Math-32B等基线模型，并与o1-mini性能相当或更优。
MemRerank: Preference Memory for Personalized Product Reranking
Authors: Zhiyuan Peng, Xuyang Wu, Huaixiao Tou, Yi Fang, Yi Gong
First: 2026-03-31T04:16:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T04:16:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM-based shopping agents increasingly rely on long purchase histories and multi-turn interactions for personalization, yet naively appending raw history to prompts is often ineffective due to noise, length, and relevance mismatch. We propose MemRerank, a preference memory framework that distills user purchase history into concise, query-independent signals for personalized product reranking. To study this problem, we build an end-to-end benchmark and evaluation framework centered on an LLM-based \textbf{1-in-5} selection task, which measures both memory quality and downstream reranking utility. We further train the memory extractor with reinforcement learning (RL), using downstream reranking performance as supervision. Experiments with two LLM-based rerankers show that MemRerank consistently outperforms no-memory, raw-history, and off-the-shelf memory baselines, yielding up to \textbf{+10.61} absolute points in 1-in-5 accuracy. These results suggest that explicit preference memory is a practical and effective building block for personalization in agentic e-commerce systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MemRerank：基于偏好记忆的个性化商品重排序
基于大语言模型的购物智能体日益依赖长购买历史和多轮交互实现个性化，但直接将原始历史数据附加至提示往往因噪声、长度及相关性错配而效果不佳。我们提出MemRerank——一种偏好记忆框架，可将用户购买历史提炼为简洁、独立于查询的信号，用于个性化商品重排序。为研究该问题，我们构建了以基于大语言模型的\textbf{五选一}任务为核心的端到端基准与评估框架，同时衡量记忆质量与下游重排序效用。我们进一步通过强化学习训练记忆提取器，并以下游重排序性能作为监督信号。在两个基于大语言模型的重排序器上的实验表明，MemRerank在无记忆、原始历史及现成记忆基线方法中均取得稳定优势，在五选一准确率上最高提升\textbf{10.61}个绝对百分点。这些结果表明，显式偏好记忆是构建智能化电商系统个性化能力的实用且有效的核心组件。

MindCube: Spatial Mental Modeling from Limited Views
Authors: Qineng Wang, Baiqiao Yin, Pingyue Zhang, Jianshu Zhang, Kangrui Wang, Zihan Wang, Jieyu Zhang, Keshigeyan Chandrasegaran, Han Liu, Ranjay Krishna, Saining Xie, Jiajun Wu, Li Fei-Fei, Manling Li
First: 2025-06-26T16:38:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T03:37:22+00:00
Comments: The latest version includes an expanded discussion of scaffolding, along with updated data statistics and experimental results
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Can Vision-Language Models (VLMs) imagine the full scene from just a few views, like humans do? Humans form spatial mental models naturally, internal representations of unseen space, to reason about layout, perspective, and motion. Our MindCube benchmark with 21,154 questions across 3,268 images exposes this critical gap, where existing VLMs exhibit near-random performance. Using MindCube, we systematically evaluate how well VLMs build robust spatial mental models through representing positions (cognitive mapping), orientations (perspective-taking), and dynamics (mental simulation for "what-if" movements). We then explore three approaches to help approximate spatial mental models in VLMs, focusing on incorporating unseen intermediate views, natural language reasoning chains, and cognitive maps. The significant improvement comes from a synergistic approach, "map-then-reason", that jointly trains the model to first generate a cognitive map and then reason upon it. By training models to reason over these internal maps, we boosted accuracy from 37.8% to 57.8% (+20.0%). Adding reinforcement learning pushed performance even further to 61.3% (+23.5%). Our key insight is that such scaffolding of spatial mental models, actively constructing and utilizing internal structured spatial representations with flexible reasoning processes, significantly improves understanding of unobservable space.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MindCube：基于有限视角的空间心理建模
视觉语言模型能否像人类一样，仅凭少量视角想象完整场景？人类天生能构建空间心理模型——即对不可见空间的内部表征，从而推理布局、视角和运动。我们提出的MindCube基准包含3,268张图像中的21,154个问题，揭示了现有视觉语言模型在此关键能力上的缺失，其表现接近随机水平。通过MindCube，我们系统评估了视觉语言模型在构建稳健空间心理模型方面的能力，涵盖位置表征（认知映射）、方向推理（视角采择）和动态模拟（针对“假设性”运动的心理仿真）。我们随后探索了三种帮助视觉语言模型近似空间心理模型的方法，重点关注融入不可见中间视角、自然语言推理链和认知地图。最显著的改进来自协同方法“先建图后推理”，该方法联合训练模型首先生成认知地图，再基于地图进行推理。通过训练模型在这些内部地图上进行推理，我们将准确率从37.8%提升至57.8%（+20.0%）。结合强化学习后，性能进一步提升至61.3%（+23.5%）。我们的核心发现是：通过主动构建并利用具有灵活推理过程的内部结构化空间表征，这种空间心理模型的支架式构建能显著提升对不可观测空间的理解能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces MindCube, a benchmark designed to evaluate whether Vision-Language Models (VLMs) can form spatial mental models from limited visual inputs, a capability inherent to humans for reasoning about unseen spaces. To address the poor performance of existing VLMs on this task, the authors propose and systematically test three approaches, with the most effective being a "map-then-reason" method that trains models to first generate an internal cognitive map and then perform reasoning on it. Experimental results show this approach, especially when enhanced with reinforcement learning, significantly boosts accuracy from a baseline of 37.8% to 61.3%, demonstrating that structured internal spatial representations are crucial for understanding unobservable environments.
该论文提出了MindCube基准，旨在评估视觉语言模型能否像人类一样从有限视角形成空间心理模型，以推理不可见空间。针对现有模型在此任务上的性能不足，作者系统探索了三种方法，其中最有效的是“先建图后推理”策略，即训练模型首先生成内部认知地图，然后基于其进行推理。实验结果表明，该方法将准确率从37.8%显著提升至57.8%，结合强化学习后进一步提高到61.3%，证明了构建和利用结构化内部空间表征对于理解不可观测空间的关键作用。
A Quantum-Driven Evolutionary Framework for Solving High-Dimensional Sharpe Ratio Portfolio Optimization
Authors: Mingyang Yu, Jiaqi Zhang, Haorui Yang, Adam Slowik, Huiling Chen, Jing Xu
First: 2026-01-16T06:50:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T03:06:30+00:00
Comments: The authors wish to withdraw this paper due to a significant error in the description within Section 3.2 that affects the overall clarity/validity of the results
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
High-dimensional portfolio optimization faces significant computational challenges under complex constraints, with traditional optimization methods struggling to balance convergence speed and global exploration capability. To address this, firstly, we introduce an enhanced Sharpe ratio-based model that incorporates all constraints into the objective function using adaptive penalty terms, transforming the original constrained problem into an unconstrained single-objective formulation. This approach preserves financial interpretability while simplifying algorithmic implementation. To efficiently solve the resulting high-dimensional optimization problem, we propose a Quantum Hybrid Differential Evolution (QHDE) algorithm, which integrates Quantum-inspired probabilistic behavior into the standard DE framework. QHDE employs a Schrodinger-inspired probabilistic mechanism for population evolution, enabling more flexible and diversified solution updates. To further enhance performance, a good point set-chaos reverse learning strategy is adopted to generate a well-dispersed initial population, and a dynamic elite pool combined with Cauchy-Gaussian hybrid perturbations strengthens global exploration and mitigates premature convergence. Experimental validation on CEC benchmarks and real-world portfolios involving 20 to 80 assets demonstrates that QHDE's performance improves by up to 73.4%. It attains faster convergence, higher solution precision, and greater robustness than seven state-of-the-art counterparts, thereby confirming its suitability for complex, high-dimensional portfolio optimization and advancing quantum-inspired evolutionary research in computational finance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向高维夏普比率投资组合优化的量子驱动进化框架
高维投资组合优化在复杂约束下面临显著计算挑战，传统优化方法难以平衡收敛速度与全局探索能力。为此，本文首先提出一种基于增强夏普比率模型，通过自适应惩罚项将所有约束纳入目标函数，将原约束问题转化为无约束单目标形式，在保持金融可解释性的同时简化算法实现。为高效求解所得高维优化问题，提出量子混合差分进化算法，将量子启发的概率行为融入标准差分进化框架。该算法采用薛定谔启发的概率机制进行种群进化，实现更灵活多样的解更新。为进一步提升性能，采用好点集-混沌反向学习策略生成分布均匀的初始种群，并结合动态精英池与柯西-高斯混合扰动增强全局探索、缓解早熟收敛。在CEC基准测试和20至80项实际资产组合上的实验表明，该算法性能最高提升73.4%，相比七种前沿对比算法具有更快收敛速度、更高解精度及更强鲁棒性，证实其适用于复杂高维投资组合优化，并推进计算金融领域的量子启发进化研究。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the computational challenges of high-dimensional portfolio optimization by introducing an enhanced Sharpe ratio model that transforms constrained problems into unconstrained ones using adaptive penalty terms, preserving financial interpretability. To solve this efficiently, a Quantum Hybrid Differential Evolution (QHDE) algorithm is proposed, integrating quantum-inspired probabilistic behavior with a Schrodinger-inspired mechanism for population evolution, alongside strategies like good point set-chaos reverse learning and dynamic elite pools to enhance exploration and prevent premature convergence.
